gurur atropanetā | ata eva āpastambaḥ: "tamaso vā eṣa tamaḥ praviśati yam avidvān upanayate yaś cāvidvān iti hi brāhmaṇam | tasminn abhijanavidyāsamudetaṃ samāhitaṃ saṃskartāram īpset" iti | yaś cāvidvān upanayate so 'pi tamaḥ praviśatīty arthaḥ | etac ca lakṣaṇābhidhānaṃ pitṛvyatiriktānāṃ gurutvam aupacārikam iti darśayitum | ata eva manuḥ śrutopakāriṇaḥ pūjyatvamātrābhiprāyeṇ guruśabdam āha |

	alpaṃ vā bahu vā yasya śrutasyopakaroti yaḥ |

	tam apīha guruṃ vidyāc chrutopakriyayā tayā || iti |

apiśabdaprayogād ity abhiprāyaḥ | yat tu devalenoktam,

	upādhyāyaḥ pitā jyeṣṭho bhrātā caiva mahīpatiḥ |

	mātulaḥ śvaśuras trātā mātāmahapitāmahau ||

	varṇajyeṣṭhaḥ pitṛvyaś ca puṃsy ete guravaḥ smṛtāḥ |

	mātā mātāmahī gurvī pitur mātuś ca sodarāḥ ||

	śvaśrūḥ pitāmahī jyeṣṭhā dhātrī ca guravaḥ striyām |

	ity ukto guruvargo 'yaṃ mātṛtaḥ mitṛto dvidhā || iti |

tad api pitrādivan mānyatvābhiprāyam | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	mātāmaho mātulaś ca pitṛvyaḥ śvaśuro guruḥ |

	pūrvajaḥ snātakaś cartvik mānyās te guravaḥ sadā ||

	mātṛṣvasā tātulānī svaśrūr dhātrī pitṛṣvasā |

	pitāmahī pitṛvyastrī gurustrī mātṛvac caret || iti |

manur api |

	pitur bhaginyāṃ mātuś ca jyāyasyāṃ ca svasary api |

	mātṛvad bhaktim ātiṣṭhen mātā tv ābhyo garīyasī || iti |

ācāryasyāpi lakṣaṇam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	upanīya dadad vedam ācāryaḥ sa udāhṛtaḥ | iti |

yo yasyopanayanamātraṃ kṛtvā vedaṃ prayacchati sa tasyācārya ity arthaḥ | vedagrahaṇaṃ kalpasūtrāder api pradarśanārtham | ata eva manuḥ |

	upanīya tu yaś śiṣyaṃ vedam adhyāpayed dvijaḥ |

	sakalpaṃ sarahasyaṃ ca tam ācāryaṃ pracakṣate || iti |

rahasyam upaniṣat | etac copanayanādikartṛtvam pitur abhāve jyeṣṭhabhrātur eva veditavyam,

	pitṛvat pālayet putrān jyeṣṭho bhrātā yavīyasaḥ |

	pitṛvac cāpi varteran jyeṣṭhabhrātari dharmataḥ ||

iti manunā tayoḥ pitṛputradharmātideśāt | yas tu vedabhāgam aṅgāni vā vṛttyartham adhyāpayati sa upādhyāyaḥ | tad āha manuḥ |

	ekadeśaṃ tu vedasya vedāṅgāny atha vā punaḥ |

	yo 'dhyapayati vṛttyartham upādhyāyaḥ sa ucyate || iti |

vṛtttir jīvikā | ata eva śaṅkhaḥ |

	bhṛtakādhyāpako yas tu upādhyāyaḥ sa ucyate | iti |

mūlyenādhyayanaṃ bhṛtakādhyāpanam | tathā ca viṣṇuḥ: "yas tv enaṃ mūlyenādhyāpayet tam upādhyāyam" iti | vidyād iti śeṣaḥ | ṛtviglakṣaṇam api manunaivoktam |

	agnyādheyaṃ pākayajñān agniṣṭomādikān makhān |

	yaḥ karoti vṛto yasya sa tasyartvig ihocyate || iti |

ete ca pūrvoktācāryopādhyāyartvijo yathāpūrvaṃ mānyā veditavyāḥ | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	ete mānyā yathāpūrvaṃ yebhyo mātā garīyasī |

mānyāḥ pūjyā ity arthaḥ | garīyasī gurutarā pūjyatameti yāvat | devalo 'pi |

	gurūṇām api sarveṣāṃ pūjyāḥ pañca viśeṣataḥ |

	yo bhāvayati yā sūte yean vidyopadiśyate ||

	jyeṣṭhabhrātā ca bhartā ca pañcaite guravaḥ smṛtāḥ |

	teṣām ādās trayaḥ śreṣṭhās teṣāṃ mātā supūjitā || iti |

atropapattim āha vyāsaḥ |

	māsān daśodarasthaṃ yā dhṛtvā śūlaiḥ samākulā |

	vedanāvividhair duḥkhaiḥ prasūyeta vimūrcchitā ||

	prāṇair api priyān putrān manyate sutavatsalā |

	kas tasyā niṣkṛtiṃ kartuṃ śakto varṣaśatair api || iti |

ata iyaṃ pūjyatamety abhiprāyaḥ | tasyā niṣkṛtir ānṛṇyam | atra śaṅkhaḥ: "na putraḥ pitur mucyetānyatra sautrāmaṇīyāgāj jīvann ṛṇān mātuḥ" iti | manur api mātaiva garīyasīty āha |

	upādhyāyān daśācārya ācāryāṇāṃ śataṃ pitā |

	sahasraṃ tu pitṝṇ mātā gauraveṇātiricyate || iti |

etac ca saṃskārādikaraṇarahitotpādakamātraviṣayam | anyathā tu pitaiva śreyān | tathā ca purāṇam |

	dvau gurū puruṣasyeha pitā mātā ca dharmataḥ |

	dharā gurutarā tadvan mātā gurutarā tataḥ ||

	tayor api pitā śreyān bījaprādānyadarśanāt |

	abhāve bījino mātā tadabhāve tu pūrvajaḥ || iti |

ācāryo 'pi janakamātrāpekṣayā garīyān eva | tad āha manuḥ |

	utpādakabrahmadātror garīyān brahmadaḥ pitā |

brahmada ācāryaḥ na tūpādhyāyaḥ | yato 'nantaram āha |

	brahmajanma hi viprasya pretya ceha ca śāśvatam |

yad brahmagrahaṇārthaṃ janmopanayanākhyaṃ tad yataḥ karotīty arthaḥ | yas tu bālo vṛddham adhyāpayati so 'pi garīyān ity āha viṣṇuḥ: "bāle samānavayasi vādhyāpake guruvad varteta" iti | atra purāvṛttam āha manuḥ |

	adhyāpayāmāsa pitṝn śiśur āṅgirasaḥ kaviḥ |

	putrakā iti hovāca jñānena parigṛhya tān ||

	te tam artham apṛcchant devān āgatamanyavaḥ |

	devāś caitān sametyocur nyāyyaṃ vaḥ śiśur uktavān ||

	ajño bhavati vai bālaḥ pitā bhavati mantradaḥ |

	ajñaṃ hi bāla ity āhuḥ pitety eva ca mantradam ||

	na hāyanair na palitair na vittair na bandhubhiḥ |

	ṛṣayaś cakrire dharmaṃ yo 'nūcānaḥ sa no mahān || 

hāyanādibhir mahattvam iti na dharmaṃ vyavasthāpitavantaḥ | kiṃ tu yo 'nūcānaḥ pravaktā sa eva mahān iti | ata eva cāsmai na druhyāt | tad aha manuḥ |

	ya āvṛṇoty avitathaṃ brahmaṇā śravaṇāv ubhau |

	sa mātā sa pitā jñeyas taṃ na druhyet kadācana ||

āvṛṇoty āpūrayati | avitathaṃ visvarādirahitaṃ kṛtvety arthaḥ | vyāso 'pi |

	upādhyāyaṃ pitaraṃ mātaraṃ ca ye druhyanti manasā karmaṇā vā |

	teṣāṃ pāpaṃ bhrūṇahatyāvaśiṣṭaṃ tasmād ebhyaḥ pāpakṛn nāsti loke ||

manur api |

	ācāryaś ca pitā caiva mātā bhrātā ca pūrvajaḥ |

	nārtenāpy avamantavyā brāhmaṇena viśeṣataḥ || iti |

yas tu pitror nityaṃ priyam evācarati sa dharmajātam avāpnotīty āha devalaḥ |

	yāvat pitā ca mātā ca dvāv etau nirvikāriṇau |

	tāvat sarvaṃ parityajya putraḥ syāt tatparāyaṇaḥ ||

	mātā pitā ca suprītau syātāṃ putraguṇair yadi |

	sa putaḥ sakalaṃ dharmaṃ prāpnuyāt tena karmaṇā ||

vikāro maraṇam | manur api |

	yaṃ mātāpitarau kleśaṃ sahete saṃbhave nṛṇām |

	na tasya niṣkṛtiḥ sakyā kartuṃ varṣaśatair api ||

	tayor nityaṃ priyaṃ brūyād ācāryasya ca sarvadā |

	teṣu hi triṣu tuṣṭeṣu tapaḥ sarvaṃ samāpyate ||

	teṣāṃ trayāṇāṃ śuśrūṣā paramaṃ tapa ucyate |

	na tair abhyananujñato dharmam anyaṃ samācaret ||

	ta eva hi trayo lokās ta eva traya āśramāḥ |

	ta eva hi trayo vedās ta evoktās trayo 'gnayaḥ ||

	pitā vai gārhapatyāgniḥ mātāgnir dakṣiṇāḥ smṛtaḥ (?) |

	gurur āhavanīyo 'gniḥ sāgnitretā garīyasī ||

	imaṃ lokaṃ mātṛbhaktyā pitṛbhaktyā tu madhyamam |

	guruśuśrūṣayā caiva brahmalokaṃ samaśnute ||

	sarve tasyādṛtā dharmā yasyaite traya ādṛtāḥ |

	anādṛtās tu yasyaita sarvās tasyāphalāḥ kriyāḥ ||

	yāvat trayas te jīveyus tāvan nānyaṃ samācaret |

	teṣv eva nityaṃ śuśrūṣāṃ kuryāt priyahite rataḥ ||

	teṣām anuparodhena pāratryaṃ yad yad ācaret |

	tat tan nivedayet tebhyo manovacanakarmabhiḥ |

	eṣa dharmaḥ paraḥ sākṣād upadharmo 'nya ucyate || 

pāratryaṃ pāralaukikam | devalo 'pi | |

	nāsti mātṛsamaṃ daivaṃ nasti pitrā samo guruḥ |

	tayoḥ pratyupakāro hi na kathaṃcana vidyate || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ gurvādinirūpaṇam**

**athābhivādanam**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	tato 'bhivādayed vidvān asāv aham iti bruvan |

tato 'gnikāryād anantaram ity arthaḥ | asāv ity asya sthāne svaṃ nāma kīrtayet | tathā ca manuḥ |

	abhivādanāt paraṃ vipro jyāyāṃsam abhivādayan |

	asau nāmāham asmīti svaṃ nāma parikīrtayet ||

abhivādāt "abhivādaye" ity asya śabdasyopari devadattanāmāham asmīti svanāma brūyāt | asyopari bhoḥśabdo 'pi kīrtanīyaḥ | tad āha sa eva |

	bhoḥśabdaṃ kīrtayed ante svasya nāmno 'bhivādane | iti |

evaṃ saty evāṃ prayogo bhavati "abhivādaye devadattanāmāham asmi bho" iti | tatra āpastambaḥ: "dakṣiṇaṃ bāhuṃ śrotrasamaṃ prasārya brāhmaṇo 'bhivādayītoraḥsamaṃ rājanyo madhasamaṃ vaiśyo nīcaiḥ śūdraḥ prāñjaliḥ" iti | etac ca hastadvayena kāryam anyathā doṣaśravaṇāt | tathā ca viṣṇuḥ |

	janmaprabhṛti yat kiṃcic cetasā dharmam ācaret |

	sarvaṃ tan niṣphalaṃ yāti ekahastābhivādanāt ||

etad api vidvadviṣayam | yad āha sa eva |

	śiṣyāṇām āśiṣaṃ dadyāt padmākārau guror atha |

	ajākarṇena viduṣāṃ mūrkhāṇām ekapāṇinā ||

padmākārau vyatyastāv ity arthaḥ | atrir api |

	dakṣiṇaṃ pāṇim uddhṛtya prākāram abhivādayet |

	śrotriye tv añjaliḥ kāryaḥ pādopagrahaṇaṃ guroḥ || iti |

brāhmaṇasamavāye tv abhivādanakramam āha manuḥ |

	laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ vāpi tathādhyātmikam eva vā |

	ādadīta yato jñānaṃ taṃ pūrvam abhivādayet || iti |

etac ca pratyutthāya kāryam, "sarvatra pratyutthāyābhivadanam" ity āpastambasmaraṇāt | manur āpi |

	ūrdhvaṃ prāṇā hy utkramanti (?) yūnaḥ sthavira āgate |

	pratyutthānābhivādābhyāṃ punas tān pratipadyate ||

etacchīlasyāyurādayo 'pi vivardhanta it sa evāha |

	abhivādanaśīlasya nityavṛddhopasevinaḥ (?) |

	catvāri tasya vardhante āyur vidyā yaśo balam || iti |

abhivāditena yad vaditavyaṃ tad api manur evāha |

	āyuṣmān bhava saumyeti vācyo vipro 'bhivādane |

	akāraś cāsya nāmno 'nte vācyaḥ pūrvākṣaraḥ plutaḥ ||

akāra ity etan nāmno 'ntasvaropalakṣaṇārtham, nāmnaḥ sarvatrākārāntatvaniyamābhāvāt | ataś cābhivādakanāmno 'nte yo 'yam akārādyaḥ svaraḥ pūrvākṣaraḥ sa eva plutaḥ kāryaḥ | na punar apūrvo 'kāro nāmno 'nte vidhīyate | pūrvākṣaratvaṃ ca pūram akṣaraṃ yasya sa pūrvākṣara iti | vasiṣṭho 'pi: "āmantrite svaro 'ntyo 'sya plutaḥ" iti | āmantrite kartavye 'bhivādakanāmno 'nte yaḥ svaraḥ sa pluto bhavati trimātro bhavatīty arthaḥ | evaṃ caivaṃ prayogo bhavati "āyuṣmān bhava saumya devadatā" iti | ye tu nāmasaṃbandhaṃ pratyabhivādanaṃ na jānate tān abhivādayan "ahaṃ bho" iti brūyāt | sarvāḥ striyaś ca | tathā ca manuḥ |

	nāmadheyasya ye kecid abhivādaṃ na jānate |

	tān prājño 'ham iti brūyāt striyaḥ sarvās tathaiva ca || iti |

yas tu pratyabhivādanasvarūpam eva na jānāti nāsāv abhivādya ity āha sa eva |

	yo na vetty abhivādasya vipraḥ pratyabhivādanam |

	nābhivādyaḥ sa viduṣā yathā śūdras tathaiva saḥ || iti |

yaḥ punar jānann api pratyabhivādanādi na karoti tasya doṣo bhaviṣyatpurāṇe darśitaḥ |

	abhivāde kṛte yas tu na karoty abhivādanam |

	āśiṣaṃ vā na kurute sa yāti narakaṃ dhruvam ||

	abhivāde kṛte yas tu taṃ vipraṃ nābhivadayet |

	śmaśāne jāyate vṛkṣo gṛdhrakākopasevitaḥ || iti |

yamo 'pi |

	abhivāde tu yaḥ pūrvam āśiṣaṃ na prayacchati |

	yad duṣkṛtaṃ bhavet tasya tasmād bhāgaṃ prapadyate ||

	tasmāt pūrvābhibhāṣī syāc caṇḍālasyāpi dharmavit |

	surāṃ pibeti vaktavyam evaṃ dharmo na hīyate || iti |

āśiṣam api sa evāha |

	svastīti brāhmaṇo brūyād āyuṣmān iti bhūmipaḥ |

	vardatām iti vaiśyas tu śūdras tu svāgataṃ vadet ||

etac ca sarvavarṇasādhāraṇam | tathā ca bhaviṣyatpurāṇe |

	brāḥmaṇaḥ sarvavarṇānāṃ svasti kuryād iti sthitiḥ |

svastiśabdārtham api yama evāha |

	yat sukhaṃ triṣu lokeṣu vyādhivyasanavarjitam |

	yasmin sarve sthitāḥ kāmāḥ sā svastīty abhisaṃjñitā ||

etac cābhivādanam adhikavayasām eva kāryam, "jyāyāṃsam abhivādayet" iti manusmaraṇāt | ata eva cartvigādīnāṃ mānyatve 'pi kanīyasām anabhivādyatvam āha gautamaḥ: "ṛtvikśvaśurapitṛvyamātulānāṃ tu yavīsasāṃ pratyuttānam anabhivādhyāḥ" iti | yat tu vasiṣṭhenoktam, "ṛtvikśvaśurapitṛvyamātulān avaravayasaḥ prtyuttāyābhivadet" iti, tad apy abhivaded ābhimukhyena vaded ity abhibhāṣaṇamātrābhiprāyam | ata eva bodhāyanaḥ: "ṛtvikśvaśurapitṛvyamātulānāṃ tu yavīyasāṃ pratyutthāyābhibhāṣaṇam" iti | abhibhāṣaṇe 'pi niyamam āha manuḥ |

	brāhmaṇaṃ kuśalaṃ pṛcchet kṣatrabandhum anāmayam |

	vaiśyaṃ kṣemaṃ samāgamya śūdram ārogyam eva ca || iti |

āpastambo 'pi: "kuśalam avaravayasaṃ vayasyaṃ vā pṛcchet" iti | vayasyaś samānavayāḥ | etad api śrotriyaviṣayam, yad āha sa eva, "nāsaṃbhāṣya śrotriyaṃ vyatikramed araṇye ca striyam" iti | strīsaṃbhāṣaṇe 'pi niyamam āha manuḥ |

	parapatnī tu yā strī syād asaṃbandhā ca yonitaḥ |

	tāṃ brūyād bhavatīty eva subhage bhaginīti vā ||

evaṃ ca kanīyasi vayasye vābhibhāṣaṇamātram, jyāyasyabhivādanam iti mantavyam | tatra jyāyastvaṃ kiyatā kālena bhavatīty apekṣite manur āha |

	daśābdākhyaṃ paurasakhyaṃ pañcābdākhyaṃ kalābhṛtām |

	tryabdapūrvaṃ śrotriyāṇāṃ svalpenāpi svayoniṣu ||

samānapuranivāsināṃ daśabhir varṣaiḥ pūrvaḥ sakhā bhavati | tato 'dhiko jyāyān | kalābhṛtāṃ gītanṛtyādividyāvatāṃ pañcābdapūrvaḥ sakhā | śrotiryāṇāṃ vedādhyāyināṃ tryabdapūrvaḥ sakhā bhavati | tato 'dhiko jyāyān | svayoniṣu bhrātrādiṣu svalpenāpi vayasā pūrvaḥ sakhā bhavati | tato 'dhiko 'py abhivādya ity arthaḥ | etac ca brāhmaṇaviṣayam | yad āha manuḥ |

	brāhmaṇaṃ daśavarṣaṃ tu satavarṣaṃ tu bhūmipaṃ |

	pitāputrau vijānīyād brāhmaṇas tu tayoḥ pitā ||

ato brāhmaṇa evābhivādya ity abhiprāyaḥ | ata eva śātātapaḥ |

	abhivādyo namaskāryaḥ sirasā vandya eva ca |

	brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyādyais tu śrīkāmaiḥ sādaraṃ sadā ||

	nābhivādyās tu vipreṇa kṣatriyādyāḥ kadācana |

	jñānakarmaguṇopetā yady apy ete bahuśrutāḥ || iti |

ata eva kṣatriyādyabhivādane prāyaścittam apy āha sa eva |

	kṣatraṃ vaiśyaṃ vābhivādya prāyaścittaṃ kathaṃ bhavet |

	brāhmaṇānāṃ daśāṣṭau ca abhivādya viśudhyati ||

	abhivādya dvijaḥ śūdraṃ sacelaṃ snānam ācaret |

	brāhmaṇānāṃ śataṃ samyag abhivādya viśudhyati ||

	arcayet puṇdarīkākṣaṃ devaṃ vāpi trilocanam |

	brāhmaṇaṃ vā mahābhāgam abhivādya viśudhyati ||

brāhmaṇeṣv api kvacit kvacid abhivādasyāpavādam āha viṣṇuḥ |

	sabhāsu caiva sarvāsu yajñe rājagṛheṣu ca |

	namaskāraṃ prakurvīta brāhmaṇān nābhivādayet ||

gurvādiviṣaye tv abhivādana eva viśeṣam āha gautamaḥ: "guroḥ pādopasaṃgrahaṇaṃ prātaḥ" iti | gurur atrācāryaḥ | yataḥ sa evāha: "mātṛpitṛtadvadhūnāṃ pūrvjānāṃ vidyāgurūṇāṃ tadgurūṇāṃ ca" iti | pūrvajā jyeṣṭhabhrātaraḥ | vidyāgurava upādhyāyāḥ | tadguravo mātrādiguravaḥ | eteṣām api pādopasaṃgrahaṇaṃ kāryam ity arthaḥ | pādopasaṃgrahaṇaṃ pādasparśanam | tatprakāram āha manuḥ |

	vyastyastapāṇinā kāryam upasaṃgrahaṇaṃ guroḥ |

	savyena savyaḥ spraṣṭavyo dakṣiṇena tu dakṣiṇaḥ ||

savyadakṣiṇābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ guroḥ savyadakṣiṇapādau spṛśed ity arthaḥ | atra viśeṣam āha paiṭhīnasiḥ: "uttānābhyāṃ hastābhyāṃ dakṣiṇena dakṣiṇaṃ savyena savyaṃ pādāv abhivādayet" iti | bodhāyano 'pi: "śrotre saṃspṛśya" iti | upasaṃgrahaṇam iti śeṣaḥ | etac ca gurupatnīnām api kāryam | tad āha manuḥ |

	guruvat pratipūjyāḥ syuḥ savarṇaguruyoṣitaḥ |

	asavarṇās tu saṃpūjyāḥ pratyutthānābhivādanaiḥ ||

evaṃ bhrātṛbhāryā apy upasaṃgrāhyāḥ | tad āha sa eva |

	bhrātṛbhāryopasaṃgrāhyā savarṇāhany ahany api |

	viproṣya tūpasaṃgrāhyā jñātisaṃbandhayoṣitaḥ || iti |

evam aviśeṣeṇopasaṃgrahaṇe prāpte kvacid apavādam āha sa eva |

	gurupatnī tu yuvatir nābhivādyeha pādayoḥ |

	pūrṇaviṃśativarṣeṇa guṇadoṣau vijānatā ||

atra hetum āha sa eva |

	avidvāṃsam alaṃ loke vidvāṃsam api vā punaḥ |

	pramadā hy utpathaṃ netuṃ kāmakrodhavaśānugam ||

vidvāṃsam avidvāṃsaṃ vā striyaḥ kāmādivaśagam utpathaṃ netuṃ yato 'laṃ samarthā ity arthaḥ | ataḥ |

	kāmaṃ tu gurupatnīnāṃ yuvatīnāṃ yuva bhuvi |

	vidhivad vandanaṃ kuryād asāv aham iti bruvan ||

	vipras tu pādagrahaṇam anvahaṃ cābhivādanam |

	gurudāreṣu kurvīta satāṃ dharmam anusmaran ||

atrābhivādanavidhānam āha āpastambaḥ: "na sopānadveṣṭitaśirā avahitapāṇir vābhivādayīta" iti | avahitapāṇir aprasāritapāṇiḥ | pracetasāpy uktam: "sopānatkas tv ācamanaśayanayānārohaṇābhivādananamaskārādīn varjayet" iti | śaṅkho 'pi: "nodakumbhahasto 'bhivādayen na baikṣaṃ carann apuṣpānnahasto nāśucir na devapitṛkāryaṃ kurvan na śayānaḥ" iti | āpastambo 'pi: "aprayatena nābhivādyam | tathāprayatāya | aprayataś ca na pratyabhivadet | prativayasaḥ striyaḥ" iti | baudhāyano 'pi: "samiddhāry udakumbhapuṣpānnahasto nābivādayet" iti | evam abhivādye 'pi draṣṭavyam | tathā cāpastambaḥ |

	samitpuṣpakuśājyāmbumṛdannākṣatapāṇikam |

	japaṃ homaṃ ca kurvāṇaṃ nābhivādyeta vai dvijam ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	srukpāṇikam anājñātam aśaktaṃ ripum āturam |

	yoginaṃ ca tapaḥsaktaṃ kaniṣṭhaṃ nābhivādayet ||

śātātapo 'pi |

	udakyāṃ sūtikāṃ nārīṃ bhartṛghnīṃ garbhaghātinīm |

	abhivādya dvijo mohād ahorātreṇa śudhyati ||

	pāṣaṇḍaṃ patitaṃ vrātyaṃ mahāpatikinaṃ śaṭham |

	nāstikaṃ ca kṛtaghnaṃ ca nābhivandet kathaṃcana ||

	dhāvantaṃ ca pramattaṃ ca mūtrotsarjanatatparam |

	bhuñjānam ācamānārhaṃ (?) nābhivādet dvijottamaḥ ||

	vasantaṃ jṛmbhamāṇaṃ ca kurvantaṃ dantadhāvanam |

	abhyaktaśirasaṃ caiva snāsyantaṃ nābhivādayet ||

tathā ca jamadagniḥ |

	devatāpratimāṃ dṛṣṭvā yatiṃ dṛṣṭvā tridaṇḍinam |

	namaskāraṃ na kuryāc ced ahorātreṇa śudhyati ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyām abhivādanam**

**atha mānyatvanimittāni**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	vidyākarmavayobandhuvittair mānyā yathākramam |

vidyā śrutismṛtī | karma vihitakriyā | vaya ātmano 'tiriktam | bandhuḥ svajanasaṃpattiḥ | vittaṃ dhanam | etair yuktāḥ krameṇa mānyā veditavyāḥ | pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ garīya ity arthaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	vittaṃ bandhur vayaḥ karma vidyā bhavati pañcamī |

	etāni mānyasthānāni garīyo yad yad uttaram ||

mānyasthānāni mānyatvanimittānīty arthaḥ | etebhyo vittadibhyaḥ śrutaṃ garīyaḥ tasya dṛṣṭādṛṣṭamūlatvāt | tad āha gautamaḥ: "śrutaṃ tu sarvebhyo garīyas tanmūlatvād dharmasya" iti | etair vittādibhir yukto hīnajātir apy utkṛṣṭajativan mānya ity āha manuḥ |

	pañcānāṃ triṣu varṇeṣu bhūyāṃsi guṇavanti ca |

	yatra syurḥ so 'tra mānārhaḥ śūdro 'pi daśamīṃ gataḥ ||

varṣaśatasyāntimo bhāgo daśamī | navatihāyanātīta ity arthaḥ | etac ca vārdhakaṃ vittādiyogopalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	etaiḥ prabhūtaiḥ śūdro 'pi vārdhake mānam arhati | iti |

vittādirāhitye 'pi keṣāṃcit patho dānena mānam āha manuḥ |

	cakriṇo daśamīsthasya rogiṇo bhāriṇaḥ striyāḥ |

	snātakasya ca rājñaś ca panthā deyo varasya ca ||

cakrī śākatikaḥ | snātakaḥ kṛtasamāvartanaḥ | varo vivāhodyataḥ | eteṣāṃ pathi militānāṃ panthā deyaḥ mārgād apasartavyam ity arthaḥ | yadā tu teṣām eva melanaṃ mārge patho dānena snātakarājānau mānyau | tad āha sa eva |

	teṣāṃ tu samavetānāṃ mānyau snātakapārthivau |

tayoś ca melane snātaka eva rājñā mānanīya ity āha sa eva |

	rājasnātakayor evaṃ snātako nṛpamānabhāk |

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	vṛddhabhārinṛtpasnātastrīrogivaracakriṇām |

	panthā deyo nṛpas teṣāṃ mānyaḥ snātas tu bhūpateḥ ||

vṛddhagrahaṇaṃ bālāder api pradarśanārtham | ata eva pathā deya ity anuvṛttau śaṅkhaḥ: "bālavṛddhamṛtopahatadehabhārākrāntastrīsnātakapravrajitebhyaḥ" iti | strī cātra garbhiṇī veditavyā | tathā ca bodhāyanaḥ |

	vṛddhāya bhārataptāya garbhiṇyai durbalāya ca |

	panthā deyo brāhmaṇāya gave rājñe hy acakṣuṣe || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ mānyatvanimittāni**

**atha bhikṣāṭanam**

tatra manuḥ |

	pratigṛhyepsitaṃ daṇḍam upasthāya ca bhāskaram |

	pradakṣiṇaṃ parītyāgniṃ cared bhaikṣaṃ yathāvidhi ||

yathāśāstram ity arthaḥ | tat katham ity apekṣite gautamaḥ: "ādimadhyānteṣu bavacchabdaḥ prayojyo varṇānupūrvyeṇa" iti | bhikṣāprārthanāvākye varṇakrameṇādimadhyavasāneṣu bhavacchabdaḥ prayoktavya ity arthaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	bhavatpūrvaṃ cared bhaikṣam upanīto dvijottamaḥ |

	bhavanmadhyaṃ tu rājanyaḥ vaiśyas tu bhavaduttaram ||

atraivaṃ prayogaḥ: bhavati bhikāṃ dehīti brāhmaṇaḥ, bhikṣāṃ bhavati dehīti kṣatriyaḥ, bhikṣāṃ dehi bhavatīti vaiśyaḥ | atra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	brāhmaṇexu cared bhaikṣam anindyeṣv ātmavṛttaye |

bhikṣāṇāṃ samūho bhaikṣam | tatprāptaṃ cared ity arthaḥ | tac ca brāhmaṇaviṣayam | tad āha vyāsaḥ |

	brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśaś careyur bhaikṣam anvaham |

	sajātīyagṛheṣv eva sārvavarṇikam eva vā ||

atra viśeṣam āha manuḥ |

	vedayajñair ahīnānāṃ praśastānāṃ svakarmasu |

	brahmacāry āhared bhaikṣaṃ gṛhebhyaḥ prayato 'nvaham ||

ukteṣv api keṣucid apavādam āha sa eva |

	guroḥ kule na bhikṣeta na jñātikulabandhuṣu |

guroḥ kule gurugṛha ity arthaḥ | yat tu tenaivoktam,

	mātaraṃ vā svasāraṃ vā mātur vā bhaginīṃ nijām |

	bhikṣeta bhikṣāṃ prathamāṃ yā cainaṃ nāvamānayet || 

iti, tad upanayanāṅgabhikṣāviṣayam iti, "guroḥ kule na bhikṣeta" ity anenāviruddham | anyatra bhikṣālābhe guroḥ kule bhikṣāṭanam aviruddham ity āha gautamaḥ: "ācāryajñātigurusveṣv alābhe 'nyatra" | sveṣu svakīyeṣu bandhuṣv ity arthaḥ | atrāpi pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ parityajed yady uttarottaragṛheṣu bhikṣā labhyeta | tad api tenaivoktam: "teṣāṃ pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ pariharet" iti | vyāsas tu traivarṇikaṃ bhikṣācaraṇam āha |

	brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviṣaś careyur bhaikṣam anvaham |

	sajātīyagṛheṣv eva sārvavarṇikam eva vā ||

sarvaśabdasya prakṛtavarṇatrayaparatvād ity abhiprāyaḥ | etat pūrvoktasajātīyālābhaviṣayam | tathā ca bhaviṣyatpurāṇam |

	sarvaṃ vā civared grāmaṃ pūrvoktānām asaṃbhave |

	antyavarjyaṃ mahābāho ity āha bhagavān vibhuḥ ||

antyaḥ śūdraḥ | yat tu manunoktam,

	sarvaṃ vā vicared grāmaṃ pūrvoktānām asaṃbhave |

	niyamya prayato vācam abhiśastāṃś ca varjayet || 

iti, tad api purāṇena samānārthaṃ na punaḥ śūdrād api prāptyartham, "vedayajñair ahīnānām" iti tenaivoktatvāt | yad api bhaviṣyatpurāṇe,

	cāturvarṇyaṃ cared bhaikṣam alābhe kurunandana |

iti, tad apy āpadi pūrvapūrvālābhe veditavyam | ata eva viṣṇuḥ |

	kṣatravaiśyagṛheṣv eva kriyāvartiṣu sādhuṣu |

	cāturvarṇyaṃ cared bhaikṣam āpatkāla upasthite || iti |

etac ca sāyaṃ prātaḥ kāryam, "sāyaṃ prātar amatreṇa bhikṣācaryaṃ caret" ity āpastambasmaraṇāt | amatraṃ śarāvādi | ata evaikānnāśitvaniṣedham āha manuḥ |

	bhaikṣeṇa vartayen nityaṃ naikannādī bhaved vratī |

etad anāpadviṣayam | tad āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	brahmacarye sthito naikam annam adyād anāpadi | iti |

bhaikṣāsinaḥ phalam āha manuḥ |

	bhaikṣeṇa vratino vṛttir upavāsasamā smṛtā |

atrir api |

	śākabhakṣāḥ payobhakṣāḥ ye cānye yāvakāśinaḥ |

	sarve te bhakṣabhakṣasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ||

	taptakāñcanavarṇena gavāṃ mūtreṇa yāvakam |

	pibed dvādaś varṣāṇi na tad bhaikṣasamaṃ bhavet ||

yāvako yavakṛto yavāgūḥ | na cātra phalaśravaṇād aniyataṃ bhikṣācaraṇam iti vācyam, akaraṇe manunā prāyaścittavidhānāt:

	akṛtvā bhakṣavaraṇam asamidhya ca pāvakam |

	anāturaḥ saptarātram avakīrṇivrataṃ caret || iti |

āpastambas tu bhikṣamāṇaṃ brahmacāriṇaṃ na pratyācakṣetety āha: "strīṇāṃ ptryācakṣāṇānāṃ samāhito brahmacārīṣṭaṃ dattaṃ hutaṃ prajāṃ paśūn brahmavarcasam annādyaṃ vṛṅkte | tasmād u ha vai brahmacārisaṅghaṃ carantaṃ na pratyācakṣīta" iti | etac ca vratādhyaynādiyogibrahmacāriviṣayam | ata eva manuḥ |

	bhikṣāṃ ca bhikṣave dadyād vidhivad brahmacāriṇe | iti |

vidhivad ity anena tadvihīnasya niṣedham āha | ata eva vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	avratā hy anadhīyānā yatra bhaikṣacarā dvijāḥ |

	taṃ grāmaṃ daṇḍayed rājā corabhaktaprado hi saḥ || iti |

bhikṣādānaṃ prakṛtyāha manuḥ |

	haste dattā tu yā bhikṣā lavaṇaṃ vyañjanāni ca |

	bhuktvā hy aśucitāṃ yāti dātā svargaṃ na gacchati || iti |

etac ca bhaikṣaṃ yāvadartham evāhartavyam anyathā doṣaśravaṇāt | tad āha sa eva |

	āhāramātrād adhikaṃ na kvacid bhaikṣam āharet |

	yujyate steyadoṣeṇa kāmato 'dhikam āharan ||

	mādhūkarīṃ ya ādāya brāhmaṇebhyaḥ prayacchati |

	sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ bhoktā bhuṅkte ca kilbiṣam ||

	tasmān nopahared bhaikṣam atiriktaṃ kadacana |

mādhūkarī bhikṣā | kāmata iti vadan akāmato 'dhikāharaṇe na doṣa ity āha | ata evādhikasya pratipattiniyamam āha āpastambaḥ: "na cocchiṣṭaṃ kuryād aśaktau bhūmau nikhaned apsu vā praviśed ācāryāya vā paryavadadhyād antardhine vā śūdrāya" iti | antardhine ācāryadāsāyety arthaḥ | na cātrocchiṣṭaśabdenāśucidravyābhidhānam āśaṅkanīyam, "nocchiṣṭaṃ kasyacid dadyāt" iti manunā tasya dānaniṣedhāt | evam āhṛtya tad bhaikṣaṃ gurave nivedyāśnīyāt | tathā ca manuḥ |

	samāhṛtya tu tad bhaikṣaṃ yāvad artham amāyayā |

	nivedya gurave 'śnīyād ācamya prāṅmukhaḥ śuciḥ || iti |

gurvasaṃnidhāne tu tadbhāryādibhyo nivedayet | tad āha gautamaḥ: "asaṃnidhau tu tadbhāryāputrasabrahmacārisadbhyaḥ" iti | sabrahmacārī sahādhyāyī santaḥ śrotriyāḥ | tathā cāpastambaḥ: "vipravāse guror ācāryagulāya tair vipravāse 'nyebhyo 'pi śrotriyebhyaḥ" iti | tato gurvādyanujñayā bhuñjīta | tathā ca hārītaḥ: "bhaikṣam avokṣitaṃ paryagnikṛtam ādityadarśitam anujñātam amṛtasaṃmitaṃ prāhus tad aśnan brahmacārī brahmasiddhim avāpnoti" iti | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	kṛtāgnikāryo bhuñjīta vāgyato gurvanujñayā |

	āpośanakriyāpūrvaṃ satkṛtyānnam akutsayan ||

āpośanakriyā amṛtopastaraṇam asīty evamādikā | tāṃ pūrvaṃ kṛtvā bhuñjīta | satkṛtya pūjayitvety arthaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	pūjayed aśanaṃ nityam adyāc caitad akutsayan |

	pūjitaṃ hy aśanaṃ nityaṃ balam ūrjaṃ ca yacchati ||

	apūjitaṃ tu yad bhuktam ubhayaṃ tu hinasti tat |

kutsayann anindayann ity arthaḥ | gautamo 'pi: "sāyaṃ prātas tv annam abhipūjitam anindan bhuñjīta" iti | sāyaṃ prātar iti vadan madhye bhojananiṣedham āha manuḥ |

	sāyaṃ prātar dvijātīnām aśanaṃ śruticoditam |

	nāntarā bhojanaṃ kuryād agnihotrasamo vidhiḥ ||

agnihotrasama ity anena kaladvaye 'pi bhojanam āvaśyakam ity āha | tathā ca śrutiḥ: "tasmāt sāyaṃ prātar āśyeva syāt" iti | atra vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	aṣṭau grāsā muner bhakṣyā vānaprasthasya ṣoḍaśa |

	dvātriṃśataṃ gṛhasthasya hy amitaṃ brahmacāriṇaḥ || iti |

āpastambo 'pi |

	āhitāgnir anaḍvāṃś ca brahmacārī ca te trayaḥ |

	aśnanta eva sidhyanti naiṣāṃ siddhir anaśnatām || iti |

na cātrāmitam ity anenātyaśanam āśaṅkanīyam | ata āha paiṭhīnasiḥ: "kāle 'nnādyaṃ laghukṣipram alpam adyād rasottaram" | manur api |

	na caivātyaśanaṃ kuryān na cocchiṣṭaḥ kvacid vrajet |

	anārogyam anāyuṣyam asvargyaṃ cātibhojanam ||

	apuṇyaṃ lokavidviṣṭaṃ tasmāt tat parivarjayet ||

tathā bhoktur diṅniyamam āha sa eva |

	āyuṣyaṃ prāṅmukho bhuṅkte yaśasyaṃ dakṣināmukhaḥ |

	śriyaṃ pratyaṅmukho bhuṅkte ṛtaṃ bhuṅkta udaṅmukhaḥ ||

āyuṣe hitam āyuṣyam | tat prāṅmukho bhuṅkte bhuñjītety arthaḥ | evaṃ cāyuṣkāmaḥ prāṅmukho bhuñjītety uktaṃ bhavati | evaṃ yaśase hitaṃ yaśasyam | tad dakṣiṇāmukho bhuñjīta | śriyam icchan pratyaṅmukhaḥ | ṛtaṃ satyam | tad icchann udaṅmukha iti | hārīto 'pi: "prāṅmukha āyuṣkāmo 'śnīyād yaśo 'rthī dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ śrīkāmaḥ pratyaṅmukhaḥ" iti | yat tu manunoktam,

	yad veṣṭitaśirā bhuṅkte yad bhuṅkte dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ |

	sopānatkaś ca yad bhuṅkte tad vai rakṣāṃsi gacchati || 

iti, tac chrāddhaviṣayam, tasya tatprakaraṇe pāṭhāt | atra pātraniyamam āha hārītaḥ: "lohamaye mṛnmaye vā pātre bhuñjīta" | tac ca bhuktvā svayaṃ prakṣālayet | tad āha āpastambaḥ: "bhuktvā svayam amatraṃ prakṣālayīta" iti | "bhaikṣeṇa vartayen nityam" ity uktam | tasya kvacid apavadam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	brāhmaṇaḥ kāmam aśnīyāc chrāddhe vratam apīḍayan |

apīḍayan madhumāṃsādi varjayann ity arthaḥ, tasya brahmacariṇaḥ pratiṣiddhatvāt | ata eva manuḥ |

	pratiṣiddhaṃ na bhoktavyaṃ madhumāṃsādi nityasaḥ | iti |

madhunaḥ punar akāmenopapannasya naiva doṣo 'stīty āha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "akāmopannaṃ madhu vajasaneyake na duṣyati" iti | yat tu viṣṇunoktam: "śrāddhakrtalavaṇaśuktaparyuṣitavarjanam" iti, tad anabhyarthitābhiprāyam | ata eva manuḥ |

	kāmam abhyarthito 'śnīyād vratam asya na lupyate | iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ bhikṣāṭanam**

**athopanītadharmāḥ**

tatra saṃvartaḥ |

	saṃdhyāṃ prātaḥ sanakṣatrām upāsīta yathāvidhi |

	sādityāṃ paścimāṃ saṃdhyām ardhāstamitabhāskarām ||

	tiṣṭhan pūrvāṃ japaṃ kuryād brahmacārī samāhitaḥ |

	āsīnaḥ paścimāṃ saṃdhyāṃ japaṃ kuryād atandritaḥ ||

	agnikāryaṃ ca kurvīta medhāvī tadanantaram |

	tato 'dhīyīta vedaṃ tu vīkṣamāṇo guror mukham ||

	sāyaṃ prātaś ca bhikṣeta brahmacārī samāhitaḥ |

	nivedya gurave 'śnīyāt prāṅmukho vāgyataḥ śuciḥ ||

manur api |

	nityaṃ snātvā śuciḥ kuryād devarṣipitṛtarpaṇam |

	devatābhyarcanaṃ kuryāt saṃdhyopāsanam eva ca || iti |

atra dakṣaḥ |

	prātar madhyāhnayoḥ snānaṃ vānaprasthagṛhasthayoḥ |

	yates triṣavaṇaṃ proktaṃ sakṛt tu brahmacāriṇaḥ || iti |

atra viśeṣam āha viṣṇuḥ: "daṇḍavan majjanam" iti | daṇḍavad ity anenāṅganairmalyaṃ na kāryam ity āha | ata eva āpastambaḥ: "nāpsu ślāghamānaḥ snayāt" iti | atra ye tv asādhāraṇadharmā agnīndhanādayas te yāvat samāvartanaṃ tāvad eva kāryā ity āha manuḥ |

	agnīndhanaṃ bhaikṣacaryam adhaḥśayyāṃ guror hitam |

	ā samāvartanaṃ kuryāt kṛtopanayano dvijaḥ ||

etac cānyeṣām apy evaṃjātīyānām upalakṣaṇārtham | at eva purāṇam |

	mekhalām ajinaṃ daṇḍam upavītaṃ ca nityaśaḥ |

	kaupīnaṃ kaṭisūtraṃ ca brahmacārī tu dhārayet ||

yamo 'pi |

	daṇḍaṃ kamaṇḍaluṃ vedaṃ mauñjīṃ ca raśanāṃ tathā |

	dhārayed brahmacaryaṃ ca bhikṣānnāśī gurau vasan ||

vedo dharbhamuṣṭiḥ | gurau gurugṛha ity arthaḥ | atra vasato ye dharmās tān āha vyāsaḥ |

	jaghanyaśāyī pūrvaṃ syād utthāya guruveśmani |

	yac ca śiṣyeṇa kartavyaṃ kāryaṃ dāsena vā punaḥ ||

	kṛtam ity eva tat sarvaṃ kṛtvā tiṣṭhet tu pārśvataḥ |

	kiṅkaraḥ sarvakāryeṣu sarvakarmasu kovidaḥ ||

	nābhuktavati nāśnīyād apītavati no pibet |

	na tiṣṭhati tathāsīta nāsupte prasvapet tathā ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	guruṃ caivāpy upāsīta svādhyāyarthaṃ samāhitaḥ |

	āhūtaś cāpy adhīyīta labdhaṃ cāsmai nivedayet ||

hārīto 'pi: "athodakumbhakuśapuṣpasaminmūlāharanasaṃmārjanopalepāṅgaśuśrūṣāprabhṛtibhir gacchantaṃ tiṣṭhantaṃ śayānam āsīnaṃ bhaktyānuvarteta | nāsya nirmālyaśayanāsanacchāyāpāduke vā kāmayet" iti | āpastambo 'pi: "ācāryādhīnaḥ syād anyatra patanīyebhyaḥ" iti | bodhāyano 'pi: "sarvatrāpratihataguruvākyo 'nyatra pātakāt" iti | yamo 'pi |

	gurvadhīno 'svatantaḥ syāt pūrvotthāyī guror gṛhe |

	sadā jaghanyasaṃveśī jitaśiśno jitodaraḥ ||

	jitanidro jitālasyo jitakrodho jitātmavān |

	śuśrūṣur anahaṃvādī gurudevārvane rataḥ ||

gurvarcanaṃ gurupūjā | tasyāḥ phalam āha śaṅkhaḥ |

	na snānena na homena naivāgniparicaryayā |

	brahmacārī divaṃ yāti sa yāti gurupūjanāt ||

manur api niyamāntarāṇy āha |

	nīcaśayyāsanaṃ cāsya nityaṃ syād gurusaṃnidhau |

	guroś ca cakṣurviṣaye na yatheṣṭāsano bhavet ||

etac ca gavādivyatiriktaviṣayam, tatra sahāsanavidhānāt | tad āha sa eva |

	go 'śvoṣṭrayānaprāsādaprastareṣu kaṭeṣu ca |

	āsīta guruṇā sārdhaṃ śilāphalakanauṣu ca ||

viṣṇur api: "nāsyaikāsano bhaved ṛte śilāphalakayānebhyaḥ" iti | tathā na guroḥ parīvādādy ākarṇanīyam | tathā ca manuḥ |

	guror yatra parīvādo nindā vāpi pravartate |

	karṇau tatra pidhātavyau gantavyaṃ vā tato 'nyataḥ || iti |

saddoṣakhyāpanaṃ parīvādaḥ | asaddoṣābhidhānaṃ nindā | na ca svenāpi parīvādādi kāryam | yad āha sa eva |

	parīvādāt kharo bhavati śvā vai bhavati nindakaḥ |

	paribhoktā krimir bhavati kīṭo bhavati matsarī ||

ananujñātagurudhanopajīvī paribhoktā | hārīto 'pi |

	amṛtasya pradātāraṃ guruṃ yas tva avamanyate |

	tac cainaṃ dahati brahma tiryagyonau ca jāyate ||

	ṛcaṃ vā yadi vā pādam ardhaṃ vā yadi vākṣaram |

	sakāśād yasya gṛhṇīyān niyataṃ tasya gauravam ||

tathā ca gurvāder nāmāpi na kīrtanīyam | tathā ca smṛtiḥ |

	ācāryaṃ caiva tatputraṃ tadbhāryāṃ dīkṣitaṃ gurum |

	pitaraṃ ca pitṛvyāṃś ca mātaraṃ mātulaṃ tathā |

	hitaiṣaṇaṃ ca vidvāṃsaṃ śvaśuraṃ yatim eva ca |

	na brūyān nāmato vidvān mātuś ca bhaginīṃ tathā || iti |

yatra punar gurvādināmagrahaṇam āvaśyakaṃ tatropādhyāyādiśabdena sa brūyāt | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "nāmagotre guroḥ samānato nirdiśet" iti | samānato mānena sahety arthaḥ | ata eva manuḥ |

	nodāhared asya nāma parokṣaṃ api kevalam |

	na caivāsyānukurvīta gatibhāṣitaceṣṭitam ||

tathā gurubhāryāder api śuśrūṣā kāryety āha viśvāmitraḥ |

	tadbhāryāputryoś caiva vṛddhānāṃ dharmaśālinām |

	śuśrūṣā sarvathā kāryā praṇāmo bhaktir eva ca || iti |

nārado 'pi |

	ā vidyāgrahaṇāc chiṣyaḥ śuśrūṣāprayato gurum |

	tadvṛttir gurudāreṣu guruputre tathaiva ca || iti |

sumantur api brahmacāriniyamam āha |

	brahmacaryaṃ tapo bhaikṣaṃ saṃdhyayor agnikarma ca |

	svādhyāyo guruvṛttiś ca caryeyaṃ brahmacāriṇaḥ || iti |

tapaḥśabdenātra brahmacāriniyamā ucyante | tathā cāpastambaḥ: "niyameṣu tapaḥśabdaḥ | tadatikrame vidyākarma niḥsravati" iti | ato niyamānuṣṭhānam āvaśyakam ity abhiprāyaḥ | ata eva manuḥ |

	sevetemāṃs tu niyamān brahmacārī gurau vasan |

	saṃniyamyendriyagrāmaṃ tapovṛddhyartham ātmanaḥ ||

	indriyāṇāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ yady ekaṃ kṣaratīndriyam |

	tenāsya kṣarati prajñā dṛteḥ pādād ivodakam ||

te ca yājñavalkyenoktāḥ |

	madhumāṃsāñjanocchiṣṭaśuktaṃ strīprāṇihiṃsanam |

	bhāskarālokanāślīlaparīvādādi varjayet ||

madhu kṣaudram | māṃsaṃ chāgāder api varjyam | etac ca vyādhirāhitye veditavyam, anyathā tu vaidyopadiṣṭaṃ madhumāṃsādikaṃ guror ucchiṣṭaṃ kṛtvā prāśnīyāt | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "sa ced vyādhīyīta kāmaṃ guror ucchiṣṭaṃ bhaiṣayjārthaṃ sarvaṃ prāśnīyāt" iti | vyādhīyīta vyādhimattām anubhavatīty arthaḥ | añjanaṃ tailādinā gātrasya, kajjalādinā cākṣṇoḥ | etad apy anyatra vaidyopadeśāt | auṣadhasyāvrataghnatvāt | tathā ca smṛtiḥ |

	aṣṭau tāny avraghnāni āpo mūlaṃ ghṛtaṃ payaḥ |

	havir brāhmaṇakāmyā ca guror vacanam auṣadham || iti |

ucchiṣṭaṃ guruvyatiriktasya varjayet | tad āha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "ucchiṣṭam aguror abhojyam" iti | aguror abhojyam ity anena guror ucchiṣṭaṃ bhojyam ity āha | ata eva āpastambaḥ: "pitur jyeṣṭhasya ca bhrātur ucchiṣṭaṃ bhoktavyam" iti | na ca, "ācāryaḥ śreṣṭho gurūṇāṃ mātety eke" iti mātur api gurutvaśravaṇāt tasyā ucchiṣṭaṃ bhoktavyam iti śaṅkanīyam, "sa gurur yaḥ kriyāḥ kṛtvā vedam asmai prayacchati" iti gurulakṣaṇavailakṣaṇyāt | atas tatraupacāriko guruśabda iti mantavyam | ata eva manuḥ |

	guruvat saṃprapūjyāḥ syuḥ savarṇā guruyoṣitaḥ | iti |

ata eva gautamo 'pi: "tadbhāryāputreṣu caivam" iti gurudharmātideśaṃ kṛtvā taducchiṣṭabhojanāpavādam āha: "nocchiṣṭāśanasnāpanaprasādhanapādaprakṣālanonmardanopasaṃgrahaṇāni" it | prasādhanam alaṃkaraṇam | unmardanam aṅgamardanam | evam atiśeṣeṇa guror ucchiṣṭabhojane prāpte kvacid apavādam āha āpastambaḥ: "dharmavipratipattāv abhojyam" iti | adharmopetasya pitur ucchiṣṭam abhojyam ity arthaḥ | śuktaṃ niṣṭhuraṃ vākyam | tad api varjayet | ata eva varjayed ity anuvṛttau gautamaḥ: "śuktā vācaḥ" iti | bhāskarālokam ādityāvekṣaṇam | tad api na kāryam ity āha manuḥ |

	nekṣetodyantam ādityam astaṃyantaṃ kadācana |

	nopaspṛṣṭaṃ na vāristhaṃ na madhyanabhaso gatam ||

upaspṛṣṭaṃ rāhugrastam | aślilam asatyabhāṣaṇam | parīvādaḥ paranindā | ādigrahaṇam anyeṣām api niyamānām upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva gautamaḥ: "varjayen madhumāṃsagandhamālya-divāsvapnāñjanābhyañjanayānopānacchatrakāmakrodhalobhamohavādanasnānadantadhāvana-harṣanṛttagītaparivādabhayāni" iti | gandhaś candanādi | tasya bhogārthasya pratiṣedho na devatāśiṣṭasya | tathā ca smṛtiḥ: "devatāśiṣṭam eva gṛhṇīyād brahmacārī" iti | evaṃ mālāyām api draṣṭavyam | yānaṃ śibikādi | vādo bahupralāpaḥ | vādanaṃ bherītāḍanādi | snānam upabhogārtham, nityasya vihitatvāt | bhayaṃ parasya | manur api |

	varjayen madhu māṃsaṃ ca gandhamālyarasān striyaḥ |

	śuktāni caiva sarvāṇi prāṇināṃ caiva hiṃsanam ||

	abhyaṅgam añjanaṃ cākṣṇor upānacchatradhāraṇam |

	kāmaṃ krodhaṃ ca lobhaṃ ca nartanaṃ gītavādanam ||

	dyūtaṃ ca janavādaṃ ca parivādaṃ tathānṛtam |

	strīṇāṃ ca prekṣaṇālambham upaghātaṃ parasya ca || iti |

rasā iṣṅurasādayaḥ | madhuno rasatve 'pi pṛthaṅgrahaṇaṃ prāyaścittagurutvakhyāpanārtham | strīprekṣaṇālambhane tu yatra maithunaśaṅkā tatraiva varjayet, itaratrāśakyaparihāratvāt | ata eva varjayed ity anuvṛttau gautamaḥ: "strīprekṣaṇālambhane maithunaśaṅkāyām" iti | tathā niyamāntarāṇy api sa evāha: "gurudarśane kaṇṭhaprāvṛtāvasakthikāpāśrayaṇapādaprasāraṇāni niṣṭhīvitahasitavijṛmbhitāvasphoṭanāni" | atrāpi varjayed ity anuvartate | kaṇṭhaprāvṛtaṃ vastrādinā kaṇṭhaprāvaraṇam | avasakthikā jānvor madhyasya ca vastrādinā bandhanam | apāśrayaṇaṃ kuḍyādisaṃśrayaṇam | vijṛmbhitaṃ jṛmbhaṇam | avasphoṭanaṃ bhujāsphālanādi | hasitaṃ prasiddham | tac ca yady aśakyaparihāraṃ tadā mukhaṃ pidhāya kāryam | tad āha āpastambaḥ: "yadi smayetāpigṛhya smayetati hi brāhmaṇam | nopajighret striyaṃ mukhena na hṛdayena prārthayen nākāraṇād upaspṛśet" iti | punar āpastambaḥ: "datvā nānukathayet kṛtvā ca nanusmared ātmapraśaṃsā paragarhām iti ca varjayet" iti | hārīto 'pi: "hayagamarathacaitya-vṛkṣaviṣamārohaṇapracayanasaṃsiddhisarpaṇamahānadyarṇavaprataraṇamahāsāhasaviruddhāni varjayet" iti | āpastambo 'pi: "strībhir yāvad arthasaṃbhāṣī mṛduḥ śānto dānto hrīman dṛḍhadhṛtiḥ" iti | viṣṇur api: "kṛtalavaṇaṃ brahmacārī varjayet" iti | kṛtalavaṇam ūṣaralavaṇam | manur api |

	nainaṃ grāme 'bhinimlocet sūryo nābhyudayāt kvacit |

	sūryeṇa hy abhinirmuktaḥ śayāno 'bhyuditaś ca yaḥ ||

	prāyaścittam akurvāṇo yuktaḥ syān mahatainasā |

	muṇḍo vā jaṭilo vā syād atha vā syāc chikhājaṭaḥ || iti |

muṇḍaḥ śikhāvihīnaḥ, "muṇḍaḥ śikhī vā" iti gautamasmaraṇāt | kātyāyano 'pi |

	saśikhaṃ vapanaṃ kāryam ā snānād brahmacāriṇaḥ |

	ā śarīravimokṣāt tu brahmacaryaṃ na ced bhavet || iti |

etac chandogābhiprāyam | tathā ca śrīviṣṇupurāṇe bharatavākyam |

	ete lūnaśikhās tasya daśanair acirodgataiḥ |

	kuśakāśā virājante vaṭaḥ sāmagā iva ||

"adhaḥ śayīta" ity uktaṃ gautamena | tatra viśeṣam āha yamaḥ |

	khaṭvāsanaṃ ca śayanaṃ varjayed dantadhāvanam |

	svaped ekaḥ kuśeṣv eva na retaḥ skandayet kvacit ||

manur api |

	ekaḥ śayīta sarvatra na retaḥ skandayet kvacit |

	kāmād dhi skandayed reto hinasti vratam ātmanaḥ ||

vrataṃ brahmacaryam | akāmata utsarge prāyaścittamātraṃ na vratalopa ity āha sa eva |

	svapne siktvā brahmacārī dvijaḥ śuklam akāmataḥ |

	snātvārkam arcayitvāpi punar mām ity ṛcaṃ japet || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām upanītadharmāḥ**

**atha vedapraśaṃsā**

tatra manuḥ |

	cāturvarṇyaṃ trayo lokāś catvāraś cāśramāḥ pṛthak |

	bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyac ca sarvaṃ vedāt prasiddhyati ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	yajñānāṃ tapasāṃ caiva śubhānāṃ caiva karmaṇām |

	veda eva dvijātīnāṃ niḥśreyasakaraḥ paraḥ ||

yajñādīnāṃ karmaṇāṃ madhye vedābhyāsa eva dvijātīnāṃ para utkṛṣṭo niḥśreyasakaraḥ, tasya taporūpatvāt | tathā ca manuḥ |

	vedam eva sadābhyaset tapas tapsyan dvijottamaḥ |

	vedābhyāso 'pi viprasya tapaḥ param ihocyate ||

	ā haiva sa nakhāgrebhyaḥ paramaṃ tapyate tapaḥ |

	yaḥ sragvy api dvijo 'dhīte svādhyāyaṃ śaktito 'nvaham ||

yaḥ pratyahaṃ yathāśakti svādhyāyam adhīte sa ā nakhāgrebhyaḥ param utkṛṣṭaṃ tapaḥ karotīty arthaḥ | heyti prasiddhau | sragvī ghṛtamālyo niyamavihīno 'pīti yāvat | vyāso 'pi |

	nānyato jñāyate dharmaḥ vedād evaiṣa nirbabhau |

	tasmāt sarvaprayatnena dharmārthī vedam abhyaset ||

dharmārthī dharmajñānārtham | ata eva manuḥ |

	pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇāṃ vedaś cakṣur sanātanaḥ | iti |

vedavidaḥ phalam api sa evāha |

	yathā jātabalo vahnir dahaty ārdrān api drumān |

	tathā dahati vedajñaḥ karmajaṃ doṣam ātmanaḥ ||

tathā vedavihīnasya sarvakriyānaiṣphalyam api sa evāha |

	yathā ṣaṇḍo 'phalaḥ strīṣu yathā gaur gavi cāphalā |

	yathā cājñe 'phalaṃ dānaṃ tathā vipro 'nṛco 'phalaḥ ||

vasiṣṭho 'pi |

	yaś ca kāṣṭhamayo hastī yaś ca carmamayo mṛgaḥ |

	yaś ca vipro 'nadhīyānas trayas te nāmadhārakāḥ ||

yathā dārvādinirmito hastī yuddhādikarmayogyo na bhavati tathānadhīyāno 'pi svakarmayogyo na bhavatīty arthaḥ | ata evāyaṃ brāhmaṇo na bhavatīty āha sa eva |

	nānṛco brāhmaṇo bhavati na vaṇiṅ na kṛṣīvalaḥ |

	na śūdrapreṣaṇaṃ kurvan na steno na cikitsakaḥ ||

manur api |

	yo 'nadītya dvijo vedān anyatra kurute śramam |

	sa jīvann eva śūdratvam āśu gacchati sānvayaḥ ||

ataḥ pūrvaṃ vedādhyayanena bhavitavyam ity arthaḥ | ata eva śaṅkhaḥ: "na vedam anadhītyānyāṃ vidyām adhīyītānyatra vedāṅgasmṛtibhyaḥ" iti | aṅgāder api tadarthaparijñānārthatvād ity abhiprāyaḥ | tathā ca hārītaḥ: "vedo vai vidyā brāhmaṇasya | tatparijñānārtham aṅgāni" iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vedapraśaṃsā**

**atha śrutapraśaṃsā**

tatra laghuvyāsaḥ |

	na vedapāṭhamātreṇa saṃtoṣaṃ kārayed budhaḥ |

	pāṭhamātrāvasāyī tu paṅke gaur iva sīdati || iti |

nirukte 'pi: "sthāṇur ayaṃ bhāraharaḥ kilābhūd adhītya vedaṃ na vijānāti yo 'rtham" iti | laghuvyāso 'pi |

	vedasvādhyayanaṃ sarvaṃ dharmaśāstrasya cāpi yat |

	ajānato 'rthaṃ tat sarvaṃ tuṣāṇāṃ khaṇḍanaṃ yathā ||

	yathā paśur bhāravāhī na tasya bhajate phalam |

	dvijas tadarthānabhijño na vedaphalam aśnute ||

vaidikakarmaphalabhāṅ na bhavatīty arthaḥ | ata evāsya śūdrasamānatvam āha sa eva |

	yo 'dhītya vidhivad vipro vedārthaṃ na vicārayet |

	sa sānvayaḥ śūdrasamaḥ pātratāṃ na prapadyate ||

ata eva caiteṣāṃ vāṅmātreṇāpi pūjā na kāryety āha sa eva |

	pāṭhamātrapārān nityaṃ dvijātīṃś cārthavarjitān |

	paśūn iva sa tān prājño vāṅmātreṇāpi nārcayet ||

ato 'dhītavedasya tadarthavicāra āvaśyaka ity abhiprāyaḥ | ata eva dakṣaḥ |

	vedasvīkaraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ vicāro 'bhyasanaṃ japaḥ |

	taddānaṃ caiva śiṣyebhyo vedābhyāso hi pañcadhā ||

vicāro vedārthavicāraḥ | laghuvyāso 'pi |

	śrutahīnam adhītaṃ yat naha nāputra tad bhavet |

	śrutaṃ tu kevalam api samuddārāya kalpate ||

kiṃ punaḥ samuccitam ity abhiprāyaḥ | tad āha sa eva |

	jñānaṃ karma ca saṃyuktaṃ muktyarthaṃ kathitaṃ yathā |

	adhītaṃ śrutasaṃyuktaṃ tathā śreṣṭhaṃ na kevalam ||

	samuccitaṃ stokam api śrutādhītaṃ viśiṣyate |

	caturṇām api varṇānāṃ kevalādhyayanād dvijāt || iti |

vedārthavidaḥ phalam āha manuḥ |

	vedaśāstrārthatattvajño yatra yatrāśrame vaset |

	ihaiva tiṣṭhan loke sa brahmabhūyāya kalpate ||

hārīto 'pi |

	mantrārthjño japan juhvaṃs tathaivādhyāpayan dvijaḥ |

	svargalokam avāpnoti narakaṃ tu viparyaye ||

nirukte 'pi: "yo 'rthavit sakalaṃ bhadram aśnute sa nākam eti jñānavidhūtapāpmā" iti | manus tv abhyasanīyāni śāstrāṇy āha |

	buddhivṛddhikarāṇy āśu dhānyāni ca hitāni ca |

	nityaṃ śāstrāṇy avekṣeta nigamāṃś caiva vaidikān ||

purāṇe 'pi |

	dharmaśāstraṃ tu vijñeyaṃ śabdaśāstraṃ tathaiva ca |

	purāṇānītihāsāś ca tad ākhyānāni yāni ca ||

	mahātmanāṃ ca caritaṃ śrotavyaṃ nityam eva ca | iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ śrutapraśaṃsā**

**athādhyayanavidhiḥ **

tatra manuḥ |

	tapoviśeṣair vividhair vrataiś ca vidhicoditaiḥ |

	vedaḥ kṛtsno 'dhigantavyaḥ sarahasyo dvijanmanā ||

rahasyam upaniṣat | adhigantavyo 'dhyetavya ity arthaḥ | tathā ca srutiḥ: "svādhyāyo 'dhyetavyaḥ" iti | svakulaparaṃparāgatā śākhādhyetavyeti yāvat | ata eva vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	pāramparyāgato yeṣāṃ vedaḥ saparibṛṃhaṇaḥ |

	tacchākhaṃ karma kurvīta tacchākhādhyayanaṃ tathā || iti |

śākhāntarādhyayane śākhāraṇḍo bhavatīty abhiprāyaḥ | yad āha sa eva |

	ekadeśe 'pi śākhānāṃ madhye yo 'nyatamaṃ vrajet |

	svaśākhāṃ saṃparityajya śākhāraṇḍaḥ sa ucyate ||

tasya doṣam ap sa evāha |

	svaśākhāṃ yaḥ parityajya pārakyam adhigacchati |

	sa śūdravad bahiṣkāryaḥ sarvakarmasu sādhubhiḥ ||

	ātmaśākhāṃ parityajya paraśākhāsu vartate |

	ucchettā tasya vaṃśasya rauravaṃ narakaṃ vrajet ||

	svīyaśākhojjhitā yena brahma tenojjhitaṃ param |

	brahmahaiva sa vijñeyaḥ sadbhir nityaṃ vigarhitaḥ || iti |

logākṣir api |

	yaḥ svaśākhāṃ parityajya pārakyam adhigacchati |

	sa śūdravad bahiṣkāryo havyakavyeṣu dātṛbhiḥ ||

anena svaśākhāyā aparityāgena śākhāntarādhyayanam aviruddham ity āha | ata eva vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	adhītya śākhām ātmīyāṃ paraśākhāṃ tataḥ paṭhet |

tathā niyamāntaram api sa evāha |

	yac chākhīyais tu saṃskāraiḥ saṃskṛto brāhmaṇo bhavet |

	tac chākhādhyayanaṃ kuryāt tyāgena patito bhavet ||

yas tu svaśākhīyaṃ karma parityajya śākhāntaroktam ācarati, so 'pi śākhāraṇḍa ity āha vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	na jātu paraśākhoktaṃ budhaḥ karma samācaret |

	ācaran paraśākhoktaṃ śākhāraṇḍaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||

saṃgrahakāras tv asyāp doṣam āha |

	yaḥ svaśākhoktam utsṛjya paraśākoktam ācaret |

	apramāṇam ṛṣiṃ kṛtvā so 'ndhe tamasi majjati ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	svaśākhāśrayam utsṛjya paraśākhāśrayaṃ tu yaḥ |

	kartum icchati durmedhā moghaṃ tasya viceṣṭitam ||

anenāpi svaśākhīyakarmāparityāgena śākhāntarāśrayaṇam aviruddham iti jñāyate | tad api tenaivoktam |

	yan nāmnātaṃ svaśākhāyāṃ paroktam avirodhi ca |

	vidvadbhis tad anuṣṭheyam agnihotrādikarmavat || iti |

athādhyayanārambhaṃ prakṛtyāha manuḥ |

	oṅkārapūrvikās tisro mahāvyāhṛtayo 'vyayāḥ |

	tripadā caiva sāvitrī vijñeyā brahmaṇo mukham ||

oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar iti mahāvyāhrtayas tisraḥ | tat savitur iti sāvitrī brahmaṇo mukhaṃ vedasya mukham ārambha ity arthaḥ | gautamas tu pañca vyāhṛtayaḥ prayojyā ity āha: "oṃpūrvā vyāhṛtayaḥ pañca satyāntāḥ" iti | etac cānvahaṃ veditavyam | tathā ca saṃvartaḥ |

	praṇavaṃ prāk prayuñjīta vyāhṛtīs tadanantaram |

	sāvitryāś cānuvacanaṃ tato vṛttāntam ārabhet ||

vṛttāntaṃ yat prastutam ity arthaḥ | praṇavoccāraṇam api prāṇāyāmatrayād upari veditavyam | tad āha manuḥ |

	prākkūlān paryupāsīnaḥ pavitraiś caiva pāvitaḥ |

	prāṇāyāmais tribhiḥ pūtas tata oṃkāram arhati ||

prākkūlān prāgagrān ity arthaḥ | pavitraṃ pāvanam iti | gautamenoktam: "prāṇopasparśanaṃ darbhaiḥ" iti | prāṇā iti cakṣurādīndriyāṇi śrīṣanyāny ucyante | tāni darbhair upaspṛśed ity arthaḥ | prāṇāyāmā api tenaivoktāḥ: "prāṇāyāmās trayaḥ pañcadaśamātrāḥ" iti | prāṇāyāmaḥ prāṇanirodhaḥ nirucchvāsenāvasthānam iti yāvat | laghvakṣaroccāraṇakālo mātrā | pañcadaśamātrā ity anena "savyāhṛtikāṃ sapraṇavām" ity asya pratiṣedham āha | etac ca praṇavoccāraṇam adhītyāpi kāryam | tad āha manuḥ |

	brahmaṇaḥ praṇavaṃ kuryād ādāv ante ca sarvadā |

	sravaty anoṃkrtaṃ pūrvaṃ parastāc ca viśīryati || iti |

niyamāntaram api sa evāha |

	brahmārambhe 'vasāne ca pādau grāhyau guroḥ sadā |

pādagrahṇam upasaṃgrahaṇam | yad āha aṅgirāḥ |

	prāpte vedānuvacane visarge cānvahaṃ guroḥ |

	upasaṃgrahaṇaṃ kāryaṃ viproṣya tv āgatena ca || iti |

gautamas tv adhyettur diṅniyamam āha: "prāṅmukho dakṣiṇataḥ śiṣya udaṅmukho vā" iti | manur api |

	adhyeṣyamāṇas tv ācānto yathāśāstram udaṅmukhaḥ |

	brahmāñjalikṛto 'dhyāpyo laghuvāsā jitendriyaḥ ||

adhyeṣyamāṇa iti vacanād etad ācamanam adhyayanāṅgam | brahmāñjalim api sa evāha |

	saṃhatya hastāv adhyeyaṃ sa hi brahmāñjaliḥ smṛtaḥ | iti |

atra viśeṣam āha saṃvartaḥ |

	tato 'dhīyīta vedaṃ tu vīkṣamāṇo guror mukham |

	hastau tu saṃhatau kāryau jānubhām upari sthitau ||

guror mukhaṃ vīkṣamāṇa ity anena gurumukhād eva vedo 'dhyetavya ity āha | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	pustakapratyayādhītaṃ nādhītaṃ gurusaṃnidhau |

	bhrājate na sabhāmadhye jāragarbha iva striyāḥ ||

gurusaṃnidhāne 'pi tadanujñayādhyetavyam, anyathā doṣaśravaṇāt | tad āha laghuvyāsaḥ |

	ṛcam ardharcam atha vā pādaṃ vā yadi vākṣaram |

	gṛhṇāti yo 'nanujñāto parasmāt parato dvijaḥ ||

	sa brahmasteyasaṃyukto narakaṃ pratipadyate |

tathā śūdrasaṃnidhāne 'pi nādhyetavyam | tad āha sa eva |

	anadhyāyeṣv adhītaṃ yad yac ca śūdrasya saṃnidhau |

	pratigrahanimittaṃ ca narakāya tad ucyate ||

manur api |

	nāvispaṣṭam adhīyīta na śūdrajanasaṃnidhau |

	na niśānte pariśrānto brahmādhītya punaḥ svapet ||

avispaṣṭaṃ varṇasvarādirahitam | niśānte rātrer aparabhāge | brahmādhītya śrānto 'pi punar na svaped ity arthaḥ | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "nāpararātram adhītya punaḥ pratisaṃviśet" iti | hārīto 'pi: "brāhme muhūrte pratibudhya svādyāyam āvartya na pratisaṃviśet" | nāradas tu varṇasvarādirahitādhyayane doṣam āha |

	hastahīnaṃ tu yo 'dhīte svaravarṇavivarjitam |

	ṛgyajuḥsāmabhir dagdho viyonim adhigacchati ||

	hastenādhīyamānas tu svaravarṇān prayojayan |

	ṛgyajuḥsāmabhiḥ pūto brahmalokaṃ sa gacchati ||

etac cādhyayanādiphalaṃ garbhādhānādisaṃskāravata eva nānyasyety āha laghuvyāsaḥ |

	saṃskāravadbhiḥ kartavyaṃ vedasyādhyayanaṃ dvijaiḥ |

	śūdrasya phalavat tat syād anyathā niṣphalaṃ smṛtam ||

niyamāntarāṇy api sa evāha |

	mekhalājinadaṇḍānāṃ dhāribhir brahmacāribhiḥ |

	vedaḥ kṛtsno 'dhigantavyaḥ satpathācāravartibhiḥ ||

	bhikṣāśibhir guror nityaṃ śuśrūṣāyāṃ ratais tathā |

	ā samāpter vrataṃ kuryād vedasya vidhirvād (?) dvijaiḥ ||

śuśrūṣā paricaryā | tasyāḥ phalam āha manuḥ |

	yathā khanan kanitreṇa naro vāry adhigacchati |

	evaṃ gurugatāṃ vidyāṃ śuśrūṣur adhigacchati ||

nārado vidyādhigamopāyam āha |

	yo 'her iva ṛṇād bhītaḥ sauhityān narakād iva |

	rākṣasībhya iva strībhyaḥ sa vidyām adhigacchati \|

	yat kīṭaiḥ pāṃsubhiḥ ślakṣṇair valmīkaḥ kriyate mahān |

	na tatra balasāmarthyam udyogas tatra kāraṇam ||

	śanair vidyāṃ śanair arthān ārohet parvataṃ śanaiḥ |

tṛptiḥ sauhityam | tathā vighanahetūn api sa evāha |

	dyūtaṃ pustakaśuśrūṣā nāṭakāsaktir eva ca |

	striyas tandrī ca nidrā ca vidyāvighnakarāṇi ṣaṭ ||

śusrūṣā śrotum icchā | tandrī ālasyam | evam uktaniyamavihīnād adhyayanābhāvo varam ity āha laghuvyāsaḥ |

	ṛkpādam apy adhīyīta mārgeṇoktena dharmavit |

	na tv eva caturo vedān anyāyena kadācana ||

	vedaviplāvanāt tena varaṃ maunaṃ samāśritam |

	vedaviplāvanād vipro narakaṃ yāty adhomukhaḥ ||

vedaviplāvakasya lakṣaṇam āha yamaḥ |

	yo 'rthārthīmān dvije dadyāt paṭhed evāvidhānataḥ |

	anadhāye ca taṃ prāhur vedaviplāvakaṃ budhāḥ ||

atra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	kṛtajño 'drohī medhāvī śuciḥ kalpo 'nasūyakaḥ |

	adhyāpyāḥ sādhuśaktāptasvārthadā dharmatas tv ime ||

kṛtajña upakārasmartā | adrohy anaparādhī | medhāvī dhāraṇāvān | śuciḥ prayataḥ | kalyo virogaḥ | anasūyakaḥ parapuruṣadoṣān āviṣkaraṇaśīlaḥ | sādhuḥ vṛttavān | śaktaḥ śuśrūṣāyāṃ | āpto 'pratārakaḥ | svaḥ jñātiḥ | arthado gurvarthapradātā | ime dharmataḥ dharmānatirekeṇādhyāpyāḥ | 	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> arthado 'dhyāpya it na ghaṭate,

	bhṛtād adhyayanādānaṃ bhṛtkādhyāpanaṃ tathā |

ity upapātakamadhye paṭhitatvāt | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivaṃ</span> bhṛtisaṃpratipattipūrvakam evādhyāpanaṃ pratiṣiddham itarasya vṛttihetutvenāvirodhāt | ata eva manuḥ |

	dharmārthau yatra na syātāṃ śuśrūṣā vāpi tadvidhā |

	tatra vidyā na vaktavyā śubhaṃ bījam ivoṣare ||

yamo 'pi |

	yato dharmāgamo na syān na śusrūṣādhanāgamau |

	vidyayā saha martavyaṃ na vidyām ūṣare vapet ||

manus tu jñānado 'py adhyāpya ity āha |

	ācāryaputraḥ śusrūṣur jñānado dhārmikaḥ suciḥ |

	āptaḥ śakto 'rthadaḥ sādhuḥ svo 'dhyāpyā daśa dharmataḥ ||

śakto vidyāgrahaṇasamarthaḥ | jñānado vidyāpradaḥ | nārado 'pi |

	guruśuśrūṣayā vidyā puṣkalena dhanena vā |

	atha vā vidyayā vidyā caturthaṃ nopalabhyate ||

ime 'dhyāpyā iti vadann asūyakadayo nādhyāpyā ity āha | ata eva vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	vidyā ha vai brāhmaṇam ājagām gopāya mā śevadhis te 'ham asmi |

	asūyakāyānṛjave 'yatāya na māṃ brūyā vīryavatī tathā syām ||

	yam eva vidyāḥ śucim apramattaṃ medhāvinaṃ brahmacaryopapannam |

	yas te na druhyet katamac ca nāha tasmai māṃ brūyā nidhipāya brahman || iti |

śevadhiḥ nidhiḥ | viṣṇur api: "naparīkṣitaṃ yajayen nādhyāpayen nopanayet" iti | adhyāpane niyamaviśeṣān āha yamaḥ |

	satataṃ prātar utthāya dantadhāvanapūrvakam |

	snātvā hutvātha śiṣyebhyo kuryād adhyāpanaṃ naraḥ ||

āpastambo 'pi: "śayānaś cādhyāpanaṃ varjayen na ca tasyāṃ śayyāyām adhyapayed yasyāṃ śayīta" iti | manur api |

	adhyeṣyamāṇas tu gurur nityakālam atandritaḥ |

	adhīṣva bho iti brūyād viromo 'stv iti cāramet ||

āramed adhyapanān nivartayetety arthaḥ | yaḥ punar ananyamanā nādhīte taṃ nirbhartsanādinā śikṣayet | tad āha gautamaḥ: "śiṣyaśiṣtir avadhena" iti | śiṣṭiḥ śāsanam | avadhena tāḍanam akṛtvety arthaḥ | śiṣyagrahaṇam anyasyāpi bhāryādeḥ śāsanīyasyānyasyopalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva manuḥ |

	bhāryā putraś ca dāsaś ca preṣyo bhrātā ca sodaraḥ |

	prāptāparādhās tāḍyāḥ syū rajjvā veṇudalena vā ||

etac ca nirbhartsanādinā śāsitum aśaktau veditavyam | ata eva gautamaḥ: "aśaktau rajjuveṇudalābhyāṃ tanubhyām" iti | tādanam iti śeṣaḥ | tac ca śirasi na kāryam | tad āha manuḥ |

	pṛṣṭhatas tu śarīrasya nottamāṅge kathaṃ cana |

	ato 'nyathā tu praharan prāptaḥ syāc corakilbiṣam ||

yas tu hastādinā tāḍayati sa rājñā śāsanīya ity āha gautamaḥ: "anyena nighnan rājñā śāsyaḥ" iti | ya punar arthine vidyāṃ na prayacchati tasya doṣam āha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "yo hi vidyām adhītyārthine na saṃpradadyāt sa karmānarhaḥ syāt" iti | yamo 'pi |

	saṃvatsaroṣite śiṣye gurur jñānaṃ na nirdiśet |

	harate duṣkrtaṃ tasya śiṣyasya vasato guruḥ ||

etac ca śūdraśiṣyavyatiriktaviṣayam | tasyādhyayananiṣedhāt tathā cāpastambaḥ: "aśūdrāṇām aduṣṭakarmaṇām upāyanaṃ vedādhyayanam agnyādheyaṃ phalavanti ca karmāṇi" iti | etac cādhyayanaṃ brāhmaṇād eva kāryam | tasyaiva pravacane 'dhikārāt | tathā ca manuḥ |

	adhīyīraṃs trayo varṇāḥ svakarmasthā dvijātayaḥ |

	prabrūyād brāhmaṇas teṣāṃ netarāv iti niścayaḥ ||

etad anāpadviṣayam | āpadi kṣatriyāder apy adhyayanavidhānāt | tad āha sa eva |

	abrāhmaṇād adhyayanam āpatkāle vidhīyate |

	anuvrajyā ca śuśrūṣā yāvad adhyayanaṃ guroḥ ||

tatrānugamanamātram eva śuśrūṣā | sāpi yāvad adhyayanaṃ tāvad eva kāryam ity arthay | gautamo 'pi: "āpatkalpo brāhmaṇasyābhrāhmaṇād vidyopayogo 'nugamanaṃ śuśrūṣā samāpte brāhmaṇo guruḥ" iti | vidyāgrahaṇam anyeṣāṃ ratnaprabhṛtīnām upalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva devalaḥ |

	ratnāny āpaḥ striyo vidyā dharmaḥ śaucaṃ subhāṣitam |

	vividhāni ca śilpāni samādeyāni sarvataḥ ||

manur api |

	śraddadhānaḥ subhāṃ vidyām ādadītāvarād api |

	antyād api paraṃ dharmaṃ strīratnaṃ duṣkulād api ||

	viṣād apy amṛtaṃ grāhyaṃ bālād api subhāṣitam |

	amitrād api sadvṛttam amedhyād api kāñcanam ||

tathā vidyāphalam api sa evāha |

	tapo vidyāpi viprasya niḥśrayasakaraṃ param |

	tapasā kalmaṣaṃ hanti vidyayāmṛtam aśnute ||

devalo 'pi |

	vidyā vittaṃ tapaś ceti trīṇi tejāṃsi dehinaḥ |

	iha cāmutra ca śreyas tad etaiḥ sādhyate tribhiḥ ||

	vidyayā nirmalaṃ jyotir vittatyāgāt sukhodayam |

	tapasā vimalāṃ bhūtiṃ prāpnuyān mānavas tribhiḥ || iti |

vidyādānasya phalam āha yamaḥ |

	daśānāṃ tu sahasrāṇāṃ yuktānāṃ dhuryavāhinām |

	supātre viniyuktānāṃ kanyā vidyā ca tatsamam || iti |

bṛhaspatir api |

	sahasrasaṃmitā dhenur anaḍvān daśa dhenavaḥ |

	daśānaḍutsamaṃ yānaṃ daśayānasamo hayaḥ ||

	daśavājisamā kanyā bhūmidānaṃ ca tatsamam ||

	bhūmidānāt paraṃ nāsti vidyādānaṃ tato 'dhikam ||

manur api |

	sarveṣām eva dānānāṃ brahmadānaṃ viśiṣyate |

	vāryannagomahīvāsastilakāñcanasarpiṣām ||

saṃvarto 'pi |

	vidyādānena sumanāḥ śivaloke mahīyate | iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām adhyayanavidhiḥ**

**athopākaraṇam**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	adhyāyānām upākarma śrāvaṇyāṃ śravaṇena vā |

	hastenauṣadhibhāve vā pañcamyāṃ śrāvaṇasya tu ||

adhīyanta ity adhyāyā vedāḥ | teṣām upākarmākhyaṃ karma śrāvaṇyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ śravaṇena vā nakṣatreṇa hastena vā yuktāyāṃ pañcamyām oṣadhiprādurvāve sati kāryam | tathā ca āśvalāyanaḥ: "athāto 'dhyāyānām upākaraṇam oṣadhīnāṃ prādurbhāve śravaṇena śrāvaṇyāṃ pañcamyāṃ hastena vā" iti | yadā tu śrāvaṇe māsi na prādurbhavanty odhayas (?) tadā prauṣṭhapadyāṃ karyam | ata eva śaunakaḥ: "tad vārṣikam ity etad ācakṣate" iti | vasiṣṭho 'pi: "athātaḥ svādhyāyopākarma śrāvaṇyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ prauṣṭhapadyāṃ vā" iti | prauṣṭhapadī bhādrapadasya paurṇamāsī | tatra śravaṇe nakṣatre viśeṣam āha vyāsaḥ |

	śravaṇena tu yat karma uttarāṣāḍhasaṃyutam |

	saṃvatsarakṛto 'dhyāyas tatkṣaṇād eva naśyati ||

	dhaniṣṭhāsaṃyutaṃ kuryāc chrāvaṇe karma tad bhavet |

	tat karma saphalaṃ vidyād upākaraṇasaṃjñitam || iti |

bodāyanas tv āṣāḍhyām evopākaraṇam āha: "śrāvaṇyāṃ paurṇamāsyām āṣāḍhyāṃ vopākṛtya taiṣyāṃ māghyāṃ votsṛjet" iti | taiṣī tiṣyasya paurṇamāsī | evaṃ chandāṃsy upākṛtyānantaraṃ pakṣadvaye 'pi sārdhāṃś caturo māsān adhīyīta | tathā ca manuḥ |

	śrāvaṇyāṃ prauṣṭhapadyāṃ vāpy upākṛtya yathāvidhi |

	yuktaḥ chandāṃśy adhīyīta māsān vipro 'rdhapañcamān ||

yukto yatnavān vasiṣṭhas tv ardhaṣaṣṭhān māsān adhīyītety āha: "ardhapañcamān māsān ardhaṣaṣṭhān vā" iti | etac cādhyayanaṃ gṛhasthasyāpy aviruddham | ata evādhīyītety anuvṛttau śaunakaḥ: "samāvṛtto brahmacārikalpena yathānyāyam itare jāyopeyīty eke" | itare brahmacāriṇa ity arthaḥ |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām upākaraṇam**

**athotsarjanam**

tatra manuḥ |

	puṣye tu chandasāṃ kuryād bahir utsarjanaṃ dvijaḥ |

	mādhaśuklasya vā prāpte pūrvāhṇe prathame 'hani ||

śuklapratipadi pūrvāhṇi ity ubhayatrāpi saṃbadhyate | atra yaḥ śrāvaṇyām upākuryād asau puṇyamāsasya śuklapratipat pūrvāhṇe utsṛjet | itaras tu māghe | ardhapañcamān māsān adhīyīteti tenaivoktatvāt | āpastambas tu taiṣyāṃ paurṇamāsyām utsarjanam āha: "taiṣyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ rohiṇyāṃ vā viramet" iti | rohiṇy api tiṣyasyaiva grāhyā | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	pauṣamāsasya rohiṇyām aṣṭakāyām athāpi vā |

	jalānte chandasāṃ kuryād utsargaṃ vidhivad bahiḥ || iti |

atra purāṇam |

	upākarmaṇi cotsarge yathākālaṃ sametya ca |

	ṛṣīn darbhamayān kṛtvā pūjayet tarpayet tataḥ || iti |

evam utsṛjyānantaraṃ chandāṃsi śuklapakṣeṣv adhīyīta | vedāṅgāni kṛṣṇapakṣeṣv adhīyīta | tathā ca manuḥ |

	ata ūrdhvaṃ tu chandāṃsi śukleṣu niyataḥ paṭhet |

	vedāṅgāni tu sarvāṇi kṛṣṇapakṣeṣu saṃpaṭhet ||

vasiṣṭho 'pi: "ata ūrdhvaṃ śuklapaṣeṣv adhīyīta kāmaṃ tu vedāṅgāni" iti | kāmam iti vadann aṅgādhyayanam anadhyāye 'py aviruddham ity āha | ata eva manuḥ |

	vedopakaraṇe caiva svādhyāye caiva naityake |

	nānurodho 'sty anadhyāye homamantreṣu caiva hi ||

vedopakaraṇāny aṅgāni | nityasvādhyāyo brahmayajñaḥ | etat karmadvayaṃ chandasām ayātayāmatvāyety āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	pratyabdaṃ yad upākarma sotsargaṃ vidhivat dvijaiḥ |

	kriyate chandasāṃ tena punar āpyāyanaṃ bhavet ||

	ayātayāmaiś chandobhir yat karma kriyate dvijaiḥ |

	krīḍamānair api sadā tat teṣāṃ siddhikāraṇam || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām utsarjanam**

**athānadhyāyāḥ**

tatra manuḥ |

	vidyutstanitavarṣeṣu maholkānāṃ ca saṃplave |

	ākālikam anadhyāyam eteṣu manur abravīt ||

stanitaṃ medhagarjanam | eteṣu vidyudādiṣu pratyekam ākāliko nimittakālād ārabhya paredyur yāvat sa eva kālas tāvad anadhyāya ity arthaḥ | etac ca vidyudāditrayaṃ varṣābhyo 'nyatra saṃdhyākāle veditavyam | yad āha sa eva |

	etān abhyuditān vidyād yadā prāduṣkṛtāgniṣu |

	tadā vidyād anadhyāyam anṛtau cābbhradarśane ||

prāduṣkaraṇaṃ viharaṇam | tenātra saṃdhyakālo lakṣyate | anṛtau varṣābhyo 'nyatra | athākālikā ity anuvṛttau gautamaḥ: "stanayitnuvarṣavidyutaś ca prāduṣkṛtāgniṣu" iti | ulkāyāṃ tu sarvadākālikam eva | tathā ca āpastambaḥ: "ulkāyām agnuyutpāte ca sarvāsāṃ vidyānāṃ sārvakālikam ākālikam" iti | agnyutpāte tu manur api|

	caorair upaplute grāme saṃbhrame cāgnikārite |

	ākālikam anadhyāyaṃ vidyāt saarvādbhuteṣu ca ||

adbhuteṣu rudhirādivarṣeṣu | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "upalarudhirapāṃsuvarṣeṣv ākālikam" iti | yadā tu vidyudāditrayaṃ yugapad utpadyate tadā tryaham anadhyāyaḥ | ata eva trirātram ity anuvṛttau gautamaḥ: "varṣavidyutstaniyitnusaṃnipāte" iti | etad api varṣākālād anyatra veditavyam | yad āha āpastambaḥ: "vidyut stanayitnur vṛṣṭiś cāpartau yatra saṃnipateyus tryaham anadhyāyo yāvad bhūmir vyudakety eke | ekena dvābhyāṃ vaiteṣām ākālam" iti | bhāradvājo 'pi: 

	agnyutpāte 'partuvarṣe grāme 'nadhyayanaṃ bhavet |

	ākālikaṃ trirātraṃ tu savidyutstanayitnuke ||

yadā tu varṣāsv eva saṃdhyāyāṃ vidyutstanitaḥ tadā sajyotir anadhyāyaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	prāduṣkṛteṣv agniṣu tu vidyutstanitaniḥsvane |

	sajyotiḥ syād anadhyāyaḥ śeṣe rātrau yathā divā ||

prātaḥsaṃdhyāyāṃ nimittotpāte sajyotir yāvat sūryaḥ tāvad evānadhyayanaṃ divety arthaḥ | aparasyāṃ tu yāvan nakṣatrāṇi tāvad eva | śeṣe ṛtau yathā divānadhyāyas tathā rātrāv apīty arthaḥ | hārītas tu stanite viśeṣam āha: "sāyaṃ saṃdhyāyāṃ stanite rātrau nādhīyeran | prātaḥsaṃdhyāyāṃ stanite tv ahorātram" iti | āpastambo 'pi: "sapradoṣam ahar anadhyāyo dahre 'parararātre stanayitnunordhvam ardharātrād ity eke gavāṃ cāvarodhe" iti | dahre alpe apararātre stanayitnunā garjitena nimittena sapradoṣam ahar anadhyāya ity arthaḥ | nirghātādayas tu varṣāsv apy ākālikā ity āha manuḥ |

	nirghāte bhūmicalane jyotiṣāṃ copasarjane |

	etān ākālikān vidyād anadhyāyān ṛtāv api ||

nirghāta āntarikṣo dvaniviśeṣaḥ | jyotiṣām upasarjanaṃ candrasūryayoḥ pariveṣaḥ | āpastambas tu pariveṣādau tātkālikam anadhyāyam āha |

	saṃdhyāgarjitanirghātabhūkampolkānipātane |

	samāpya vedaṃ dyuniṣam āraṇyakam adhītya ca ||

dyuniṣam ahorātram | yatu tu yamenoktam,

	śakradhvajanipāte ca ulkāpāte tathaiva ca |

	anadhyāyas trirātraṃ tu bhūmikampe tathaiva ca ||

iti, tad ulkāyā vidyutsahabhāve draṣṭavyam | ata eva vasiṣṭhaḥ: "ulkāvidyutsamāse trirātram" iti | atra manuḥ |

	amāvāsyā guruṃ hanti śiṣyaṃ hanti caturdaśī |

	brahmāṣṭakāpaurṇamāsyau tasmāt tāḥ parivarjayet || iti | \
atra cānadhyayanam ahorātraṃ veditavyam | ata eva dyuniṣam ity anuvṛttau yājñavalkyaḥ |

	pañcadaśyāṃ caturdaśyām aṣṭamyāṃ rāhusūtake |

	ṛtusaṃdhiṣu bhuktvā ca śrāddhikaṃ pratigṛhya ca ||

rāhusūtake candrasūryoparāge | ṛtusaṃdhiṣu vasantādīnāṃ saṃdhiṣu pratipatsv ity arthaḥ | tathā rāmāyaṇe hanumadvākyam |

	sā svabhāvena tanvaṅgī tvadviyogāc ca karśitā |

	pratipatpāṭhaśīlasya vidyeva tanutāṃ gatā || iti |

hārīto pi |

	pratipatsu caturdaśyām aṣṭamyāṃ parvaṇor dvayoḥ |

	śvo 'nadhyāye 'dya śarvaryāṃ nādhīyīta kadācana ||

smṛtyantare 'pi |

	pradoṣe tu trayodaśyāṃ nādhyeyaṃ pratipatsu ca | iti |

śrāddhasaṃbandhi śrāddhikam | tad bhuktvā pratigṛhya vā dyuniṣam anadhyāya ity arthaḥ | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ 

	phalāṇy apas tilān bhakṣyān yac cānyac chrāddhikaṃ bhavet |

	pratigṛhyāpy anadhyāyāḥ pālyāḥ syur brāhmaṇaiḥ smṛtāḥ ||

etac ca ekoddiṣṭavyatiriktaviṣayam, tatra trirātravidhānāt | tathā ca manuḥ |

	pratigṛhya dvijo vidvān ekoddiṣṭasya ketanam |

	tryahaṃ na kīrtayed brahma rājño rāhoś ca sūtake ||

ketanaṃ nimantraṇam | rāhudarśane śaṅkho 'pi: "rāhudarśane śakradvajaprapatane ācārye ca pramṛte trirātram" iti | gautamas tv ākālikam āha: "ākālikā nirghātabhūkamparāhudarśanokāḥ" iti | evaṃ ca rāhudarśane trirātrākālikāhorātrāṇāṃ vikalpo veditavyaḥ | yājñavalkyo 'py ācāryamaraṇe trirātram āha |

	tryahaṃ preteṣv anadhyāyaḥ śiṣyartviggurubandhuṣu |

gurur atrācāryaḥ, na mukhyaḥ tatra daśāhavidhānāt | ata eva bāndhavā apy asapiṇḍā eva grāhyāḥ | vasiṣṭhas tu śiṣyartvigādiṣv apy ahorātram āha: "ācāryaputraśiṣyabhāryāsv ahorātram, ṛtvikṣu yonisaṃbandheṣu ca" iti | yonisaṃbandhā mātulādayaḥ | evaṃ sabrahmacāriṇy api draṣṭavyam | ata evāhorātram ity anuvṛttau gobilaḥ: 

	sabrahmacāriṇi prete sve ca bhūmipatāv api | iti |

upākarmotsarjanayos tu trirātraṃ veditavyam | ata eva tryaham anuvṛttau yājñavalkyaḥ |

	upākarmaṇi cotsarge svaśākhāśrotriye tathā | iti |

manus tūtsarjane pakṣiṇīm ekāhaṃ trirātraṃ ca vikalpenāha |

	yathāśāstraṃ tu kṛtvaivam utsarvaṃ chandasāṃ bahiḥ |

	viramet pakṣiṇīṃ rātriṃ yad vāpy ekam aharniśam ||

	upākarmaṇi cotsarge trirātraṃ kṣapaṇaṃ smṛtam | iti |

ubhayataḥ pakṣau divāhanī yasyā rātreḥ sā pakṣiṇī | eteṣāṃ pakṣiṇyādīnāṃ tattadgṛhyānusāreṇa vyavasthā | āpastambas tu upākaraṇam ārabya māsaṃ pradoṣe 'nadhyāyam āha: "śrāvaṇyāṃ paurṇmāsyām adhyāyam upākrtya māsaṃ pradoṣe nādhīyīta" iti | tatra trayodaśyādīnāṃ tu māsād upary api nādhīyīta | tathā ca purāṇam |

	medhākāmas trayodaśyāṃ saptamyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ |

	caturtyāṃ ca pradoṣeṣu na smaren na ca kīrtayet ||

atra prajāpatiḥ |

	ṣaṣṭhī ca dvādaśī caiva ardharātronanāḍikā |

	pradoṣe na tv adhīyīta tṛtīyā navanāḍikā ||

ardharātronanāḍikā ardharātrād ghaṭṛikayaikayā hīnety arthaḥ | navanāḍikā rātrāv iti śeṣaḥ | pradoṣe niśāyāḥ prathame prahare | yathāha uśanāḥ: "trayodaśyāṃ prathamāṃś caturo muhūrtān nādhīyīta" iti | dakṣo rajanyā madhyamayāmadvaye 'nadhyayanam āha |

	pradoṣapaścimau yāmau vedābhyāsena tau nayet |

	yāmadvayaṃ śayānas tu brahmabhūyāya kalpate || iti |

atra śātātapaḥ |

	pañcadaśyāṃ caturdaśyām aṣṭakāsu mahotsave |

	pradoṣe ca trayodaśyām aṣṭamyāṃ pratipady api ||

mahotsave pratiṣṭhādau | aṣṭakā api paiṭhīnasinoktāḥ: "pauṣaprabhṛtayaḥ kṛṣṇe bhavās tisro 'ṣṭakā mārgaśīrṣaprabhṛtaya ity eke" iti | puṣyeṇa yuktā paurṇamāsī pauṣī | sā yasmin māsi sa pauṣaḥ | śaunakas tu hemantaśiśirayoḥ kṛṣṇe bhavās tisro 'ṣṭakā ity āha: "hemantaśisirayoś caturṇām aparapakṣāṇām aṣṭamīṣv aṣṭakāḥ" iti | atra cānadhyayanam ahorātraṃ veditavyam | tathā ca manuḥ |

	aṣṭakāsu tv ahorātram ṛtvantāsu ca rātriṣu | iti |

gautamo 'pi: "kārtikī phālguny āṣāḍhī paurṇamāsī | tisro 'ṣṭakā trirātram" iti | uktapaurṇamāsīr ārabhya trirātram | tathaiva tisro 'ṣṭakāḥ saptamyādayas tāsv api trirātram anadhyayanam ity arthaḥ | evaṃ mahānavamyādiṣv api draṣṭavyam | tathā ca purāṇam |

	mahānavamyāṃ dvādaśyāṃ bharaṇyāṃ ca mahātithau |

	tathākṣayatṛtīyāyāṃ śiṣyān nādhyāpayed budhaḥ ||

	māghamāsasya saptamyāṃ rathākhyāyāṃ ca varjayet |

	adhyapanam athābhyaktasnānakāle ca varjayet ||

	nīyamānaṃ śavaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahīsthaṃ vā dvijottamaḥ |

	akālagarjitādau ca parasvāśaucakādiṣu (?) ||

	anadhyāyaṃ budhaḥ kuryād uparāgādike 'pi ca |

mahānavamyāśvayujaśuklanavamī | mahādvādaśī kārtikaśukladvādaśī | mahābharaṇī prauṣṭhapady anantarā | akṣayatṛtīyā vaiśākhaśuklatṛtīyā | rathākhyā mādhaśuklasaptamī | nāradīye 'pi |

	ayane viṣuve caiva śayane bodhane hareḥ |

	anadhyāyas tu kartavyo manvādiṣu yugādiṣu ||

purāṇantare 'pi |

	yugādiṣu ca sarveṣu tathā manvantarādiṣu |

	anadhyāyaṃ prakurvīta yā ca sopapadā tithiḥ ||

manvantaradayas tu matsyapurāṇe darśitāḥ |

	āśvayukchiklanavamī kārtike dvādaśī tathā |

	tṛtīyā caitramāsasya tathā bhādrapadasy ca ||

	phālyunasya tv amāvasyā puṣyasyaikādaśī tathā |

	āṣāḍhasyāpi daśamī māghamāsasya saptamī ||

	śrāvaṇasyāṣṭamī kṛṣṇā āṣāḍhasyāpi pūrṇimā |

	kārtīkī phālgunī caitrī jyaiṣṭhī pañcadaśī sitā ||

	manvantrādayas caite dattasyākṣayakārakāḥ | iti |

yugādayo 'pi viṣṇupurāṇoktā veditavyāḥ |

	vaiśākhamāsasya sitā tṛtīyā navamy asau kārtikaśuklapakṣe |

	nabhasyamāsasya ca kṛṣṇapakṣe trayodaśī pañcadaśī ca māghe || iti |

gautamas tu madhagamane 'nadhyāyam āha: "śvanakulasarpamaṇḍūkamārjārāṇāṃ tryaham upavāso vipravāsaś ca" iti | atropavāsaḥ prāyaścittam | vipravāsaḥ sahavāsābhāvaḥ | so 'pi trirātram eva, śvagomāyumārjārasarpanakulamūṣikānuvṛttau: "eteṣām evādhīyānānām antarāgamane trirātram upavāsas tryahaṃ ca vivaset" iti hārītasmaraṇāt | etenārthāt tryaham anadhyāya ity uktaṃ bhavati | vasiṣṭhas tv ahorātropavāsam āha: "śvamārjāranakulaśīghragānāṃ tv ahorātram" iti | abhojanam iti śeṣaḥ, tasyaivādhikārāt | etaṃ ca trirātrāśaktau veditavyam | mārjāragamane tu prāyaścittaviseṣam aha uśanāḥ: "mārjārāntarāgamane tu ghṛtaṃ prāśya tryaham upavaset" iti | āpastambas tu caṇḍālādivyavāye ṣaṇmāsānadhyayanam āha: "caṇḍālaśvapākaśaśakasya ṣaṇmāsān" iti | hastivyāghrayos tu saṃvatsaraṃ veditavyam | tad āha sa eva: "yadi hastī saṃvatsaram | vyāghras tathaiva ca" iti | manus tu paśvādigamane dyuniṣam anadhyāyam āha |

	paśumaṇḍūkamārjāraśvasarpanakulādibhiḥ |

	antarāgamane vidyād anadhyāyam aharniśam ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	paśumaṇḍukanakulaśvāhimārjāramūṣikaiḥ |

	kṛte 'ntare tv ahorātraṃ śakrapāte tathocchraye ||

śakrqpātocchrayopalakṣitakāla ity arthaḥ | atra śakrocchrayasya kālam āha gargaḥ |

	dvādaśyāṃ tu site pakṣe māsi prauṣṭhapade tathā |

	śakram utthāpayed rājā viśvaśravaṇavāsave || iti |

viśvaśabdena vaiśvadevam uttarāṣāḍhānakṣatram ucyate | vāsavaśabdena vasudaivatyaṃ dhaniṣṭhānakṣatram ucyate | śakrapāto 'pi tasminn eva māse | tathā ca purāṇam |

	māsi bhādrapade rājan śakrayaṣṭiprapātanam | iti |

atra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	śvakroṣṭṛgardabholūkasāmavāṇārtanisvane |

kroṣṭā sṛgālaḥ | ulūko ghūkaḥ (?) | vāṇo vīṇā, "vāṇaḥ śatatantur bhavati" it mahāvrate darśanāt | ārto duḥkhitaḥ | eteṣāṃ niḥsvane śabde śrūyamāṇe tāvatkālaṃ nadhīyīta, "etāṃs tātkālikān vidhuḥ" ity tenaivoktatvāt | manur api |

	nīhāre vāṇaśabde ca saṃdhyayor ubhayor api |

evaṃ bheryādiniḥsvane 'pi draṣṭavyam, "vānabherīmṛdaṅgagardārtaśabdeṣu" iti gautamasmaraṇāt | gardaḥ śakaṭaḥ | sāmaśabde tu ṛgyajuṣor evānadhyāyo nānyasya | tad āha manuḥ |

	sāmadhvanau ṛgyajūṃṣi nādhīyīta kadācana |

yamo 'pi |

	sāmaśabde nargyajuṣī mārute cātivāyati | iti |

tatra hetum āha manuḥ |

	ṛgvedo devadaivatyo yajurvedas tu mānuṣaḥ |

	sāmadedaḥ smṛtaḥ pitryas tasmāt tasyāśucir dhvaniḥ || iti |

evaṃ mṛdaṅgādisvane 'pi sāmnām anadhyāyaḥ, "śākhāntare ca sāmnām anadhyayaḥ" ity āpastambasmaraṇāt | evam amedhyādisaṃnidhāne 'pi draṣṭavyam | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	amedhyaśavaśūdrāntyaśmaśānapatitāntike |

antike samīpe | viṣṇur api: "na śūdrapatityoḥ samīpe na devayatanaśmaśānacatuṣpatharathyāsu nodakānte na pīṭhopanihitapādo na vānto na virikto nājīrṇaḥ" iti | manur api |

	nādhīyīta śmaśānānte grāmānte govraje 'pi vā |

	vasitvā maithunaṃ vāsaḥ śrāddhikaṃ pratigṛhya ca || iti |

ante samīpe | maithunaṃ vāsaḥ yena saha maitunam ācaritaṃ tad vāsaḥ paridhāyety arthaḥ | etad anirṇiktavāsoviṣayam | ata eva yamaḥ |

	vāsasy api hy anirṇikte maithunācarite sadā |

vasiṣṭho 'pi: "maithunavyapetāyāṃ śayyāyāṃ vāsasā ca mithunavyapetenānirṇiktena grāmāntare charditasya" iti | chardite tv ahorātram anadhyayaḥ, "charditaśrāddhamanuṣyayajñabhojaneṣv ahorātram" iti gautamasmaraṇāt | atha vā ghṛtaṃ prāśyadhīyīta | tad āha āpastambaḥ: "chardayitvā svapnāntaṃ sarpir vā prāśya" iti | svapnāntam odayād ity arthaḥ | manus tu grāme 'pi nadhīyītety āha |

	nityānadhyāya eva syād grameṣu nagareṣu ca |

	dharmanaipuṇakāmānāṃ pūtigandhe ca sarvataḥ ||

ye gṛhītavedās te dharmanaipuṇakāmāḥ | itare vidyānaipuṇakamāḥ | anena vidyānaipuṇakāmānāṃ grāmeṣv adhyayanam aviruddham ity āha | ata eva vasiṣṭhaḥ: "nagareṣu kāmaṃ gomayaparyukṣite parilikhite vā" iti | ata eva manur api |

	antargataśave grāme vṛṣalasya ca saṃnidhau |

	anadhyāyo rudyamāne samavāye janasya ca ||

vasiṣṭho 'pi: "saṃdhyāsv antaḥśavadivākīrtye" it | divākīrtyaś caṇḍālaḥ | antaḥcaṇḍāle grāme nādhīyītety arthaḥ | etac catuṣpathādiṣv api draṣṭavyam | tathā ca pracetāḥ: "catuṣpathamahāpatharathyām udyāneṣu na devasamīpe" | adhīyīteti śeṣaḥ | gautamo 'pi: "śmaśānagrāmāntamahāpathāśauceṣu" iti | śmaśāne tu viśeṣam āha āpastambaḥ: "śmaśāne sarvataḥ śamyāprāsāt grāmeṇādhyavasite kṣetreṇa vā nānadhyāyaḥ | śmaśānavac chūdrapatitau | samānāgāra ity eke | śūdrāyāṃ tu prekṣaṇapratiprekṣaṇayor evānadhyāyaḥ" iti | tathāśvārūdho 'pi nādhīyīta | tathā ca manuḥ |

	nādhīyītāśvam ārūḍho na vṛkṣaṃ ca na hastinam |

	na nāvaṃ na kharaṃ noṣṭraṃ neriṇastho na yānagaḥ ||

	śayānaḥ prauḍhapādaś ca kṛtvā caivāvasakthikām |	

	nādhīyītāmiṣaṃ jagdhvā sūtakānnādyam eva ca ||

	na vivāde na kalahe na senāyāṃ na saṅgare |

	na bhuktamātre nājīrṇe na vamitvā na sūtake || iti |

iriṇam ūṣaram | prauḍhapāda āsanādyārūḍhapādaḥ | avasakthikā jānvor madhyasya ca vastrādinā bandhanam | bhuktamātre yāvad ārdrapāṇir ity arthaḥ | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	deśe 'śucāv ātmani ca vidyutstanitasaṃplave |

	bhuktvārdrapānir ambho 'ntarardharātre 'timārute ||

saṃplavaḥ punaḥpunar udbhavaḥ | manur api |

	udake madhyarātre ca viṇmūtrasya visarjane |

	ucchiṣṭaśrāddhabhuk caiva manasāpi na cintayet ||

bodhāyano 'pi: "manasāpi jananamaraṇayor anadhyāyaḥ" iti | manus tu pāṃsuvarṣādāv api nādhyetavyam ity āha |

	pāṃsuvarṣe diśāṃ dāhe gomāyuvirute tathā |

	śvakharoṣṭre ca ruvati paṅktau ca na paṭhed dvijaḥ ||

sarvatra jyotiṣo darśanaṃ digdāhaḥ | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	pāṃsuvarṣe diśāṃ dāhe saṃdhyānīhārabhītiṣu |

	dhāvataḥ pūtigandhe ca śiṣṭe ca gṛham āgate ||

dhāvatas tvaritaṃ gacchataḥ | śiṣṭe coktalakṣaṇe gṛham āgate tadanujñāvadhir anadhyāya ity arthaḥ | tathā ca yamaḥ |

	āgataṃ cātithiṃ dṛṣṭvā nādhīyītaiva buddhimān |

	abhyanujñāpite tasminn adhyetavyaṃ pratnataḥ ||

manur api |

	atithiṃ cānujñāpya mārute vāti vā bhṛśam |

	rudhire ca srute gātrāc chastreṇa ca parikṣate ||

tathānṛtāv abbhradarsane 'py anadhyāyam aha gautamaḥ: "abbhradarśane cāpartau" | abbhraṃ jaladharo meghaḥ | evaṃ vṛkṣaviseṣacchāyāyām api draṣṭavyam | tathā ca yamaḥ |

	śleṣmāntakasya chāyāyāṃ śalmaler madhukasya ca |

	kadācid api nādhyeyaṃ kovidārakapitthayoḥ || iti |

yat punar manunoktam,

	dvāv eva varjayen nityam anadhāyau prayatnataḥ |

	svādhyayabhūmiṃ cāśuddhām ātmānaṃ cāśuciṃ dvijaḥ || iti |

tad brahmayajñādhyayanaviṣayam | tathā ca śrutiḥ: "tasya vā etasya yajñasya dvāv anadhyāyau yad ādtāśucir yad deśaḥ" iti | ata eva manuḥ |

	vedopakaraṇe caiva svādhyāye caiva naityake |

	nānurodho 'sty anadhyāye homamantreṣu caiva hi || iti |

vedopakaraṇāny aṅgāni | nityasvādhyāyo brahmayajñasaṃbandhī | śaunako 'pi |

	nitye jape ca kāmye ca kratau pārāyaṇe 'pi ca |

	nānadhyāyo 'sti vedānāṃ grahaṇe grahaṇe smṛtaḥ || iti |

evam uktānadhyāyādhyayane doṣam āha likhitaḥ |

	chidrāṇy etāni viprāṇāṃ ye 'nadhyāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |

	chidrebhyaḥ sravati brahma brāhmanena yad ārjitam ||

	tatkāle tasya rakṣāṃsi śriyaṃ brahma yaśo balam |

	sarvaṃ ādāya gacchanti varjayantīpsitaṃ phalam ||

yamo 'pi |

	āyuḥ prajñāṃ paśūn medhāṃ kṛntāmi sukrtaṃ ca yat |

	anadhyayeṣv abhyasato brahma vyāharatas tathā ||

indranāradasaṃvāde 'pi |

	anadhyāyeṣv adhīyānān kiṃ śakra na gato 'si tān |

	asurās te durātmāno brahmaghnā brahmadūṣakāḥ ||

	anadhyāyeṣv adhītaṃ hi nādhītaṃ yadi vaidikam |

	mṛtāḥ svargaṃ na gacchanti kiṃ nārada na te hatāḥ || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām anadhyāyaḥ**

**atha brahmacaryakālāvadhiḥ**

tatra āpastambaḥ: "upetasyācāryakule brahmacārivāsaḥ | aṣṭācatvāriṃśad varṣāṇi | pādūnam ardhena tribhir vā" iti | tathā ca devalaḥ: "ataḥ param aṣṭācatvāriṃśadvārṣikīṃ vedavratacaryām ātiṣṭhed aśaktaś cec caturviṃśativārṣikīṃ dvādaśavārṣikīṃ vā" iti | etad api prativedābhiprāyam | yad āha bodhāyanaḥ: "aṣṭācatvāriṃśad varṣāṇi paurāṇaṃ vedabrahmacaryaṃ caturviṃśatiṃ dvādaśa vā prativedam" iti | yamo 'pi |

	vased dvādaś varṣāṇi caturviṃśatim eva vā |

	ṣaṭtriṃṣataṃ vā varṣāṇi prativedaṃ vrataṃ caret ||

manus tu vedagrahaṇāntaṃ brahmacaryam ity āha |

	ṣaṭtriṃśadābdikaṃ caryaṃ gurau traivedikaṃ vratam |

	tadardhikaṃ pādikaṃ vā grahaṇāntikam eva vā ||

asyārthaḥ: traivedikam ṛgyajuḥsāmākhyātmakavedatrayaviṣayam | tat ṣaṭtriṃśadābdikaṃ kāryam | evaṃ ca prativedaṃ dvādaśa varṣāṇi brahmacaryavrataṃ cared ity uktaṃ bhavati | ardhikapakṣe prativedaṃ ṣaḍvarṣāṇi | pādike tu trīṇy eva | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	prativedaṃ brahmacaryaṃ dvādaśābdāni pañca vā |

	grahaṇāntikam ity eke keśāntaś caiva ṣoḍaśe ||

keśānto godānākhyaṃ karma | tat tu ṣaḍaśe varṣe kāryam ity arthaḥ | etac ca brāhmaṇaviṣayam | yad āha manuḥ |

	keśāntaḥ ṣoḍaśe varṣe brāhmaṇasya vidhīyate |

	rājanyabandhor dvāviṃśe vaiśyasya dvyadhike tataḥ || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ brahmacaryakālavadhiḥ**

**brahmacāridvaividhyam**

dvividho brahmacārī upakurvāṇo naiṣṭhikaś ca | tatropakurvānasyoktā dharmāḥ | adhunā naiṣṭhikabrahmacāriṇo dharmā ucyante | tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	naiṣṭhiko brahmacārī tu vased ācāryasaṃnidhau |

	tadabhāve 'sya tanaye patnyāṃ vaiśvānare 'pi vā ||

upakurvāṇoktavidhinātmānaṃ niṣṭhām utkrāntikālaṃ gamatīti naiṣṭhikaḥ | sa punar ācāryādisaṃnidhau vaset, na samāvartetety arthaḥ | atra ca tadabhāva iti sarvatrānuvartate | evaṃ ca patnyabhāve 'gniṃ paricared ity uktaṃ bhavati | etac ca sapiṇḍābhāvaviṣayam | yad āha manuḥ |

	ācārye tu khalu prete guruputre guṇānvite |

	gurudāre sapiṇḍe vā guruvad vrttim ācaret ||

	eteṣv avidyamāneṣu sthānāsanavihāravān |

	prayuñjāno 'gniśuśrūṣāṃ sādhayed deham ātmanaḥ ||

sthānāsanavihāravān kālaviśeṣāśrayaṇena utthānopaveśagamanavān ity arthaḥ | etad apy anūcānabrāhmaṇagurvādiviṣayam anyathā doṣaśravaṇāt | tad āha sa eva |

	nābrāhmaṇe gurau śiṣyo vāsam ātyantikaṃ vaset |

	brāhmaṇe vānanūcāne kāṅkṣan gatim anuttamām || iti |

tatra vasato ye dharmās tān āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	upakurvāṇakasyaitat samādiṣṭaṃ mayā vratam |

	adhunā saṃpravakṣyāmi naiṣṭhikasya samāsataḥ ||

	saṃdhyāgnikāryaṃ svādhyāyo bhikṣādhaḥśayanaṃ dayā |

	ā mṛtyor naiṣṭhikaṃ kurvan brahmalokam avāpnuyāt || iti |

vasiṣṭho 'pi: "saṃyatavāk caturthaṣaṣṭhāṣṭakalabhojī bhaikṣam ācaret gurvadhīno jaṭilaḥ śikhājaṭo vā guruṃ gacchan tam anugacchan āsīnaṃ cet tiṣṭhan śayānaṃ ced āsīna upāsīta | āhūtādhyāyī sarvaṃ labdhaṃ nivedya tadanujñayā bhuñjīta | khaṭvāśayanadantaprakṣālanāñjanābhyañjanopānacchatravarjī tiṣṭhed ahani rātrāv āsīta | trir aho 'bhyupeyād apaḥ" iti | ahani trir apo 'bhyupeyāt triṣavaṇasnāyī syād ity arthaḥ | devalo 'pi: "brahmasūtrākṣamālādaṇḍakāṣṭhakuṇḍikāmauñjīmekhalādhāraṇaṃ sakṛdbhojanam asakṛdavagāhanam ubhayakālam agnihotraṃ saṃdhyopāsanam aluptalomakesanakhatvaggandhamālyasnehāñjanābhyañjanaveṣālaṃkāracchatropānadvāhana-laṅghanaplavanadhāvanacikitsājyautiṣalakṣaṇavāstuvidyāmaṅgalapauṣṭikaśāntikarmagāndharva-saṅghasamayabandhanaśilpalekhanakārukarmaveśmakṣetradravyadhanadhānyaparicchadavastra-dyūtavyavahārajñabhāvalīlāparihāsapraṇayakuhakavismāpanavidambanavivādotsekaparivedana-rodanapādodvartanavarjanam" iti | hārītas tv agniparicaryāvidhim āha: "yajñiyāḥ samidha āhṛtya saṃmārjanopalepanodbodhanasamūhanasamindhanaparyagnikaraṇaparikramopasthānahoma-stotranamaskārādibhir agniṃ paricaren nāgnim adhitiṣṭhen na padbhyāṃ karṣen na mukhenopadhamet | nāpaś cāgniṃ ca yugapad dhārayet | nājīrṇabhuṅ nārthibho dadyān nendhanebhyo dadhad atikrāmen na niṣṭhīved vividhacaruhavirdhānaviśeṣair āgneyair ahar ahar agnim indhetāmantrya gacched āhṛtya nivedayet" iti | evaṃ kurvataḥ phalam āha manuḥ |

	ā samāpteḥ śarīrasya yas tu śusrūṣate gurum |

	sa gacchaty añjasā vipro brahmaṇaḥ sadma śāśvatam ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	anena vidhinā dehaṃ sādhayan vijitendriyaḥ |

	brahmalokam avāpnoti na cehājāyate punaḥ ||

yamo 'pi |

	ā nipātāc charīrasya ye caranty ūrdhvaretasaḥ |

	te yānti brahmaṇaḥ sthānaṃ jāyante na punar bhuvi ||

yat tu hārītenoktam, 

	bhṛtyoḥ parastād amṛtā bhavanti ye brāhmaṇā brahmacaryaṃ caranti |

iti, tad brahmavinnaiṣṭhikaviṣayam, "sarve te puṇyalokā bhavanti brahmasaṃstho 'mṛtatvam eti" it śruteḥ | sarva ete catvāra āśramiṇaḥ karma kurvāṇāḥ puṇyalokā bhavanti | yaḥ punar eṣāṃ madhye brahmasaṃstho brahmaniṣṭhaḥ so 'mṛtatvam apunarāvṛttilakṣaṇaṃ phalam eti | etac ca naiṣṭhikatvaṃ kubjādīnāṃ nityam ity āha viṣṇuḥ |

	kubjavāmanajātyandhaklībapaṅgvārtarogiṇām |

	vratavaryā bhavet teṣāṃ yavajjīvam anaṃśataḥ ||

anaṃśataḥ aṃśābhāvād ityarthaḥ | saṃgrahakāro 'pi |

	paṅgvādīnām anaṃśatvād asamarthyāc ca śāstrataḥ |

	niyataṃ naiṣṭhikatvaṃ syāt karmasv anadhikārataḥ || iti |

nanv evaṃ tarhi kubjādīnām eva naiṣṭhikatvam astu netareṣām | maivam,

	yadi tv ātyantikaṃ vāsaṃ rocayet guroḥ kule |

	yuktaḥ paricared enam ā śarīravimokṣaṇāt ||

iti pākṣikatvapratipādakamanuvacanavirodhāt | na hi kubjādīnāṃ pākṣikaṃ naiṣṭhikatvam asti | nanu ca yadītareṣām api naiṣṭhikatvam asti, tarhi "yāvajjīvam agnihotraṃ juhuyāt" iti gṛhasthadharmavidhāyikā śrutir bādhyeta | maivam, naiṣṭhikatvasya pākṣikatvena viṣayāntarasaṃbhavāt, ye hi strīrāgavaśād gārhasthyam eva kamayante tadviṣayeyaṃ yavajjīvikā śrutir ity avirodhaḥ | tathā ca jābāliḥ: "gṛhī vanaṃ praviśet | yadi gṛham eva kāmayeta tadā yāvajjīvam agnihotraṃ juhuyāt" iti | yuktaṃ caitat, anyathā "yam icchet tam āviśed yadi vetarathā brahmacaryād eva pravrajet" ityādayo bādhyeran | nanu ca smārtanaiṣṭhikatvasya śrautāgnihotrādinā bādha evāstu | maivam, tasyāpi "brahmacāry ācāryakulavāsī dvitīyo 'tyantam ātmānam ācāryakule 'vasādayet" ity etacchrutimūlatvenāviśeṣāt | ato na brahmacāridvaividhyam apahātuṃ śakyam | uktaṃ ca hārītena: "dvividho brahmacārī upakurvāṇō naiṣṭhikas ca" iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> brahmacāridvaividhye catvāra āśramā ity āpastambādivacanaṃ bādhyeta | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, saṃkalpabhedamātreṇa nityakāmyāgnihotravad anayor abhedopapatteḥ | ata eva dakṣaḥ |

	dvitīyo naiṣṭhikaś caiva tasminn evāśrame sthitaḥ | iti |

tasminn evāśrame iti vadan taddharmātideśam āha | ata eva gautamaḥ: "tatroktaṃ brahmacāriṇaḥ" iti | tatropakurvāṇaprakaraṇe yad uktam agnīndhanabhaikṣacaryādikaṃ tan naiṣṭhikasyāpi bhavatīty arthaḥ |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ brahmacāriprakaraṇam**

**athāśramasamuccayavikalpau**

tatra samuccayaṃ prakṛtyāha manuḥ |

	brahmacārī gṛhasthaś ca vānaprastho yatis tathā |

	ete gṛhasthaprabhavāś catvāraḥ pṛthag āśramāḥ ||

	sarve 'pi kramaśas tv ete yathāśāstraṃ niṣevitāḥ |

	yathoktakāriṇaṃ vipraṃ nayanti paramāṃ gatim ||

gṛhasthaprabhavās tadupajīvina ity arthaḥ | kramaśa ity anenāśramaprātilomyaṃ pratiṣiddham ity āha | ata eva dakṣaḥ |

	trayāṇām ānulomyaṃ syāt prātilomyaṃ na vidyate |

	prātilomyena yo jāti na tasmāt pāpakṛttamaḥ || iti |

ata eva mṛtabhāryeṇa punar vivāhāsāmarthye na brahmacāriṇā bhavitavyam ity āha sa eva |

	yo gṛhāśramam āsthāya brahmacārī bhavet punaḥ |

	na yatir na vanasthaś ca sa sarvāśramavarjitaḥ || iti |

āpastambo 'pi samuccayam evāha: "catvāra āśramāḥ gārhastyam ācāryakulaṃ maunaṃ vānaprasthyam iti | teṣu sarveṣu yathopadeśam avyagro vartamānaḥ kṣemaṃ gacchati" iti | purāṇe 'pi |

	brahmacārī gṛhasthaś ca vānaprasthaś ca bhikṣukaḥ |

	apramatto bhavān yena mā gāḥ (?) putra kuvartvamā ||

jābāliśrutis tu caturṇāṃ trayāṇāṃ dvayor vā samuccayam āha: "brahmacaryaṃ parisamāpya gṛhī bhavet | gṛhī bhūtvā vanī bhavet | vanī bhūtvā pravrajet | yadi vetarathā brahmacaryād eva pravrajet | gṛhād vā vanād vā" | manus tu sakalasamuccaye kālavyavasthām āha |

	caturtham āyuṣo bhāgam uṣitvādyaṃ gurau dvijaḥ |

	dvitīyam āyuṣo bhāgaṃ kṛtadāro gṛhe vaset ||

	vaneṣu tu vihṛtyaivaṃ tṛtīyaṃ bhāgam āyuṣaḥ |

	caturtham āyuṣo bhāgaṃ tyaktvā saṅgān parivrajet ||

"śatāyur vai puruṣaḥ" iti śrutyabhihitāyuścaturtho bhāgaḥ pañcaviṃśativarṣāṇīty arthaḥ | evaṃ kurvataḥ phalam āha hārītaḥ |

	anena vidhinā yo hi āśramān upasevate |

	sa sarvalokān nirjitya brahmalokāya kalpate || iti |

yat tu gautamenoktam, "aikāśramyaṃ tv ācaryāḥ pratyakṣavidhānād gārhasthyasya" iti, tad gārhasthyasya śraiṣṭhyapratipādanaparam, itareṣām api, "brahmacaryaṃ parisamāpya gṛhī bhavet | gṛhī bhūtvā vanī bhavet | vanī bhūtvā pravrajet," "aṣṭame varṣe brāhmaṇam upanayīta," ityādipratyakṣaśrutivihitatvenāviśeṣāt | ata eva vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	gṛhastha eva yajate gṛhasthas tapyate tapaḥ |

	caturṇām āśramāṇāṃ ca gṛhasthaś ca viśiṣyate ||

manur api |

	sarveṣām api caiteṣāṃ vedasmṛtividhānataḥ |

	gṛhastha ucyate śreṣṭhaḥ sa trīn etān bibharti hi ||

	yathā nadīnadāḥ sarve sāgare yānti saṃsthitim |

	tathaivāśramiṇaḥ sarve gṛhasthe yānti saṃsthitim ||

vasiṣṭhas tu caturṇām āśramāṇāṃ vikalpam āha: "catvāra āśramā brahmacārigṛhasthavānaprathaparivrājakāḥ | teṣāṃ vedam adhītya vedau vā vedān vā 'viśīrṇabrahmacaryo yam icchet tam āvaset" iti | vedaṃ vedau vedān veti phalabhūyastvābhiprāyam | vedam adhītyāviplutabrahmacaryas teṣām āśramāṇāṃ madhye yam icchet tam āvaset āśrayet tatraiva niṣṭhāṃ yāyād ity arthaḥ | bhaviṣyatpurāṇe 'pi |

	gārhasthyam icchan bhūpāla kuryād dāraparigraham |

	brahmacaryeṇa vā kālaṃ nayet saṃkalpapūrvakam ||

	vaikhānaso vāpi bhavet parivrāḍ atha vecchayā|

gautamo 'pi: "tasyāśramavikalpam eke bruvate" iti | uśanasāpy uktam |

	ācāryeṇābhyanujñātaś caturṇām ekam āśramam |

	ā vimokṣāc charīrasya so 'nutiṣṭhed yathāvidhi || iti |
