evaṃ ca yasya samuccayānuṣṭhānasāmarthyaṃ nāsti tasyāyaṃ vikalpa ity mantavyam | ā vimokṣād anutiṣṭhed ity anena āśraminā sthātavyam ity āha | ata eva dakṣaḥ |

	anāśramī na tiṣṭheta dinam ekam api dvijaḥ |

	āśrameṇa vinā tiṣṭhan prāyaścittī yato hi saḥ ||

	jape home tathā dāne svādhyāye vā rataḥ sadā |

	nāsau phalam avāpnoti kurvāṇo 'py āśramāc cyutaḥ ||

hārīto 'pi |

	anāśramī vyapetaś ca āśramī ca nirarthakaḥ |

	mithyāśramī ca sarve vai nirayaṃ yānti mānavāḥ || iti |

etac cāśramacatuṣṭayaṃ brāhmaṇādivarṇatrasya veditavyam | ata eva kalpānāṃ sūtrakāraḥ: "trayāṇāṃ varṇānāṃ catvāra āśramāḥ" iti | evaṃ ca yad uktaṃ manunā,

	eṣa vo 'bhihito dharmo brāhmaṇasya caturvidhaḥ |

iti, tad dvijātyupalakṣaṇārtham iti mantavyam |

**iti smṛticandrikāyām āśramanirṇayaḥ**

**atha samāvartanam**

tatra dakṣaḥ |

	svīkaroti yadā vedaṃ cared vedavratāni ca |

	brahmacārī bhavet tāvad ūrdhvaṃ snāto gṛhī bhavet ||

vratāni brahmacaryam | vedasvīkaraṇaṃ vedārthavicārasyāpi pradarśanārtham | ata eva smṛtyantaraṃ: "vedam adhītya chandoviṣayān arthān budhvā snāyāt" iti | laghuvyāso 'pi |

	ṛkpādam apy adhītyāto nyāyatas tu tadarthavit |

	samyag vratāni saṃsevya samāvartanam arhati || iti |

nyāyato gurumukhāvekṣaṇādyuktanyayenety arthaḥ | etac ca samuccayasaṃpadanasamarthaviṣayam | atha vā vratamātrasamāptāv api snānaṃ bhavaty eva | tad āha yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	gurave tu varaṃ datvā snāyād vā tadanujñayā |

	vedaṃ vratāni vā pāraṃ nītvā hy ubhayam eva vā ||

pūrvoktanyāyena vedaṃ vratāny ubhayaṃ vā pāraṃ nītvā samāpya gurave varam abhilaṣitaṃ datvā samāvartetety arthaḥ | etena snātakatraividhyaṃ pratipaditaṃ bhavati | yad āha hārīta: "trayaḥ snātakā bhavanti vidyāsnātako vratasnātako vidyāvratasnātakaś ca" iti | yaḥ samāpya vedam asamāpya vratāni samāvartate sa vidyāsnātakaḥ | yas tu samāpya vratāny asamāpya vedaṃ sa vratasnātakaḥ | yaḥ punar ubhayaṃ samāpya snāti sa vidyāvratasnātaka iti | evaṃ ca vratasnātakasy pariṇayanottarakālam adhyayanasamāpanaṃ tadarthajñānaṃ ceti mantavyam | yat tu,

	guruśuśrūṣayā vidyāṃ saṃprāpya vidhivad dvijaḥ |

	snāyīta gurvanujñāto datvāsmai dakṣiṇā hi gām ||

ity vyāsena godānam uktam, tad api prītisādhanadravyopalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva manuḥ |

	kṣetraṃ hiraṇyaṃ gām aśvaṃ chatropānaham antataḥ |

	dhānyaṃ vāsāṃsi śākaṃ vā gurave prītim āharet ||

anena sati saṃbhave prakṛṣṭam eva deyam ity uktaṃ bhavati | ata eva laghuhārītaḥ |

	ekam apy akṣaraṃ yas tu guruḥ śiṣye nivedayet |

	prthivyāṃ nāsti tad dravyaṃ yad datvā tv anṛṇī bhavet ||

etac ca dakṣiṇādānam āśramāntarapraveśe 'pi veditavyam | tathā ca nṛsiṃhapurāṇam |

	gurave dakṣiṇāṃ datvā sa yam icchet tad āvaset | iti 

yasya punar dakṣiṇādānasāmarthyaṃ nāsti tasya tadanujñāyāṃ snānam | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "vidyānte gurur arthena nimantryaḥ | krtvānujñātasya vā snānam" iti | vidyānte gurum arthena hetunā nimantrya praṣṭavyam "ko 'rthas tubhyaṃ mayā dātavyaḥ" iti | tam artham ācāryāya datvā snāyāt | aśaktas tadanujñayā vety arthaḥ | "vidyānte dadyāt" ity anena pūrvaṃ niṣedham āha | ata eva manuḥ |

	na pūrvaṃ gurave kiṃcid upakurvīta dharmavit |

	snāsyaṃs tu guruṇājñaptaḥ śaktyā gurvartham āharet ||

etad api bhṛtipradānābhiprāyam, itarasyāniṣedhāt | ata eva yamaḥ |

	yato dharmāgamo na syān na śuśrūṣādhanāgamau |

	vidyayā saha martavyaṃ na vidyām ūṣare vapet || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ samāvartanam **

**vivāhaḥ**

uktā gurukulā nivṛttir upakurvāṇasya | tasyedānīṃ vivāha ucyate | tatra manuḥ |

	guruṇā samanujñātaḥ samāvṛtto yathāvidhi |

	udvaheta dvijo bhāryāṃ savarṇāṃ lakṣaṇānvitām (?) ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	aviplutabrahmacaryo lakṣaṇyāṃ striyam udvahet |

viplutiḥ skhalanam | lakṣaṇyā lakṣaṇayuktā | sā ca kiṃlakṣaṇā bhavatīty ukte sa evāha |

	ananyapūrvikāṃ kāntām asapiṇḍāṃ yavīyasīm |

	arogiṇīṃ bhrātṛmatīm asamānārṣagotrajām ||

ananyapūrvikā yā dānenopabhogena vā puruṣāntarapūrvikā na bhavati sā | kāntā kamanīyā pariṇetur manasaḥ ānandakāriṇīty arthaḥ | āpastambo 'pi: "yasyāṃ manaścakṣuṣor nībandhas tasyām ṛddhiḥ" iti | samāna ekaḥ piṇḍo yasyāḥ sā sapiṇḍā | na sapiṇḍā asapiṇḍā | ekapiṇḍatā caikasyāṃ piṇḍadānakriyāyāṃ dātṛtvena devatātvena lepabhāktvena vānupraveśād bhavati | tathā ca matsyapurāṇam |

	lepabhājaś caturthādyāḥ pitrādyāḥ piṇḍabhājinaḥ |

	piṇḍadaḥ saptamas teṣāṃ sāpiṇḍyaṃ sāptapūruṣam ||

caturthādyāḥ prapitāmasya pitṛprabhṛtayaḥ uttare trayo lepabhājo bhavanti pitrādyās tu trayaḥ piṇḍabhāginaḥ piṇḍadāne devatābhūtāḥ teṣāṃ saptamaḥ piṇḍadātā | evam ete sapta sapiṇḍā bhavanti | ekapiṇḍadānakriyānupraveśinaḥ sapiṇḍā ity arthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> yady ekapiṇḍakriyānupraveśāt sāpiṇḍyaṃ tarhi bhrātṝṇāṃ bhinnkriyānupraveśināṃ tadadbhāvenanyonyaṃ sāpiṇḍyaṃ na syāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, ekoddeśyāvacchedenaikakriyānvayitvasaṃbhavāt | ye hi putraniṣpādyakriyanupraveśinaḥ pitrādayas ta eva putrāntarotpādyakriyāyām apīti vyaktam ekoddeśānvayitvam | ata eva pitāmahādeḥ santatijātānāṃ putreṇa saha sāpiṇḍyasiddhiḥ | putrakriyānvayinaḥ pitāmahādes tatkriyāsaṃbandhāt | yadā tv ekasyāpi pitāmahādes tatkriyāsaṃbandho nāsti tad etad deśyabhedena kriyābhedāt sāpiṇḍyanivṛttiḥ | tad āha manuḥ |

	sapiṇḍatā tu puruṣe saptame vinivartate | iti  \
gautamo 'pi: "piṇḍanivṛttiḥ saptame pañcame vā" iti | bhāryāyāś ca sahakartṛtvāt sāpiṇḍyasiddhiḥ | evaṃ sarvatra sāpiṇḍyanivṛttyanuvṛttī draṣṭavye | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nunv</span> evaṃ tarhi putradauhitrayor ekapiṇḍakriyānupraveśinoḥ sāpiṇḍyaṃ prasajyeta | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>, yad asau dauhitraḥ putreṇa saha samānagotraḥ syāt atraikagotratvam upādhir iti bhāvaḥ | ata eva putrīkaraṇādāv asti dauhitrasyāpi putreṇa saha sāpiṇḍyam iti vakṣyāmaḥ | tena nātiprasaktiḥ | yavīyasī janmataḥ pramāṇataś ca | arogiṇī adīrgharogā itarasya śakyaparihāratvāt | bhrātṛmatī putrikākaraṇabhayāt | yad āha manuḥ |

	yasyās tu na bhaved bhrātā na vijñāyeta vā pitā |

	nopayaccheta tāṃ prājñaḥ putrikādharmaśaṅkayā ||

yasyā**patā putrikākaraṇābhiprāyavān na veti na vijñāyetety arthaḥ | anena vinā putreṇa saha saṃpratipattiṃ pituḥ saṃkalpamātrāt putrikā bhavatīti gamyate | ata eva gautamaḥ: "abhisaṃdhimātraputrikety ekeṣām" iti | sā ca kathaṃ putrikā bhavatīty apekṣite manur āha |

	aputro 'nena vidhinā sutāṃ kurvīta putrikām |

	yad apatyaṃ bhaved asyāṃ tan mama syāt svadhākaram || iti |

vasiṣṭho 'pi |

	abhrātṛkāṃ pradāsyāmi tubhyaṃ kanyām alaṃkṛtām |

	asyāṃ yo jāyate putraḥ sa me putro bhaved iti ||

iyam eva putra iti vā putrikākaraṇam, "śāsad vahnir duhitur naptyaṃ gāt" iti śruteḥ | etac ca nirukte vyākhyātam "praśāsti voḍhā santānakarmaṇe duhituḥ putrabhāvam" iti | asamānārṣagotrajām, samānam ārṣaṃ pravaro yasya sa samānārṣaḥ | tasmāj jātāṃ samānarṣijātāṃ nodvahed ity arthaḥ | ata eva gautamaḥ: "asamānapravarair vivāhaḥ" iti | samānatā ca nāmato veditavyā | yad āha bodhāyanaḥ |

	eka eva ṛṣir yāvat pravareṣv anuvartate |

	tāvat samānagotratvam anyatra bhṛgvaṅgirogaṇāt || iti |

samānagotratvaṃ samānapravara ity arthaḥ | kathaṃ tarhi bhṛgvaṅgirogaṇeṣv ity apekṣite saṃgrahakāra āha |

	pañcānāṃ triṣu sāmāmānyād avivāhas triṣu dvayoḥ |

	bhṛgvaṅgirogaṇeṣv eva śeṣeṣv ekaṃ nivārayet ||

pañcārṣeyāṇām ṛṣitrayānuvṛttau mitho na vivāha ity arthaḥ | bodhāyano 'pi: "dvyārṣeyasaṃnipāte 'vivāhas tryārṣeyāṇṃ tryārṣeyasaṃnipāte 'vivāhaḥ pañcāryeyāṇām" iti | gotraṃ ca vaṃśaparamparāprasiddham | gotrapravarau ca pṛthag pṛthak paryudāse nimittam | tatra yāskavādhaulamānamaukānāṃ (?) gotrabhedena vivāhe prāpte tan mā bhūd ity asamānārṣagrahaṇam | teṣāṃ bhārgavavaitahavyasādevaseti  pravaraikāyat | yatra tu pravaravikalpaḥ tatrāpi pravarabhedena vivāhaprāptau tatpratixedhārtham asānagotragrahaṇam | evaṃ cāsamānārṣajām asamānagotrajām udvahed ity uktaṃ bhavati | na ca samānārṣagrahaṇaṃ gotraviśeṣaṇam iti śaṅkanīyam,

	pariṇīya sagotrāṃ tu samānapravarāṃ tathā|

	tyāgaṃ kṛtvā tatas tasyā dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret ||

iti bhedena smaraṇāt | tyāgaś cātropabhogasyaiva na punas tasyāḥ | yad āha śātātapaḥ |

	samānapravarāṃ kanyām ekagotrām athāpi vā |

	vivāhayati yo mūḍhas tasya vakṣyāmi niṣkṛtim ||

	utsṛjya tāṃ tathā bhāryāṃ mātṛvat paripālayet ||

yas tu tatra prajām utpadayati sa svajātyadinā hīyata ity āha āpastambaḥ |

	samānagotrapravarāṃ kanyām ūḍhvopagamya ca |

	tasyām utpādya caṇḍālaṃ brāhmaṇyād eva hīyate || iti |

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> cāsamānārṣagotrajām ity anenaiva pariṇetuḥ sapiṇḍāyāḥ paryudāse siddhe kim iti punar asapiṇḍām ity uktam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span>, satyam evam | tathāpi jā mātur asapiṇḍā bhavati saivodvāhakarmaṇi praśasteti vaktum | tathā ca manuḥ |

	asapiṇḍā ca yā matur asagotrā ca yā pituḥ |

	sā praśastā dvijātīnāṃ dārakarmaṇi maithune ||

yā pariṇetur mātuś ca sapiṇḍā na bhavati yā pariṇetuḥ pituś ca na sagotrā sā ca vivāhakarmaṇi praśastety arthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca mātā dānasamakālam eva pitṛsāpiṇḍyaṃ tadgotraṃ ca hitvā patisāpiṇḍyaṃ tadgotraṃ ca pratipadyate | tat katham "asapiṇḍā ca yā mātuḥ" iti | tad uktam |

	ekatvaṃ sā gatā bhartuḥ piṇḍe gotre ca sūtake | iti |

patisapiṇḍair eva patnyāḥ sāpiṇḍyaṃ na svapitrādibhir ity abhiprāyaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | nāsti mātuḥ svapitrādibiḥ saha sāpiṇḍyaṃ yadi tasyās tyāgapūrvako vivāhaḥ syāt | tyāge hi svatvanivṛttivatsāpiṇḍyasagotratvayor api nivṛttiḥ | anenaivābhiprāyeṇoktam |

	ekatvaṃ sā gatā bhartuḥ piṇḍe gotre ca sūtake | iti |

ata eva dattaputrādes tyāgenaiva pitṛgorādinivṛttiḥ siddhā | anyathā "asagotrā ca yā pituḥ" ity atra pitṛgrahaṇam anarthakṃ syāt | uktā ca gotrādinivṛttir manunā |

	gotrarikthe janayitur na hard dattimaḥ sutaḥ |

	gotrarikthānugaḥ piṇḍo vyapaiti dadataḥ svadhā || iti |

evaṃ ca putrikāyā vivāho naiva pradānapūrvaka iti na tatra sāpiṇḍyasagotratvayor nivṛttiḥ (?) | ata eva vasiṣṭho 'py aprattānām tripūruṣaṃ sāpiṇḍyam āha: "aprattānāṃ strīṇāṃ tripūruṣaṃ sāpiṇḍyam" iti | na ca putrikāvivāhe 'pi tasyāḥ pradānam astīti śaṅkānīyam (?) | pradāne tu gotrādinivṛttivat putrikātvasyāpi nivṛttis tannivṛttau ca tatkāryakartṛtvaṃ na syāt | śrūyate ca tasyāḥ putrakāryakaratvam: "abhrāteva puṃsa eti pratīcī" iti | etad api nirukte vyākhyātam: "abhrātṛkeva puṃsaḥ pitṝn ety abhimukhī santānakarmaṇi piṇḍadānāya nayati" iti | ataś ca putrikāyāḥ pradānābhāvena svapitṛsāpiṇḍyaṃ sagotratvaṃ ca siddham | ata eva logākṣiḥ: 

	mātāmahasya gotreṇa mātuḥ piṇḍodakakriyāṃ | 

	kurvīta putrikāputra evam āha prajāpatiḥ ||

evam āsurādivivāheṣv api sagotratvāder anivṛttiḥ, tatrāpi pradānābhāvāt | ata eva mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	brāhmādiṣu vivāheṣu yā tūḍhā kanyakā bhavet |

	bhartṛgotreṇa kartavyās tasyāḥ piṇḍodakakriyāḥ ||

	āsurādivivāheṣu pitṛgotreṇa dharmataḥ |

mātuḥ pitṛgotreṇety arthaḥ | evaṃ ca putrikākaraṇādau mātuḥ svapitrādisāpiṇḍyasadbhāvād yuktam uktam: (?) "asapiṇḍā ca yā mātuḥ" iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca putrasyāpi mātṛsapiṇḍatvādyā mātuḥ sapiṇḍā sā putrasyāpīti kim arthaṃ mātṛgrahaṇam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | yadā tu putrikāsutasyaiva mātṛmātāmahābhyāṃ parityāgaḥ tadā tatsāpiṇḍyanivṛttyā tatsapiṇḍāyā vivāhaprāptau tan mā bhūd ity mātṛgrahaṇam | evaṃ dattaputrādes tyāgenaiva pitṛgotranivṛttyā tatsagotrāyā vivāhaprāptau tan mā prasāṃkṣīd iti | pitṛgrahaṇam iti sarvam anavadyam | mātṛsagotrām api kecin necchanti | tad āha vyāsaḥ |

	sagotrāṃ mātur apy eke necchanty udvāhakarmaṇi |

etad api putrikākaraṇāviṣayaṃ mātuḥ patigotratvena gotrāntarābhāvāt | na ca bhūtapūrvagatyā mātṛsagotrāpratiṣedha iti vācyam, vartamāne saṃbhavati bhūtapūrvagatyāśrayaṇasyānyāyyatvāt | evaṃ ca yā pariṇetur mātuś ca na sapiṇḍā bhavati yā ca pariṇetuḥ pituś cāsagotrā sā vivāhyeti siddham | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> evaṃ tarhi brāhmādibhivivāhair nivṛttapitṛsapiṇḍabhāvāyāṃ putrasya mātulasutā pariṣeyā syāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>, kena coktaṃ na pariṇeyeti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> manvādibhir eva | yad āha śātātapaḥ |

	udvaheta sagotrāṃ yas tanayāṃ mātulasya ca |

	ṛṣibhiś caiva tulyāṃ ca sa tu cāndrāyaṇam caret ||

manur api |

	paitṛṣvaseyīṃ bhaginīṃ svasrīyāṃ mātur eva ca |

	mātuś ca bhrātur aptasya gatvā cāndrāyāṇaṃ caret ||

	etās tisras tu bhāryārthe nopayaccheta buddhimān |

	jñātitvenānupeyās tāḥ patati hy upayann adhaḥ | iti |

āptasya saṃnikṛṣṭasya sapiṇḍasyety arthaḥ | vyāso 'pi |

	tṛtīyāṃ mātṛtaḥ kanyāṃ tṛtīyāṃ pitṛtas tathā |

	śulkena codvahiṣyanti viprāḥ pāpavimohitāḥ ||

mātṛto mātṛpakṣe tṛtīyāṃ mātulasutām, pitṛpakṣe trtīyāṃ paitṛṣvaseyīm ity arthaḥ | śulkaṃ mūlyam | anena kūṭstham ārabhya gaṇayed ity uktaṃ bhavati | tathā ca purāṇe yayātivākyam |

	yo me tvaṃ hṛdayāj jāto vayas tvaṃ na prayachasi |

	pāpān mātulasaṃbandhat prajā vai te bhaviṣyati ||

sumantur api: "pitṛpatnyaḥ sarvā mātaraḥ, tadbhrātaro mātulāḥ, tadduhitaraś ca bhaginyaḥ, tadaptyāni bhāgineyāni, anyathā saṃkarakārīṇi syuḥ" iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | satyam etāni mātuladuhitṛvivāhaniṣedhaparāṇi | tathāpy āsurādivivāhena pitrādibhir anivṛttasapiṇḍabhāvāyāḥ putrasya mātulasutā pariṇetur mātuś ca sapiṇḍeti sā tāvad avivāhyā | tathaivaṃvidhāyāḥ pitṛṣvasur duhitā pariṇetuḥ pituś ca sapiṇḍā sagotrā ceti sāpi na pariṇeyā | yā tu brāhmādivivāhoḍhā tasyāḥ svapitrādibhiḥ sāpiṇḍyanivṛttes tatputrasya mātulasuāpariṇayaṇaṃ na vāryate | evaṃ paitṛṣvaseyyām api draṣṭavyam | tad idam uktaṃ manunā |

	asapiṇḍā ca yā mātur asagotrā ca yā pituḥ |

	sā praśastā dvijātīnāṃ dārakarmaṇi maithune || iti |

yā mātṛtaḥ pitṛto vā sapiṇḍā sagotrā ca saiva parityājyā nānyety abhiprāyaḥ | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	mātuḥ sapiṇḍā yatnena varjanīyā dvijātibhiḥ | iti |

ata eva śātātapo 'pi mātṛsagorāyā eva niṣedham āha |

	mātulasya sutām ūḍhvā mātṛgotrāṃ tathaiva ca |

	samānapravarāṃ caiva dvijaś cāndrāyaṇam caret ||

na cātra mātṛgorām ity anenaiva sapiṇḍamātuladuhitṛniṣedhasiddheḥ kim arthaṃ mātulasutāgrahaṇam iti vācyam, pakṣāntaratve 'pi samānatvāt | tatrāpi mātṛgotrādipratiṣedhenaiva mātuladuhitṛmātraniṣedhasiddheḥ | atha pakṣadvayenobhayavidhamātuladuhitṛniṣedhaḥ, tarhi mātulasutāgrahaṇenaivālam, kiṃ mātṛgoragrahaṇena | kiṃ ca manur api paitṛṣvaseyyāḥ pitṛsapiṇḍāyā eva paryudāsam āha |

	patiṛṣvaseyīṃ bhaginīṃ svastrīyāṃ mātur eva ca |

	mātuś ca bhrātur āptasya gatvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret ||

	etās tisras tu bhāryārthe nopayaccheta buddhimān | iti |

anyathā bhaginīśabdavaiyarthaṃ syāt, paitṛṣvasehīm ity anenaiva pitṛṣvasṛduhitṛmātraniṣedhasiddheḥ | bhaginīvad bhaginī sapiṇḍety arthaḥ | evam āptaśabde 'pi draṣṭavyam | na ca bhaginīśabdaḥ paitṛṣvaseyīṃ na viśinaṣṭīti vācyam,

	etās tisras tu bhāryārthe nopayaccheta buddhimān |

iti tritve saṅkhyāpanāt | patiṭhinasir api: "pitṛmātṛṣvasṛduhitaro mātulasutā dharmatas tā bhaginyo vajayet" iti | na cātra saṃdehanivṛttyarthaṃ bhaginīgrahaṇam iti vācyam, "varjayet" ityadividhibalenaiva saṃdehanivṛtteḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca "asapiṇḍā ca yā mātuḥ" ity anenaiva mātṛsapiṇḍādiparyudāse siddhe kim iti punaḥ "paitṛṣvaseyīṃ bhaginīm" it tasyā eva niṣedha <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | satyam evam | tathāpy atra pātityādidoṣapratipadanamukhenaikāntato nivṛttisiddhyartham | "sā praśastā" iti vacanān mātṛsapiṇḍāsagotrayor aprāśastyamātram syāt | na sarvathā varjanīyatvan, tathā,

	caturo brāhmaṇasyādyān praśastān kavayo viduḥ |

iti caturṇāṃ vivāhānāṃ prāśastya ukte 'pi na gāndharvādīnām ekāntataḥ parityāgaḥ kiṃ tv aprāśastyamātraṃ tathehāpi syāt | tataś ca yā manvādivacanair mātṛsapiṇḍā mātulasutā yā ca paitṛṣvaseyī pitṛsapiṇḍā saivodvāhakarmaṇi parityājyā nānyeti siddham | ata evoktaṃ caturviṃśatimate |

	tṛtīyāṃ vā caturthī vā pakṣayor ubhayor api |

	vivāhayen manuḥ prāha pārāśaryo 'ṅgirā yamaḥ || iti |

ubhayor mātāpitror ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca yāni mātuladuhitṛpariṇayaniṣedhaparāṇi tāny anivṛttasvamātṛsapiṇḍabhāvābhiprāyāṇīti mantavyam | kiṃ caivaṃ saty eteṣāṃ manvādivākyānāṃ caikam eva mūlaṃ parikalpitaṃ bhavati | anyathā teṣāṃ mūlāntarakalpanāgauravaṃ syāt | tena viśeṣaviṣayataiva nyāyyā | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> yadi ca mātur asapiṇḍatayā mātulasutā pariṇeyā tarhi tathāvidhā mātṛṣvaśā tadduhitā ca kim iti na pariṇeyā | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | satyam, na brūmaḥ śāstrato na pariṇeyeti, kiṃ tu lokaviruddhatvāt | yac ca dharmyam api lokaviruddham tan nānuṣṭheyam | tad uktaṃ manunā |

	asvargyaṃ lokavidviṣṭaṃ dharmyam apy ācaren na tu | iti |

varāhamihiro 'pi |

	deśācāras tāvad ādau vicintyaḥ deśe deśe yā sthitiḥ saiva kāryā |

	lokadviṣṭaṃ paṇḍitā varjayanti daivajño 'to lokamārgeṇa yāyāt || iti |

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca yājñavalkyena,

	pañcamāt saptamād ūrdhvaṃ mātṛtaḥ pitṛtas tataḥ |

iti mātṛpakṣe pañcamād ūrdhvam udvāhavidhānāt kathaṃ mātuladuhitṛpariṇayanam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | "mātur asapiṇḍām udvahet" ity anena mātṛbandhuxv apy viśeṣeṇa vivāhaprāptau tan mā prasāṅkṣīd iti mātṛto mātṛbandhubhyaḥ pañcamād ūrdhvam udvahed ity avirodhaḥ | evaṃ pitṛbandhuṣv api draṣṭavyam | ata eva gautamaḥ: "ūrdhvaṃ saptamāt pitṛbandhubhyo bīninaś ca mātṛbandhubhyaḥ pañcamāt" iti | bīnino yo niyogād utpādayati tasmād apy ūrdhvaṃ saptamād ity arthaḥ | bāndhavā api smṛtyantare darśitāḥ |

	pituḥ pitṛṣvasuḥ putrāḥ pitṛmātṛṣavasvuḥ sutāḥ |

	pitur mātualaputrāś ca vijñeyāḥ pitṛbāndhavāḥ ||

	mātuḥ pitṛṣvasuḥ putrā mātur mātṛṣvaḥsutāḥ(?) |

	mātur mātulaputrāś ca vijñeyā mātṛbāndhavāḥ ||

yat punar vasiṣṭhenoktam,

	pañcamīṃ mātṛbandhubhyaḥ saptamīṃ pitṛbandhutaḥ |

iti tad gautamīyaikavākyatvāya pañcamīṃ saptamīṃ cātītyodvahed ity etavaṃparam, na punaḥ pañcamīsaptamyor vedovāhāvadhiparam | yad api nāradenoktam,

	pañcamāt saptamād arvāg badhubhyaḥ pitṛmātṛtaḥ |

	avivāhyā sagotrā ca samānapravarā tathā ||

iti, yad api viṣṇunā,

	pañcamāt saptamād dhīnāṃ yaḥ kanyām udvahed dvijaḥ |

	gurutalpī ca vijñeyḥ sagotrāṃ caivam udvahan ||

iti, tatrāpi pañcamīsaptamyor nābhyanujñā tatra niṣeḍhaśravaṇāt | yad āha marīciḥ |

	pañcame saptame caiva yeṣāṃ vaivāhikī kriyā |

	kriyāparā api hy ete patitāḥ sūdratāṃ gatāḥ || iti |

etena yat kaiścid uktam,

	ūrdhvaṃ saptamyā alābhe saptmīm udvahet |

iti, tad apy apāstam | yad api patiṭhīnasinoktam,

	trīn mātṛtaḥ pañca pitṛtaḥ puruṣān atītya vivāhaḥ |

iti, tad apy arvāṅ niṣedhaparam | na punaś caturthīṣaṣṭhyor vivāhābhiprāyam, viṣṇvādivacanavirodhaprasaṅgāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca "asapiṇḍā ca yā mātuḥ" ity anena yā mātur asapiṇḍā tām udvahed ity ukteḥ svamātṛpakṣe 'py aviśeṣeṇa vivāhaprāptau tan mā bhūd iti mātṛto mātṛpakṣe pañcamād ūrdhvam udvahed iti niyamaḥ kiṃ na syāt | ataḥ kathaṃ mātuladuhitṛpariṇayanam | evaṃ pitṛpakṣe 'pi draṣṭavyam | uktaṃ ca viṣṇupurāṇe |

	pañcamīṃ mātṛpakṣāc ca pitṛpakṣāc ca saptamīm |

	gṛhastha udvahet kanyāṃ nyāyena vidhinā nṛpa || iti |

pañcamīm atītyety arthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> gautamādibhir bandhuṣv eva niyamavidhānāt | atha vā mā bhūd bandhuṣv eva niyamavidhānam, tathāpy uktaprakāreṇa manvādhibhir eva mātuladuhitṛpaitṛṣavaseyīpariṇayanābhyanujānāt vyatirekeṇa pakṣadvaye 'py ayaṃ niyamaḥ kriyata ity avirodhaḥ | yad vā "pañcamāt saptamāt" iti yājñavalkīyaṃ putrikākaraṇadiviṣayam ity anusaṃdheyam | yad atra yuktaṃ tad grāhyam | yat tu saṃgrahakāreṇoktam,

	strīsantatis tathā puṃsām avivāhye ubhe mate |

	strīpuṃsos tu vivāhyā syāt pañcamāt saptamāt param ||

iti, tad apy uktaviṣayam evety anavadyam | tena smṛtitaḥ siddhaṃ mātuladuhitṛpaitṛṣvseyīpariṇayanam | kiṃ ca srutir apīmam evārthaṃ (?) śrāvayati | tathā vājasaneye śrūyate |

	tasmāt samānād eva puruṣād attā cādyaś ca jāyate |

	uta tṛtīye saṅgacchāvahai caturthe saṃgacchāvahai || iti |

asyārthaḥ: samānād ekasmāt puruṣād attā bhoktā bhāryāyā adyaś ca bhogyo bhāryālakṣaṇaś ca jāyate, jāyāpatī jāyete iti yāvat | nanv ekasmād utpannayor jāyāpatitve bhrātṛbhaginyor eva jāyāpatitvam uktaṃ syāt ity āśaṅkyāha tarhi tṛtīye puruṣa ityādi | anena dauhitraputrayor matuladuhitṛpaiṛṣvaseyīpariṇayanam uktaṃ bahavati | tayoḥ kūṭastham ārabhya tṛtīyatvāt | saṃgacchāvahai vivāhāvahā ity arthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca sragvy ūhanaparo 'yam arthavādo na svārthe pramāṇam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | satyam arthavādo na svārthe pramāṇam, kiṃ tu yatra pramāṇāntaram asti tatra tatpratipāditārthāvalambanena stutiparatvaṃ yathā "vāyur vai kṣepiṣṭā (?) devatā" iti | yatra tu nāsti pramāṇāntaraṃ yathā "tṛtīye puruṣe saṃgacchāvahai" iti tatra tadanuvādānyathānupapattyā tathāvidhavidhiparikalpanaṃ kena vāryate | ata eva, "trīṇi ha vai yajñasya udarāṇi gāyatrī bṛhaty anuṣṭub atra hy evāvapantyāvodvapanti" (?) iti atra gāyatryādiṣu pratītāvāpodvāpāny athānupapattyā tatprāpako vidhiḥ kalpyate | ata eva ca "upari hi devebhyo dhārayati" ity atrāpi samiduparidhāraṇavidhiḥ | anyathā tatrāpi na syāt | yatra punaḥ pramāṇāntaravirodhaḥ na tatra vidhikalpanaṃ yathā "ādityo yūpaḥ" iti | ata eva "prajāpatir vai svāṃ duhitaram abhyadhāyat (?)" ity atrāpi na vidhikalpanāyā atiprasaṅgaḥ, duhitṛgamane manvādibhiḥ prāyaścittavidhānāt | atha vā bhavatu arthavādānusāreṇa prajāpatiḥ svāṃ duhitaraṃ hacced iti vidhiḥ | kim āyātam itareṣām | na ca mahadbir kāryaṃ kṛtam ity anenāpi kartavyam ity atra pramāṇam asti | na hīndreṇāhalyādiparadāragamanaṃ kṛtam ity anenāpi gantavyam | ata eva śaṅkhalikhitau |

	surāṃ pibanti tridaśāḥ sā cāpeyā dvijātibhiḥ |

	haranti vittaṃ yat siddhās tava siddhir n vidyate ||

vṛddhamanur api |

	anuṣṭhitaṃ tu yad devair munibhir yad anuṣṭhitam |

	nānuṣṭheyaṃ manuṣyais tad uktaṃ karma samācaret || iti |

śrutyantare 'pi: "garbhe nu nau janitā dampatī tad eva sraṣṭā savitā viśvarūpam" iti | nau āvayoḥ garbhe jaṭhare janitā jagataḥ sraṣṭā devo dampatī jāyāpatī akarod ity arthaḥ | mantro 'pi |

	āyāhīndra pathibhir īḍitabhiḥ yajñam imaṃ no bhāgadheyaṃ juṣasya |

	tṛptāṃ juhur mātulasyevaṃ yoṣā bhāgas te paitṛsvaseyī vapām iva || iti  \
he indra pathibhir mārgair īḍitebhiḥ praśastair naḥ asmākaṃ imaṃ yajñam āyāhi āgaccha | āgatya cedam asmābhir dīyamānaṃ bhāgadheyaṃ juṣasya sevasva | ata eva yajamānās tṛptām ājyādinā saṃskṛtāṃ vapām avadānākhyāṃ tvām uddiśya juhuḥ tyaktavantaḥ | atra dṛṣṭāntadveṣam, yathā mātulasya yoṣā duhitā dauhitrasya bhāgo bhajanīyā pariṇetuṃ yogyā, yathā ca paitṛṣvaseyī pautrasya tathāyaṃ te tatra bhāgovaākhya ity mantrārthaḥ | tena śrutito 'pi siddhaṃ mātulādisutāpariṇayanam | kiṃ cācārād apy avagacchāmaḥ yathā hy ācaranti tāvad dākṣiṇātyās traividyavṛddhā vedārthanuṣṭhātāraḥ śiṣṭā eva matulādisutā pariṇayanam | uktaṃ ca tadācāraprāmāṇyaṃ manunā |

	śiṣṭācāraḥ smṛtir vedās trividhaṃ dharmalakṣaṇam | iti |

lakṣaṇaṃ pramāṇam ity arthaḥ | devalo 'pi |

	yeṣu deśeṣu ye devā yeṣu deseṣu ye dvijāḥ |

	yeṣu deśeṣu yat toyaṃ yā ca yatraiva mṛttikā ||

	yeṣu sthāneṣu yac chaucaṃ dharmācāras ca yādṛśaḥ |

	tatra tān nāvamanyeta dharmas tatraiv tādṛśaḥ ||

	yasmin deśe pure grāme taividyanagare 'pi vā |

	yo yatra vihito dharmas taṃ dharmaṃ na vicālayet || iti |

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> deśācārasyāpi pramāṇāntarāvirodhina eva prāmānyam uktaṃ vasiṣṭhena: "deśācārakuladharmā āmnāyair aviruddhāḥ pramāṇam" iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>, āmnāyo vedas tadavirodhina eva prāmāṇyam iti | na cātra vedavirodho 'sti pratyutānukūla evety uktam adhastāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> smṛtuvirodhe 'py ācāro durbala eva, "śrutismrtivihito dharmas tadalābhe śiṣṭācāraḥ pramāṇam" it vasiṣṭhasmaraṇāt | asti cātra "mātulasya sutām ūḍhvā" ityādismṛtivirodhaḥ | tenātra katham ācārasya prāmānyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>, teṣāṃ mātṛsāpiṇḍāviṣayatvena virodhasya parihṛtatvāt | atha vā mā bhūt teṣāṃ viśeṣaviṣayatvam, kiṃ tūdīcyadeśe ye mātulādiduhitṛsaṃbandhān ācaranti tadvixayāṇīty avirodhaḥ, teṣām eva doṣaśravaṇāt | tathā ca baudhāyanaḥ: "pañcadhā vipratipattir dakṣiṇataḥ anupanītena bhāryayā ca sahabhojanam, paryuṣitabhojanam ucchiṣṭabhojanaṃ pitṛṣvasṛmātuladuhitṛpariṇayanam iti | tathottarataḥ pañca ūrṇāvikrayaḥ śīdhupānam ubhayatodādbhir vyavahāraḥ āyudhīyakaṃ samudrayānam iti itara itarasmin kurvan duṣyati | itara itarasmin | tatra tatra desaprāmāṇyam eva syāt" iti | ayam arthaḥ: itaro dākṣiṇātyaḥ itarasmin uttaradeśe matulasaṃbandhādikaṃ kurvan duṣyati, na svadeśe tathetaraḥ udīcyaḥ itarasmin dakṣiṇadeśe śīdhupānādikaṃ kurvan duṣyati | na svadeśe | kutaḥ, deśaprāmāṇyāt, deśanibandhanād ācāraprāmāṇyasyety arthaḥ | ata eva devalaḥ |

	yasmin deśe ya ācāro nyāyadṛṣṭas tu kalpitaḥ |

	tasminn eva sa kartavyo deśācāraḥ smṛto bhṛgoḥ || iti |

na caivaṃ saty udīcyānāṃ svadeśe paradeśe vā mātulasaṃbandhādyaviruddham iti śaṅkanīyam | yad āha āpastambaḥ |

	yeṣāṃ paramparāprāptāḥ pūrvajair apy anuṣṭhitāḥ |

	ta eva tair na duṣyeyur ācārair netariḥ punaḥ ||

yeṣāṃ pitṛpitāmahādiparamparāprāptāḥ pūrvajaiś ca traividyavṛddhair anuṣṭhitāḥ ācārāḥ santi ta eva tair ācārair anuṣṭhīyamānair na duṣyeyuḥ, netaraiḥ | na hy udīcyānāṃ tathāvidhā ācārāḥ santi (yathā) dākṣiṇātyānām | astas tair eva svadeśe kāryāṇi nānyair iti siddham | desavyavasthayā prāmāṇyam uktaṃ vārtikakāraiḥ |

	sarveṣām evamādīnāṃ pratideśaṃ vyavasthayā|

	āpastambena saṃskrtya duṣṭāduṣṭatvam āśritam || iti |

yat tu bodhāyanena "deśaprāmāṇyam" ity evamantam uktvoktam, "mithyaitad it gautamaḥ | ubhayaṃ caiva nādriyeta siṣṭāgamavirodhadarśanāt śiṣṭasmṛtivirodhadarśanāc ca" iti, tan na pūrvoktanirākaraṇārthaṃ gautamagrahaṇāt | kiṃ tu śiṣṭasmṛtivirodhadarśanād gautamasya mātṛsapiṇḍāpariṇayanam abhipretam iti darśayitum | evaṃ ca tad uktam anyaiḥ: "syād evaṃ yady anantaram eva mithyaitad iti na brūyāt" iti, tad apy apāstam | tena śruteḥ smṛter ācārāc ca siddhaṃ mātuladuhitṛpaitṛṣvaseyīpariṇayanam iti sarvam anavadyam ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ mātuladuhitṛpariṇayanasamarthanam**

**kanyālakṣaṇāni**

"ananyapūrvikāṃ kāntām" ityādinā kānicit kanyālakṣaṇāny uktāni | adhunā lakṣaṇāntarāṇy ucyante | tatra manuḥ |

	avyaṅgāṅgīṃ saumyanāmnīṃ haṃsavāraṇagāminīm |

	tanulomakeśadaśanāṃ mṛdvaṅgīṃ udvahet striyam ||

śātātapo 'pi |

	haṃsasvanāṃ medhavarṇāṃ madhupiṅgalalocanāṃ |

	tādṛśīṃ varayet kanyāṃ gṛhasthaḥ sukham edhate ||

āpastambo 'pi: "bandhuśīlalakṣaṇasaṃpannām arogām upayaccheta" iti | lakṣaṇasaṃpannām ity anena viparītāṃ nodvahed ity āha | ata eva manuḥ |

	nodvahet kapilāṃ kanyāṃ nadhikāṅgīṃ na rogiṇīm |

	nālomikāṃ nātilomāṃ na vācāṭāṃ na piṅgalām ||

vācāṭāṃ bahubhāṣiṇīm | piṅgalāṃ piṅgalākṣīm | yamo 'pi |

	hrasvā dīrghā kṣśā sthūlā piṅgākṣī gaurapāṇḍurā |

	na pūjyā na ca sevyās tā nāśamṛtyukarāḥ striyaḥ ||

viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi |

	na smaśruvyañjanavartī na caiva puruṣākṛtim |

	na ghargharasvarāṃ kṣāmāṃ na ca kākasvanāṃ tathā ||

	nātibaddhekṣaṇāṃ tadvad vṛttākṣīṃ nodvahed budhaḥ |

	yasyāś ca roaśe jaṅghe gulphau yasyās tathonnatau ||

	gaṇḍayoḥ kūpakau yasyā hasanty āstāṃ na codvahet |

	nātirūkṣacchaviṃ pāṇḍukarajām aruṇekṣaṇām ||

	āpīnahastapādāṃ ca na kanyām udvahed budhaḥ |

	na vāmanāṃ nātidīrghāṃ nodvahet saṃhatabhruvam ||

	na cāticchidradaśanāṃ na karālamukhīṃ naraḥ || iti |

atha nāmato varjyāḥ | yathāha manuḥ |

	narkṣavṛkṣanadīnāmnīṃ nāntyaparvatanāmikām |

	na pakṣyahipreṣyanāmnīṃ na ca bhīṣaṇanāmikām ||

ṛkṣaṃ nakṣatram | antyā mlecchā | bhīṣaṇaṃ bhayānakam | āpastambo 'pi: 

	nakṣatranāma nadīnāmā vṛkṣanāmāś ca garhitāḥ |

	sarvāś ca rephalakāroṣmāntā varaṇe parivarjayet ||

yamo 'pi |

	devanāmnīṃ nadīnāmnīṃ śailagandharvanāmikām |

	ṛkṣavṛkṣalatānāmnīṃ dārārthe parivarjayet ||

tathā punar bhūr apy avivāhyā | yad āha kāśyapaḥ |

	sapta paunarbhavāḥ kanyā varjanīyāḥ kulādhamāḥ |

	vācā dattā manodattā kṛtakautukamaṅgalā ||

	udakasparśitā yā ca yā ca pāṇigṛhītakā |

	agniṃ parigatā yā ca punarbhūprasavā ca yā ||

	ity etāḥ kāśyapenoktā dahantikulam agnivat |

	prarohaty agninā dagdhaḥ pādapaḥ sucirād api ||

	na paunarbhāvādagdhaṃ kulaṃ kvāpi prarohati |

paunarbhavāḥ punarbhuva ity arthaḥ | tathā ca bodhāyanaḥ: "vāgdattā manodattā agniṃ parigatā saptamaṃ padaṃ nītā bhuktā gṛhitagarbhā prasūtā ceti saptavidhā punarbhūḥ | tāṃ gṛhītvā na prajāṃ na dharmaṃ vā vindet" iti | vāgdattā punaḥsaṃskārakarmaṇi punarbhūr bhavati | atas tāṃ gṛhītvā pariṇīya prajāṃ dharmaṃ ca na vinden na bhajed ity arthaḥ | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	kanyaivākṣatayonir yā pāṇigrahaṇadūṣitā |

	punarbhūḥ prathamā proktā punaḥsaṃskārakarmaṇi ||

pāṇigrahaṇadūṣiteti vāgdattāder upalakṣaṇartham | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	akṣatā ca kṣatā caiva punarbhūḥ saṃskrtā punaḥ | iti |

akṣatā vāgdattādikā | kṣatā tu bhuktādikā | atra yady apy uktāni bāhyalakṣaṇāni kathaṃcij jñātuṃ śakyāni, tathāpy ābhyantarāṇāṃ durvijñeyatvāt tajjñānam āśvalāyanoktavidhinā kāryam | ata evāśvalāyano 'pi durvijñeyāni lakṣaṇānīty āha |


        aṣṭau piṇḍān kṛtvā ṛtam agre prathamaṃ jajñe ṛte satyaṃ pratitiṣṭhitam | yad iyaṃ kumāryabhijātā tad idam iha pratipadyatām | yat satyaṃ tad dṛśyatām | iti piṇḍān abhimantrya kumārīṃ brūyād eṣām ekam gṛhāṇeti | kṣetrāc ced ubhayataḥ sasyād gṛhṇīyāt, annavaty asyāḥ prajā bhaviṣyatīti vidyāt | goṣṭhāt paśumatī | vedapurīṣād brahmacaryasvinīti avināśino hṛdāt sarvasaṃpannā | devanāt kitavī | yadi (?) catuṣpathād vipravrājinī | īriṇād adhnyā syāt | śmaśānāt patighnī | iti

vividhaṃ vrajatīti vipravrājinī svairiṇīty arthaḥ | evam uktalakṣaṇayoginyām aviśeṣeṇa vivāhaprāptau kvacit kulato 'pavādam āha yamaḥ |

	caturdaśa kulānīmāny avivāhyāni nirdiśet |

	anārṣeyaṃ brāhmaṇānām ṛtvijāṃ ca vivarjayet ||

	atyuccamatihrasvaṃ ca ativarṇaṃ ca varjayet |

	hīnāṅgam atiriktāṅgam āmayāvikulāni ca ||

	śvitrikuṣṭhikulādīnāṃ kuryād viparivarjanam |

	sadā kāmakulaṃ varjyaṃ lomaśānāṃ ca yat kulam ||

	apasmārikulaṃ yac ca yac ca pāṇḍukulaṃ bhavet | iti |

anārṣeyam avijñātapravaram | atyuccamatidīrghā yasmin kula tad atyuccam | atihrasvam atikubjā yasmin | atiśayito varṇo yasmin tad ativarṇam | etac ca rogikulavarjanaṃ tad romasaṅkrāntibhayāt | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	sphītād api na sañcārirogadoṣasamanvitāt | iti |

sphītāt samṛddhād ity arthaḥ | doṣāḥ pātityam | manur api |

	mahānty api samṛddhāni go'jāvidhanadhānyataḥ |

	strīsaṃbandhe daśaitāni kulāni parivarjayet ||

	hīnakriyaṃ niṣpuruṣaṃ niśchando romaśārśasam |

	śayyāmayāvyapasmāriśvitrikuṣṭhikulāni ca || iti |

hīnakriyaṃ yāgādyanuṣṭhānarahitam | niṣpuruṣaṃ puruṣaśūnyam | niśchando vedahīnam | romaśaṃ bahuromaśam | arśasaṃ vyādhiviśeṣopetam | evam itarāṇy api draṣṭavyāni | etac ca hīnakriyādivarjanaṃ tathāvidhāpatyaparihārārtham | śrūyate ca tathāvidhāpatyotpattiḥ purāṇe |

	mātulān bhajate putraḥ kanyakā bhajate pitṝn |

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	yathāśīlā bhajen mātā tathāśīlā bhavet sutā | iti |

ata eva ca manuḥ sadbhir eva saha saṃbandham ācared ity āha |

	uttamair uttamair nityaṃ saṃbandhān ācaret saha |

	ninīṣuḥ kulam utkarṣam adhamān adhamāṃs tyajet ||

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	daśapuruṣavikhyātāc chrotriyāṇāṃ mahākulāt |

mātṛtaḥ pitṛtaḥ pañca vikhyātāḥ puruṣā yasmin kula tad daśapūruṣavikhyātaṃ kulam, tasmān mahākulāt putrapaśvādisamṛddhāt kanyām udvahed ity arthaḥ | sā ca savarṇaiva grāhyā | yad āha vyāsaḥ |

	snātvā samudvahet kanyāṃ savarṇāṃ lakṣaṇānvitām | iti |

etat prathamapariṇayanaviṣayam | ata eva manuḥ |

	savarṇāgre dvijātīnāṃ praśastā dārakarmaṇi | iti |

anena savarnāpariṇayanottarakālam asavarṇāpariṇayanam aviruddham ity āha | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	tisro varṇānupūrvyeṇa dve tathaikā yathākramam |

	brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ bhāryāḥ svāḥ śūdrajanmanaḥ ||

varṇakramād brāhmaṇasya kṣatriyā vaiśyā śūdrā ceti tisro bhāryāḥ | kṣatriyasya vaiśyā śūdrā ceti dve | vaiśyasyaikā śūdreti | savarṇā punaḥ sarveṣāṃ mukhyā sthitaiva | na ca brāhmaṇasya brāhmaṇī kṣatriyā vaiśyā ceti tisro bhāryā iti vyākhyānaṃ śaṅkanīyam, tathātve "svāḥ śūdrajanmanaḥ" ity avivikṣitārthaṃ syād vaiśyasyāpi tathātvenāviśeṣāt | ataḥ pūrvoktaiva jyāyasī | ata eva manuḥ |

	śūdraiva bhāryā śūdrasya sā ca svā ca viśaḥ smṛte |

	te ca svā caiva rājñaḥ syus tāś ca svā cāgrajanmanaḥ || iti |

etat tu kāmataḥ pravṛttaviṣayam | yad āha sa eva |

	kāmatas tu pravṛttānām imāḥ syuḥ kramaśo 'varāḥ | iti |

avarā jaghanyā ity arthaḥ | anena dharmārthaṃ savarṇāpariṇayanam ity uktaṃ bhavati | ata eva viṣṇuḥ |

	dvijasya bhāryā śūdrā tu dharmārthaṃ na bhavet kvacit |

	ratyartham eva sā tasya rāgāndhasya prakīrtitā || iti |

sā dharmārthaṃ na bhaved dharmakāryeṣu nānupraviśed ity arthaḥ | ata eva manuḥ |

	daivapitryātitheyāni tatpradhānāni yasya tu |

	nāśnanti pitṛdevās taṃ na ca svargaṃ sa gacchati ||

tatpradhānāni tadāyattānīty arthaḥ | yat tu tenaivoktam,

	na brāhmaṇakṣatriyayor āpady api hi tiṣṭhatoḥ |

	kasmiṃścid api vṛttānte śūdrabhāryopadiśyate ||

iti, tad agrata eva śūdrāpariṇayanaviṣayam, "imāḥ syuḥ kramaśo 'varāḥ" iti tenaiva kramavidhānāt | uktaṃ ca yājñavalkyena" tisro varṇānupūrvyeṇa" iti | "āpady api tiṣṭhatoḥ" savarṇām alabhamānayor apīty arthaḥ | etac cānayor atyantaniṣedhārtham, na punar vaiśyasya prāptyartham | yataḥ sa evāha |

	hīnajātistriyaṃ mohād udvahanto dvijātayaḥ |

	kulāny eva nayanty āśu sasantānāni śūdratām || iti |

paiṭhīnasis tu savarṇālābhe kṣatriyādivivāham āha: "alābhe kanyāyāḥ snātakavrataṃ cared api vā kṣatriyāyāṃ putrān utpādayed vaiśyāyāṃ śūdrāyāṃ vety anye" iti | yad api ca yājñavalkyenoktam,

	yad ucyate dvijātīnāṃ śūdrād dāropasaṃgrahaḥ |

	na tan mama mataṃ yasmāt tatrātmā jāyate svayam ||

iti, tad api mānavena samānārtham | na caivaṃ sati "tatrātmā jāyate svayam" iti hetutvenānuguṇam iti vācyam, tenāpi "tisro varṇānupūrvyeṇa" it śūdrāpariṇayanasyoktatvāt | kiṃ ca hetutvānusāreṇa kadācid api śūdrāvivāhānaṅgīkāre kṣatriyādivivāho 'pi na syāt, tatrāpy ātmana evotpattiḥ | ato nāyaṃ hetuḥ kiṃ tv ayam arthavāda iti mantavyam | yat punar yamenoktam,

	brāhmaṇo vṛṣalīṃ gatvā tryahaṃ bhavati sūtakī |

	athāsyāṃ garbham ādhatte brāhmaṇyād eva hīyate ||

iti, yad api manunā,

	śūdrāṃ śayanam āropya brāhmaṇo yāty adhogatim |

	janayitvā sutaṃ tasyāṃ brāhmaṇyād eva hīyate ||

iti, tenāpi vyutkrameṇodvāhakarma gamanaṃ tasyām eva sutotpattir niṣidhyate, na punas tatra sutotpattimātram | tathātve tu,

	catustridvaiyakabhāgino (?) varṇato brāhmaṇātmajāḥ |

iti vibhāgavacanaṃ na syāt | ata eva manur api kevalaśūdrāpatyatayā doṣam āha |

	śilpena vyavahāreṇa śūdrāptyaiś ca kevalaiḥ |

	gobhir aśvaiś ca yānaiś ca kṛṣyā rājopasevayā ||

	ayājyayājanaiś caiva nāstikyena ca karmaṇām |

	kulāny āśu vinaśyanti yāni hīnāni mantrataḥ || iti |

gobhir āśvair vikrīyamāṇair ity arthaḥ | tathā matāntarāṇy api sa evāha |

	śūdrāvedī pataty atrer utathyatanayasya ca |

	śaunakasya sutotpattyā tadapatyatayā bhṛgoḥ ||

asyārthaḥ: śūdrāvedī vipraḥ patati | atra atrer utathyatanayasya gautamasya ca matam uktam | atas tayor mate śūdrāvivāho nāsti | śaunakasya na vivāhamātrāt pātityam, kiṃ tu sutotpattyā | atas tasya mate śūdrām ṛtau nopeyāt | bhṛgos tu na tatra sutotpattyāpi patanam, kiṃ tu tadapatyatayā tāny eva śūdrāyām utpannāny eva apatyāni yasyāsau tadapatyaḥ, tasya bhāvas tadapatyatā, tayety arthaḥ | atas tasya mate brāhmaṇyām aprasūtāyāṃ śūdrām ṛtau nopeyad iti | tathā vasiṣṭho 'pi śūdrāpariṇayananiṣedham āha: "śūdrām apy eke mantravarjam | tad u tathā na kuryāt | aṃhobhir dhruvaḥ kulāpakarṣaḥ pratyutāsvargyaḥ" iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ kanyālakṣaṇāni**

**atha varalakṣaṇāni**

tatra gautamaḥ: "vidyācāritrabandhuśīlasaṃpannāya dadyāt" iti | vidyā vedaḥ śrutaṃ ca | cāritram anuṣṭhānam | bandhuḥ praśastābhijanaḥ | śīlaṃ vṛttam | etaiḥ saṃpannāya kanyāṃ dadyād ity arthaḥ | āpastambo 'pi: "bandhulakṣaṇaśīlasaṃpannaḥ śrutavān aroga iti varasampat" iti | yamo 'pi |

	kulaṃ ca śīlaṃ ca vapur vayaś ca vidyāṃ ca vittaṃ ca sanāthatāṃ ca |

	etān guṇānt sapta parīkṣya deyā kanyā budhaiḥ śeṣam acintanīyam || iti |

yat tu viṣṇunoktam,

	brāhmaṇasya kulaṃ grāhyaṃ na vedā na padakramāḥ |

	kanyādāne tathā śrāddhe na vidyā tatra kāraṇam \\

iti, tat kulasya prādhānyapratipādanaparam | na punar vidyānirākaraṇārtham | ata eva āśvalāyanaḥ: "kulam agre parīkṣeta" iti | tathā puṃstvam api parīkṣaṇīyaṃ tasyety āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	yatnāt parīkṣitaḥ puṃstve yuvā dhīmān janapriyaḥ |

kātyāyano 'pi |

	apatyārthaṃ striyaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ strī kṣetraṃ bījino narāḥ |

	kṣetraṃ bījavate deyaṃ nābījī kṣetram arhati || iti |

atas tatparīkṣaṇīyam iti bhāvaḥ | nāradas tu tatparīkṣopāyam āha |

	yasyāpsu plavate bījaṃ hlādi mūtraṃ ca phenilam |

	pumān syāl lakṣaṇair etair viparītas tu ṣaṇḍakaḥ || iti |

bījaṃ vīryam | hlādi śabdavat | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	hlādiphenilamūtras tu guruśuklo vṛṣasvanaḥ |

	pumān syād anyathā ṣaṇḍo duścikitso mukhebhagaḥ ||

mukhebhagaṣ ṣaṇḍaviśeṣaḥ | śātātapo 'pi varalakṣaṇāny āha |

	varo varayitavyo 'rthī kulaśīlasamanvitaḥ |

	rūpavān paṇḍitaḥ prājño yuvā doṣavivarjitaḥ || iti |

varayitavyaḥ kanyāpitreti śeṣaḥ | doṣā api kātyāyanenoktāḥ |

	unmattaḥ patitaḥ kuṣṭhī tathā ṣaṇḍaḥ sagotrajaḥ |

	cakṣuḥśrotravihīnaś ca tathāpasmāradūṣitaḥ ||

	varadoṣaḥ smṛtā hy ete kanyādoṣāś ca kīrtitāḥ |

	dūrasthānām avidyānāṃ mokṣamārgānusāriṇām ||

	śūrāṇāṃ nirdhanānāṃ ca na deyā kanyakā budhaiḥ | iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ varalakṣaṇāni **

**atha kanyādānakālāḥ**

tatra saṃvartaḥ |

	aṣṭame tu bhaved gaurī navame nagnikā bhavet |

	daśame kanyakā proktā dvādaśe vṛṣalī smṛtā ||

vṛṣalī rajasvalā,

	bandhyā tu vṛṣaḷī jñeyā vṛṣalī ca mṛtaprajā |

	aparā vṛṣalī jñeyā kumārī yā rajasvalā ||

iti devalasmaraṇāt | etac ca prāyikābhiprāyam, na punar dvādaśa eva rajasvalā bhavatīti, kāsāṃcid arvāg api rajodarśanasaṃbhavāt | ata eva yamaḥ |

	aṣṭavarṣā bhaved gaurī navavarṣā tu rohiṇī |

	dasavarṣā bhavet kanyā ata ūrdhvaṃ rajasvalā ||

yat punar āpastambenoktam,

	aṣṭavarṣā bhaved gaurī daśavarṣā tu kanyakā |

	prāpte tu dvādaśe varṣe rajaḥ strīṇāṃ pravartate || 

iti, yad api yamenoktam,

	saṃprāpte dvādaśe varṣe rajaḥ strīṇāṃ pravartate |

iti, yad api yamena,

	saṃprāpta dvādaśe varṣe yaḥ kanyāṃ na prayacchati |

	māsi māsi rajas tasyāḥ pitā pibati śoṇitam ||

iti, tad api prāyikābhiprāyam, kāsāṃcit tatrāpi rajodarśanāsaṃbhavāt | ata eva manuḥ |

	triṃśadvarṣo vahet kanyāṃ hṛdyāṃ dvādaśavārṣikīm |

	tryaṣṭavarṣo 'ṣṭavarṣāṃ vā dharme sīdati satvaraḥ || iti |

satvaro 'lpavayā ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca yāvad rajodarśanaṃ na bhavati tāvat kanyodvāho na viruddha ity uktaṃ bhavati | ata eva yamaḥ |

	tāvad udvāhayet kanyāṃ yāvan nartumatī bhavet | iti |

gautamo 'pi: "pradānaṃ prāg ṛtor aprayacchan doṣī prāg vāsaḥpratipatter ity eke" iti | saṃvarto 'pi |

	romakāle tu saṃprāpte somo bhuṅkte tu kanyakām |

	rajaḥkāle tu gandharvo vahnis tu kucadarśane ||

	tasmād udvāhayet kanyāṃ yāvan nartumatī bhavet | iti \

vasiṣṭho 'pi |

	prayacchan nagnikāṃ kanyām ṛtukālabhayāt pitā |

	ṛtumatyāṃ hi tiṣṭhantyāṃ doṣaḥ pitaram ṛcchati || iti |

nagnikā ca purāṇe darśitā |

	yāvan na lajjayāṅgāni (?) kanyā puruṣasaṃnidhau |

	yo 'nyādīny avagūheta (?) tāvad bhavati nagnikā || iti |

saṃgrahāro 'pi |

	yāvac celaṃ na gṛhṇāti yāvat krīḍati pāṃsubhiḥ \

	yāvad doṣaṃ na jānāti tāvad bhavati nagnikā ||

amaras tu yāvad ṛtudarśanaṃ nagnikety āha: "nagnikānāgatārtavā" iti | tathā varasyāpi pariṇayanakālam āha manuḥ |

	triṃśadvarṣo vahet kanyāṃ hṛdyāṃ dvādaśavārṣikīm |

	tryaṣṭavarṣo 'ṣṭavarṣāṃ vā dharme sīdati satvaraḥ || iti |

bṛhaspatir api |

	triṃśadvarṣo daśābdāṃ tu bhāryāṃ vindeta nagnikāṃ |

	ekaviṃśativarṣo vā saptavarṣām avāpnuyāt ||

viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi |

	varṣair ekaguṇair bhāryām udvahet triguṇaḥ svayam | iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ kanyādānakālāḥ**

**atha kanyādānaphalam**

yas tūkatavidhinā kanyāṃ prayacchati tasya phalam āha manuḥ |

	nāgnihotrādibhis (?) tat syād akṣayaṃ brāhmaṇasya vā |

	yat kanyāṃ vidhivad datvā phalam āpnoti mānavaḥ ||

marīcir api |

	nāgnicin narakaṃ yāti na kanyado na tatsuta |

	visvajit saṃmito yajñaḥ kanyādānaṃ mahāphalam ||

saṃvarto 'pi |

	jyotiṣṭomātirātrāṇāṃ śataṃ śataguṇīkṛtam |

	prāpnoti kanyakāṃ datvā homamantraiś ca saṃskṛtām ||

bṛhaspatir api |

	sahasrasaṃmitā dhenur anaḍvān daśa dhenavaḥ |

	daśānaḍutsamaṃ yānaṃ daśayānasamo hayaḥ ||

	daśavājisamā kanyā bhūmidānaṃ ca tatsamam |

	kanakāśvatilā nāgā dāsīrathamahīgṛhāḥ |

	kanyā ca kapilā dhenur mahādānāni vai daśa ||

yamo 'pi |

	daśānāṃ tu sahasrāṇāṃ yajñānāṃ dhuryavāhinām |

	supātre viniyuktānāṃ kanyā vidyā ca tatsamam ||

	gaurīṃ dadan nākapṛṣṭhaṃ vaikuṇṭhaṃ rohiṇīṃ dadat |

	kanyāṃ dadad brahmalokaṃ rauravaṃ tu rajasvalām || iti |

tathā rajasvalāpariṇetur api sa eva doṣam āh |

	mātā caiva pitā caiva jyeṣṭhabhrātā tathaiva ca |

	trayas te narakaṃ yānti dṛṣṭvā kanyāṃ rajasvalām ||

	yas tāṃ vivayet kanyāṃ brāhmaṇo madamohitaḥ |

	asaṃbhāṣyo hy apāṅkteyaḥ sa vipro vṛṣalīpatiḥ ||

	vṛṣalīsaṃgṛhītā yo brāhmaṇo madamohitaḥ |

	satataṃ sūtakaṃ tasya brahmahatyā dine dine || iti |

yaḥ punas tām upabhuṅkte tasyāpi sa eva doṣam āha |

	yaḥ karoty ekarātreṇa vṛṣalīsevanaṃ dvijaḥ |

	sa bhaikxabhug japan nityaṃ tribhir varṣair vyapohati ||

	vṛṣalīgamanaṃ caiva māsam ekaṃ nirantaram |

	iha janmani śūdratvaṃ mṛtaḥ śvā caiva jāyate ||

	vṛṣalīphenapītasya niśvāsopahatasya ca |

	tasyāṃ caiva prasūtasya niṣkṛtir naiva vidyate || 

yadā tu kanyaiva rajasvalā bhavati tadā tatpitur bhrūṇahatyām āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pitur gṛhe tu yā kanyā rajaḥ paśyaty asaṃskṛtā |

	bhrūṇahatyā pitus tasyāḥ sā kanyā vṛṣalī smṛtā ||

bhrūṇahatyā garbhahatyā | sā ca pratyṛtu veditavyā | tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ |

	aprayacchan samāpnoti bhrūṇahatyām ṛtāv ṛtau |

nārado 'pi |

	yāvantaś cartavas tasyāḥ samatīyuḥ patiṃ vinā |

	tāvatyo bhrūṇahatyāḥ syus tasya yo na dadāti tām ||

yat punar manunoktam,

	kāmam ā maraṇāt tiṣṭhed gṛhe kanyartumaty api |

	na tv evaināṃ prayaccheta guṇahīnāya karhicit ||

iti, tad guṇavati saṃbhavati guṇahīnāya na dadyād ity evaṃparam, na punar guṇahīnaniṣedhārtham | ata āha bodhāyanaḥ |

	dadyād guṇavate kanyāṃ nagnikāṃ brahmacāriṇe |

	api vā guṇahīnāya noparoddhyā rajasvalā ||

yamo 'pi |

	dadyād guṇavate kanyāṃ nagnikām eva śaktitaḥ |

	na tv eva guṇahīnāya noparundhyād rajasvalām || iti |

yadā tu tām api na prayacchati tadā kanyaiva svasadṛśaṃ bhartāraṃ varayet | tad āha yamaḥ |

	kanyā tu dvādaśe varṣe yāpradattā gṛhe vaset |

	bhrūṇahatyā pitus tasyāḥ sā kanyā varayet svayam ||

	etac ca varaṇam ṛtuprabhṛti varṣatrayād ūrdhvaṃ veditavyam |

tathā ca bodhāyanaḥ |

	trīṇi varṣāṇy ṛtumatī kāṅkṣeta pitṛśāsanam |

	tataś caturthe varṣe tu vindeta sadṛśaṃ patim ||

	avidyamāne sadṛśe guṇahīnam api śrayet |

sadṛśo guṇavān | manur api |

	trīṇi varṣāṇy upāsīta kumāry artumatī satī |

	ūrdhvaṃ tu kālād etasmād vindeta sadṛśaṃ patim ||

	adīyamānā bhartāram adhigacched yadi svayam |

	nainaḥ kiṃcid avāpnoti na ca yaṃ sādhigacchati ||

yaṃ bhartāram adhigacchati so 'pi na doṣam āpnotīty arthaḥ | yat tu viṣṇunoktam,

	ṛtutrayam upāsyaiva kanyā kuryāt svayaṃvaram |

iti, tad ṛtutrayād arvāṅ niṣedhaparam | atra manuḥ |

	alaṃkāraṃ nādadīta pitryaṃ kanyā svayaṃvarā |

	mātṛkaṃ bhrātṛdattaṃ vā stenā syād yadi taṃ haret ||

yas tu vācā kanyāṃ pradāya punas tām apaharati sa rājñā daṇḍya ity āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	sakṛt pradīyate kanyā haraṃs tāṃ coradaṇḍabhāk |

manur api |

	sakṛd aṃśo nipatati sakṛt kanyā pradīyate |

	sakṛd āha dadānīti trīṇy etāni sakṛt sakṛt ||

sakṛd aṃśo nipatati sakṛd eva pitrādibhir bhāgaṃ labhata ity arthaḥ | etac cāduṣṭavarābhiprāyam | yad āha nāradaḥ |

	datvā nyāyena yaḥ kanyāṃ varāya na dadāti tām |

	aduṣṭaś ced varo rājñā sa daṇḍyas tatra coravat ||

anena doṣadarśanena vāgdattām api na pūrvasmai dadyād ity uktaṃ bhavati | ata eva gautamaḥ: "pratiśrutyāpy adharmasaṃyuktāya na dadyāt" iti | anenaivābhiprāyeṇa yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	dattām api haret kanyāṃ śreyāṃś ced vara āvrajet | iti |

yat tu manunoktam,

	etat tu na pare cakrur nāpare cāpi sādhavaḥ |

	yad anyasyābhyanujñāya punar anyasya dīyate ||

iti, tad apy aduṣṭavarābhiprāyam | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	strīpuṃsayos tu saṃbandhād varaṇaṃ prāg vidhīyate |

	varaṇād grahaṇaṃ pāṇeḥ saṃskāro hi vilakṣaṇaḥ ||

	tayor aniyataṃ proktaṃ varaṇaṃ doṣadarśanāt |

tayor varaṇapāṇigrahaṇayor madhye varaṇam eva doṣadarśanād aniyatam, na pāṇigrahaṇam | tayor vāgdānamātreṇa patitvānupapatter iti bhāvaḥ | ata eva yamaḥ |

	nodakena na vācā vā kanyāyāḥ patir ucyate |

	pāṇigrahaṇasaṃskārāt patitvaṃ saptame pade ||

anena saptamapadād arvāk pariṇetuḥ maraṇe 'pi na vidhavātvam ity uktaṃ bhavati | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	adbhir vācā ca yā dattā mriyetādau varo yadi |

	na ca mantropanītā syāt kumārī pitur eva sā ||

pitur eva na pratigrahītur ity arthaḥ | kātyāyano 'pi |

	varayitvā tu yaḥ kaścit praṇaśyet puruṣo yadā |

	raktāgamāṃś trīn atītya kanyānyaṃ varayed varam ||

raktāgamo rajodarśanam | evaṃ deśāntaragate 'pi draṣṭavyam | yad āha nāradaḥ |

	pratigṛhya tu yaḥ kanyāṃ varo deśāntaraṃ vrajet |

	trīn ṛtūn samatikramya kanyānyaṃ varayed varam ||

manus tu śulkadāne viśeṣam āha |

	kanyāyāṃ dattaśulkāyāṃ mriyeta yadi śulkadaḥ |

	devarāya pradātavyā yadi kanyānumanyate || iti |

evaṃ ca vāgdānaprabhṛtyā saptamapadād doṣadarśane maraṇādau vā kanyām anyasmai dadyāt, nordhvam ity uktaṃ bhavati | ata eva kātyāyanaḥ |

	anekebhyo hi dattāyāṃ anūḍhāyāṃ tu yatra vai |

	varāgamaś ca sarveṣāṃ labhetādivaras tu tām ||

	athāgaccheyur ūḍhāyāṃ na tāṃ pūrvavaro haret |

pūrvavaraḥ svadattaṃ śulkam eva haren na kanyām ity arthaḥ | manur api |

	na datvā kasyacit kanyāṃ punar dadyāt vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	datvā punaḥ prayacched yaḥ prāpnoti puruṣānṛtam ||

tad api tenaivoktam |

	pañca paśvanṛte hanti dasa hanti gavānṛte |

	śatam aśvānṛte hanti sahasraṃ puruṣānṛte ||

pañca bāndhavān ity arthaḥ, teṣām eva prakṛtatvāt | vasiṣṭhas tu pāṇigrahaṇād upary apy anyasmai dānam āha |

	pāṇigrahe kṛte kanyā kevalaṃ mantrasaṃskṛtā |

	sā ced akṣatayoniḥ syāt punaḥsaṃskāram arhati ||

nārado 'pi |

	udvāhitāpi yā kanyā na cet saṃprāptamaithunā |

	punaḥsaṃskāram arheta yathā kanyā tathaiva sā ||

etad api doṣadarśane veditavyam | ata eva yamaḥ|

	varaś cet kulaśīlābhyāṃ na yujyeta kathaṃcana |

	na mantraḥ kāraṇaṃ tatra na ca kanyānṛtaṃ bhavet ||

	samākṛṣya tu tāṃ kanyāṃ balād akṣatayonikāṃ |

	punar guṇavate dadyād iti śātātapo 'bravīt ||

kātyāyano 'pi |

	sa tu yady anyajātīyaḥ patitaḥ klība eva vā |

	vikarmā vā sagotro vā dāso dīrghāmayo 'pi vā ||

	ūḍhāpi deyā sānyasmai saprāvaraṇabhūṣaṇā |

manur api |

	naṣṭe mṛte pravrajite klībe ca patite patau |

	pañcasv āpatsu nārīṇāṃ patir anyo vidhīyate ||

evaṃ ca yāni saṃskārād ūrdhvam akṣatayonyāḥ punar udvāhaparāṇi tāni yugāntarābhiprāyāṇīti mantavyam | ata eva ādipurāṇe |

	ūḍhāyāḥ punar udvāhaṃ jyeṣṭhāṃśaṃ govadhaṃ tathā |

	kalau pañca na kurvīta bhrātṛjāyāṃ kamaṇḍalum ||

smṛtyantare 'pi |

	devarāt tu sutotpattiṃ gomedhaṃ ca kamaṇḍulum |

	akṣatāṃ pauruṣaṃ (?) medhaṃ kalau pañca vivarjayet ||

manus tu daoṣadarsane kanyāyā api parityāgam āha |

	vidhivat pratigṛhyāpi tyajet kanyāṃ vigarhitām |

	vyādhitāṃ vipraduṣṭāṃ vā chadmanā copapāditām ||

vividhaṃ prakarṣeṇa duṣṭāṃ vipraduṣṭām | nārado 'pi |

	nāduṣṭāṃ dūṣayet kanyāṃ nāduṣṭaṃ dūṣayed varam |

	doṣe sati na doṣaḥ syād anyonyaṃ tyajator dvayoḥ ||

etad api saptapadād arvāg veditavyam, tatraiva bhāryātvasyopapatteḥ | ata eva manuḥ |

	pāṇigrahaṇika mantrā niyataṃ dāralakṣaṇam |

	teṣāṃ niṣṭā tu vijñeyā vidvadbhiḥ saptame pade ||

yas tu kanyādoṣam anabhidhāya prayacchati sa rājñā daṇḍya ity āha nāradaḥ |

	yas tu doṣavatīṃ kanyām anākhyāya prayacchati |

	tasya kuryān nṛpo daṇḍaṃ pūrvasāhasacoditam ||

paṇaśatadvayaṃ saptatyadhikaṃpūrvasāhasam | yat tu yājñavalkyenoktam,

	anākhyāya dadad doṣaṃ daṇḍa uttamasāhasam |

iti, tad doṣabhūyastvābhiprāyam | sāśītipaṇasāhasram uttamasāhasam | yaḥ punar aduṣṭām eva parityajati so 'pi daṇḍya ity āha nāradaḥ |

	pratigṛhya tu yaḥ kanyām aduṣṭām utsṛjen naraḥ |

	vineyaḥ so 'py akāmo 'pi kanyāṃ tām eva codvahet ||

vineyo daṇḍya ity arthaḥ | daṇḍam api sa evāha |

	aduṣṭāṃ pratigṛhyātha tyajann uttamasāhasam | iti |

kanyādoṣā api tenaivoktāḥ |

	dīrghakutsitarogārtā vyaṅgā. saṃspṛṣṭamaithunā |

	dhṛṣṭānyagatabhāvā ca kanyādoṣāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ kanyādānaphalāni**

**atha kanyādātṛnirṇayaḥ**

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	pitā pitāmaho bhrātā sakulyo jananī tathā |

	kanyāpradaḥ pūrvanāśe prakṛtisthaḥ paraḥ paraḥ ||

prakṛtistha unmādādidoṣarahitaḥ | aprakṛtisthatve tu pitrādināpi kṛtam akṛtam eva | yad āha nāradaḥ |

	svatanto 'pi hi yat kāryaṃ kuryād aprakṛtiṃ gataḥ |

	tad apy akṛtam eva syād asvātantyasya hetutaḥ ||

yat punar manunoktam |

	yasmai dadyāt pitāpy enāṃ bhrātā cānumatau pituḥ |

	taṃ śuśrūṣeta jīvantaṃ saṃsthitaṃ ca na laṅghayet || iti |

tat tayoḥ pradhānyapratipādanārthaṃ na punar anyaniṣedhāya (?) | ata eva nāradaḥ |

	pitā dadyāt svayaṃ kanyāṃ bhrātā vānumatau pituḥ |

	mātāmaho mātulaś ca sakulyo bāndhavas tathā ||

	mātā tv abhāve sarveṣāṃ prakrtau yadi vartate |

	tasyām aprakṛtisthāyāṃ dadyuḥ kanyāṃ svajātayaḥ || iti |

yadā tu sarveṣām abhāvas tadā rājā dadyāt | tad āha sa eva |

	yadā tu naiva kaścit syāt kanyā rājānam āvrajet |

yadāsāv api kṣitipālanādyākulatayā na dadāti tadā kanyaiva tadanujñayā svasadṛśaṃ bhartāraṃ varayet | tad api tenaivoktam |

	anujñayā varaṃ tasya pratītya varayet svayam |

yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	gamyaṃ tv abhāve dātṝṇāṃ kanyā kurtāt svayaṃvaram |

gamyaṃ gamanārtham ity arthaḥ | tathā ca varayed ity anuvṛttau nāradaḥ |

	savarṇam anurūpaṃ ca kulaśīlabahuśrutaiḥ |

	sahadharmaṃ caret tena putrāṃś cotpādayet tataḥ || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ kanyādātṛnirṇayaḥ **

**atha vidhavāniyojanam**

tatra manuḥ |

	devarād vā sapiṇḍād vā striyā samyaṅ niyuktayā |

	prajepsitādhigantavyā santānasya parikṣaye ||

striyā śvaśurādibhir niyuktayā devarād bhartur jyeṣṭhāt kaniṣṭhād vā tadabhāve sapiṇḍād vābhilaṣitā prajā puṃstvalakṣaṇā tayotpādanīyety arthaḥ | yājñavalkyo 'pi |

	aputrām gurvanujñāto devaraḥ putrakāmyayā |

	sapiṇḍo vā sagotro vā ghṛtābhyakta ṛtāv iyāt ||

putrakāmyayā tasyā iti śeṣaḥ, anyathā niyoganiṣedhāt | tathā ca yamaḥ |

	nākāmā saṃniyojyā syāt putrakāmāṃ niyojayet | iti |

na cāputrāyāḥ svargādyabhāvena putrakāmanayā bhavitavyam iti śaṅkanīyam,

	mṛte bhartari sādhvī strī brahmacarye vyavasthitā |

	svargaṃ gacchaty aputrāpi yathā te brahmacāriṇaḥ ||

iti smaraṇāt | putro 'py eka evotpādanīyo na dvitīyaḥ | tad āha manuḥ |

	vidhavāyāṃ niyuktas tu ghṛtākto vāgyato niśi |

	ekam utpādayet putraṃ na dvitīyaṃ kathaṃcana ||

kecid ekaputro 'py aputasama eveti niyogārthāniṣpattiṃ manyamānāḥ putrāntarotpatti manyante | tad api tenaivoktam |

	dvitīyam eke prajanaṃ manyante strīṣu tadvidaḥ |

	anirvṛtaṃ niyogārthaṃ paśyanto dharmatas tayoḥ ||

atra gamanavidhim āha yamaḥ |

	ṛtau tu tasyāṃ snātāyāṃ vāgyato 'stamite niśi |

	na spṛśan nakharomāṇi gandhasparśāv avedayan ||

	eka eva ghṛtāktāṅgo durgandhāh śokadurmanāḥ |

	mukhān mukhaṃ pariharan gātrair gātrāṇy asaṃspṛśan ||

	yatātmā garbham ādadhyād garbhe datte tv apavrajet |

apavrajet punar na gacched ity arthaḥ | ata eva yājñavalkyaḥ |

	ā garbhasaṃbhavād gacchet patitas tv anyathā bhavet |

	anena vidhinā jātaḥ kṣetrajo 'sya bhavet sutaḥ ||

asya pūvapariṇetur ity arthaḥ | yat punar manunoktam,

	nānyasmin vidhavā nārī niyoktavyā dvijātibhiḥ |

	anyaasmin viniyuñjānā dharmaṃ hatuḥ sanatanam || 

iti, tad api smṛtyantare,

	na dvitīyaś ca sādhvīnāṃ kvacid bhartopadiśyate |

iti, tat kalau niṣedhaparam ity avirodhaḥ | ata eva kratuḥ |

	devarān na sutotpattir dattā kanyā na dīyate |

	purākalpaḥ sa yadvac ca vidhavāyā niyojanam || iti |

**iti smṛticandrikāyāṃ vidhavāniyojanam**

**atha vivāhabhedāḥ**

tatra manuḥ |

	aṣṭāv imān samāsena strīvivāhān nibodhata |

	brāhmo daivas tathaivārṣaḥ prājāpatyas tathāsuraḥ ||

	gāndharvo rākṣasaś caiva paiśācaś cāṣṭamo 'dhamaḥ || iti |

tatra yājñavalkyaḥ |

	brāhmo vivāha āhūya dīyate śaktyalaṃkṛtā |

yasminn uktalakṣaṇaṃ varaṃ svagṛham ānīya tasmai yathāśakty alaṃkṛtā kanyā dīyate (?) sa brāhmao vivāha ity arthaḥ | manur api |

	ācchādya cārhayitvā ca śrutaśīlavate svayam |

	āhūya dānaṃ kanyāyā brāhmo dharmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||

arhayitvā alaṃkārādibhiḥ pūjayitvety arthaḥ | asyāṃ jātas tu daśa pitrādīn daśa putrādīṃś cātmānaṃ pāpān mocayati | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "daśa pūrvān daśāparān ātmānaṃ ca brāhmīputraḥ punāti" iti | sa yadi sadvṛtta iti śeṣaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	daśa pūrvāparān vargān ātmānaṃ caikaviṃśakam |

	brāhmīputraḥ sukṛtakṛn mocayaty enasaḥ pitṝn ||

gautamo 'pi: "punanti sādhavaḥ putrāḥ" iti | daivārṣayor api lakṣaṇam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	yajñasya ṛtvije daiva ādāyārṣas tu godvayam |

yajñe prārabdhe yasminn alaṃkṛtya ṛtvija kanyā dīyate sa daivo vivāhaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	yajñe tu vitate samyag ṛtvije karma kurvate |

	alaṃkṛtya sutādānaṃ daivaṃ dharmaṃ pracakṣate ||

yatra punar godvayam ādāya kanyā dīyate sa ārṣo vivāhaḥ | godvayagrahaṇaṃ pradarśanārtham | ata eva manuḥ |

	ekaṃ gomithunaṃ dve va varād ādāya dharmataḥ |

	kanyāpradānaṃ vidhivad ārṣo dharmaḥ sa ucyate ||

mithunaṃ vṛṣabho dhenuś ca | anayoḥ phalam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	caturdaśa prathamajaḥ punāty uttarajaś ca ṣaṭ (?) |

prathamajo daivotpannaḥ saptapūrvān saptāparān punātīti | uttaraja ārṣotpannaḥ | sa punas trīṃs trīn | tathā ca manuḥ |

	daivoḍhajaḥ sutaś caiva sapta sapta parāvarān |

	ārṣoḍhajaḥ sutas trīṃs trīn ṣaṭ ṣaṭ kāyoḍhajaḥ sutaḥ ||

kāyaḥ prājāpatyaḥ | tatsvarūpam api sa evāha |

	sahobhau caratāṃ dharmam iti vācānubhāṣya tu |

	kanyāpradānam abhyarcya prājāpatyo vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ || iti |

tathāsurādicatuṣṭayam āha yājñavalkyaḥ |

	āsuro draviṇādānād gāndharvaḥ samyān mithaḥ |

	rākṣaso yuddhaharaṇāt paiśācaḥ kanyakāc chalāt ||

varād draviṇam ādāya yat pitrādibhir dānarahitaṃ kanyārpaṇaṃ sa āsuro vivāhaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	jñātaye draviṇaṃ datvā kanyayai caiva śaktitaḥ |

	kanyāpradānaṃ svācchandyād āsuro dharma ucyate ||

āpradānam ādānaṃ svīkāraḥ | svācchandyāt svecchāta ity arthaḥ | gāndharvas tu kanyāvarayor icchayānyonyasaṃyogaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	icchayānyonyasaṃyogaḥ kanyāyāś ca varasya ca |

	gāndharvaḥ sa tu vijñeyo maithunyaḥ kāmasaṃbhavaḥ ||

maithunyo maithunāya hita ity arthaḥ | rākṣasas tu yuddhena kanyāharaṇam | tathā ca manuḥ |

	hatvā chitvā ca bhitvā ca krośantīṃ rudatīṃ gṛhāt |

	prasahya kanyāharaṇaṃ rākṣaso vidhir ucyate ||

prasahya balātkāreṇety arthaḥ | paiśācaḥ punaḥ kanyakāchalād bhavati | chalanaṃ chalaḥ | chadmanā svāpādyavasthāsu kanyāharaṇaṃ paiśāca ity arthaḥ | tathā ca śaunakaḥ: "suptānāṃ pramattānāṃ vāpahāre paiśācaḥ" iti | teṣv āsurādiṣu santatidoṣān āha manuḥ |

	brāhmādiṣu vivāheṣu caturṣv evānupūrvaśaḥ |

	brahmavarcasvinaḥ (?) putrā jāyante śiṣṭasaṃmatāḥ ||

	rūpasattvaguṇopetā dhanavanto yaśasvinaḥ |

	paryāptabhogā dharmiṣṭā jīvanti ca śataṃ samāḥ ||

	itareṣu tu śiṣṭeṣu nṛśaṃsānṛtavādinaḥ |

	jāyante durvivāheṣu brahmadharmadviṣaḥ sutāḥ ||

nṛśaṃso hiṃsraḥ | brahmadviṣo vedadviṣaḥ | na cāsurādivivāheṣu saptapadātikramaṇādyabhavena patitvabhāryātvayor anupapattir iti śaṅkanīyam, tatrāpi svīkārānantaram eva saṃskāravidhānāt | tathā ca devalaḥ |

	gāndharvādivivāheṣu punar vivāhiko vidhiḥ |

	kartavyaś ca tribhir varṇaiḥ samayenāgnisākṣikaḥ ||

gṛhyapariśiṣṭe 'pi |

	gāndharvāsurapaiśācavivāhā rākṣasas ca yaḥ |

	pūrvaṃ pariśrayas teṣāṃ paścād dhomo vidhīyate ||

pariśayaḥ svīkāraḥ | ata eva vasiṣṭho 'pi na balād apahāramātreṇa bhāryātvam āha |

	balāc cet prahṛtā kanyā mantrair yadi na saṃskṛtā |

	anyasmai vidhivad deyā yathā kanyā tathaiva sā ||

atra varṇavyavasthayā vivāhaniyamam āha manuḥ |

	ṣaḍ ānupūrvyā viprasya kṣatrasya caturo 'parān |

	viṭchūdrayos tu tān eva vidyād dharmyān arākṣasān ||

brāhmādīn gāndharvāntān brāhmaṇasya dharmyān dharmād anapetān vijānīyāt | aparān āsurādīn paiśacān tān kṣatriyasya | vaiśyaśūdrayor api tān eva rākṣasavarjitān | eteṣv api praśastān āha sa eva |

	caturo brāhmaṇasyādyān praśastān kavayo viduḥ |

	rākṣasaṃ kṣatriyasyaikam āsuraṃ vaiśyaśūdrayoḥ ||

smṛtyantare 'pi |

	catvāro brāhmaṇasyāyāḥ śastā gāndharvarākṣasau |

	rājñas tathāsuro vaiśye śūdre cāntyas tu garhitaḥ ||

garhito na kasyāpi praśasta ity arthaḥ | ata eva yamaḥ |

	apakṛṣṭo vivāhānāṃ paiśācaḥ kathito 'ṣṭamaḥ | iti |

ata evānyavivāhālābha eva paiśācam āha vyāsaḥ |

	sarvopāyair asādhyā syāt sukanyā puruṣasya yā |

	cauryeṇāpi vivāhena sā vivāhyā rahaḥsthitā || iti |

kecid ārṣam api praśastaṃ necchanti, tatrāpi śulkagrahaṇāt | tathā ca manuḥ |

	ārṣe gomithunaṃ śulkaṃ kecid āhur mṛṣaiva tat |

	alpo 'pi vā mahān vāpi vikryas tāvad eva saḥ || iti |

mṛṣā mithyā | naitad dharmāya, yatas tāvanmātreṇāpy asau vikrya ity arthaḥ | devalas tu na gomithunaṃ śulkam ity āha |

	evaṃ vivāhāś catvāro dharmyāḥ śreyaḥpradāyakāḥ |

	aśulkā brāhmaṇādyarhās tato yānti dvayoḥ kulam || iti |

evaṃ ca brāhmaṇasya āsuragāndharvau praśastavivāhālābhe veditavyau | evaṃ kṣatriyāder api draṣṭavyam | yatu tu kāśyapenoktam,

	krītā dravyeṇa yā nārī na sā patny abhidhīyate |

	na sā daive na pitrye ca dāsīṃ tāṃ kaśyapo 'bravīt ||

iti, tat praśastavivāhasaṃbhavaviṣayam | yad apy atra praśastavivāhābhiprāyeṇa manunoktam,

	durvivāhaiḥ kriyālopaiḥ vedānadhyayanena ca |

	kulāny akulatāṃ yānti brāhmaṇyātikrameṇa ca ||

iti, tad api pūrvoktena samānaviṣayam | tathā śulkādāne 'pi sa eva doṣam āh |

	na kanyayāḥ pitā vidvān gṛhṇīyāc chulkam aṇv api |

	gṛhṇan śulkaṃ hi lobhena syān naro 'patyavikrayī ||

	nānuśuśruma jātv etat pūrveṣv api hi janmasu |

	śulkasaṃjñena mūlyena channaṃ duhitṛvikrayam ||

yamo 'pi |

	yo manuṣyo manuṣyasya vikrayād dhanam icchati |

	tasya mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca sa paratropajīvati ||

	kanyāvikrayiṇo mūrkhā iha kilbiṣakāriṇaḥ |

	patanti narake ghore dahatyā saptamaṃ kulam || iti |

etad ātmarthaṃ dhanagrahaṇe veditavyam | kanyārthe tu na doṣa ity āha manuḥ |

	yāsāṃ nadadate śulkaṃ jñātayo na sa vikrayaḥ |

	arhaṇaṃ tat kumārīṇām ānṛśaṃsyaṃ ca kevalam || iti |

yac chulkaṃ kanyārthaṃ tat kumārīṇāṃ kevalam arhaṇaṃ pūjanam ity arthaḥ | ānṛśaṃsyam apāpitvam | atra yajñapārśvaḥ |

	vivāhe vitate tantre homakāla upasthite |

	kanyāyā ṛtur āgacchet kathaṃ kurvanti yājñikāḥ ||

	snāpayitvā tu tāṃ kanyām arcayitvā yathāvidhi |

	yuñjāna āhutiṃ hutvā tatas tantraṃ pravartayet || iti |

**iti śrīsakalavidyāviśāradakeśavādityabhaṭṭopādhyāyasūnu-**

**yājñikavedaṇabhaṭṭopādhyāvaviracitāyām**

**smṛticandrikāyāṃ vivāhaprakaraṇam**

**samāptaḥ saṃskarakāṇḍaḥ**
